# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Optimized Three-Dimensional Photovoltaic Structures with LLM guided Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16191)
*Michael P. Brenner,Lizzie Dorfman,John C. Platt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文展示了如何将通用AI编码代理（AntiGravity）与大语言模型驱动的树搜索算法（ERA）结合，自主生成高效率三维光伏（3DPV）结构。该流程从复现已有计算结果开始，经过大规模树搜索发现潜在更优设计，但遭遇奖励黑客（reward hacking）问题。通过编码代理迭代修补物理引擎、添加约束消除该问题后，ERA发现了一系列在固定集热面积、优化天顶角追踪和避免自遮挡方面性能更优的设计方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索AI编码系统能否用于生成新颖的科学假说（novel scientific hypotheses），具体目标是自主设计出能够克服中纬度地区平板太阳能电池板能量损失的高效三维光伏（3DPV）结构。

Method: 将通用AI编码代理（Google的AntiGravity）与大语言模型驱动的树搜索算法ERA（Empirical Research Assistance）相结合。工作流程分三步：先由AntiGravity复现已有三维光伏计算结果；再以此为基础进行大规模树搜索，以日产量（diurnal yield）为评分指标寻找更优方案；最后针对树搜索中出现的奖励黑客（reward hacking）问题，由编码代理迭代修补物理引擎（physics engine），添加约束条件以消除非物理的设计特征。

Result: 初始树搜索产生了名义上更高效的方案，但这些方案源于奖励黑客，表现为非物理设计特征，例如结构上悬空的断开层级（structurally levitating disconnected tiers）以及对光学求解器离散化（discretizations）的利用。在消除奖励黑客后，ERA发现了一系列受不同约束且性能提升的设计，包括具有不同固定集热面积的最优设计、优化天顶角追踪（zenith tracking）以及避免自遮挡（self shadowing）的设计。

Conclusion: 将编码代理与树搜索（ERA）相结合，为科学发现提供了一个强大的通用平台，尤其适用于那些解可以通过评分函数（score function）进行经验性评估的问题。

Abstract: We present a case study for how AI coding systems can be used to generate novel scientific hypotheses. We combine a generic coding agent (Google's AntiGravity) with an LLM-driven tree search algorithm (Empirical Research Assistance / ERA) to autonomously generate high-efficiency three-dimensional photovoltaic (3DPV) structures that overcome losses limiting flat solar panels at mid-latitudes. These structures operate by presenting favorable angles to the sun throughout the day, and for illustrative purposes we focus on optimizing performance for a single solar day. Our workflow begins by using AntiGravity to reproduce calculations \cite{bernardi2012solar} showing that 3DPV can have energy densities much higher than stationary flat PV panels. We use these initial designs as the starting point for large scale tree search, where we seek improved solutions and score them for their diurnal yield. The initial tree search leads to nominally more efficient solutions, yet they are caused by algorithmic reward hacking, arising from non-physical design features such as structurally levitating disconnected tiers and exploitations of the discretizations in the optics solver. To counteract this, we develop a workflow where the coding agent iteratively patches the physics engine with constraints to eliminate reward hacking. With reward-hacking eliminated, ERA discovers a series of designs with various constraints and improved performance, including optimal designs with different fixed collector areas, optimizing zenith tracking and avoiding self shadowing.
  Combining coding agents with tree search (ERA) provides a powerful platform for scientific discovery, for problems whose solutions can be empirically evaluated with a score function.

</details>


<div id='hep-ph'></div>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Hierarchies from Higher Flavor Spin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15267)
*Admir Greljo,Alessandro Valenti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个通过高维表示下的完全无序（anarchic）spurion产生汤川层级结构（Yukawa hierarchies）的理论框架，并研究了重整化标量势是否能够动态生成相关spurion，预言了味改变中性流与随机引力波背景等可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）存在显著的层级结构（hierarchy），其起源是味物理学（flavor physics）的核心难题。现有机制往往引入额外的对称性或调参，本文旨在探索能否仅通过味对称群（flavor symmetry group）的高维表示中的无序spurion自然产生汤川层级。

Method: 框架基于味对称群SU(2)^{n_2}×SU(3)^{n_3}，利用高维表示下的完全无序spurion通过复合二重态（composite doublets）与三重态（triplets）的连续外积（successive outer products）逐步提升汤川矩阵的秩（rank）。具体构建了完整的理论构造并给出显式模型，进而分析了SU(2)高维表示的重整化标量势能否动态产生非零复合spurion。

Result: 该框架预言了味改变中性流（flavor-changing neutral currents, FCNC）中的独特模式，以及可能可观测的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的机制表明，完全无序的高维表示spurion能够自然产生汤川层级，且重整化标量势有可能动态实现该结构，为味物理的起源提供了新的理论路径，并产生了可被实验检验的唯象预言。

Abstract: We develop a framework in which Yukawa hierarchies arise from powers of fully anarchic spurions transforming in higher representations of the flavor symmetry group $SU(2)^{n_2}\times SU(3)^{n_3}$. The core mechanism is the progressive lifting of Yukawa ranks through successive outer products of composite doublets and triplets. We formulate the general construction in detail and build explicit models realizing it. We then investigate whether renormalizable scalar potentials for higher $SU(2)$ representations can dynamically generate anarchic spurions with non-vanishing composites. The framework predicts distinctive patterns in flavor-changing neutral currents and potentially observable stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds.

</details>


### [3] [Sivers Tomography from Charge and Angle Only](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15280)
*Haotian Cao,Xiaohui Liu,Frank Petriello*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种利用单点电荷关联子（OPCC）探测Sivers效应的新方法，仅依赖带电径迹的符号与方向，无需量热或粒子鉴别信息，并在微扰QCD框架下实现N³LL精度求和，为未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）上的自旋物理提供了干净的理论方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探测Sivers效应的方法通常依赖非微扰碎裂函数（fragmentation functions）或径迹函数（track functions），且需要量热或粒子鉴别信息，导致理论复杂性高、实验难度大。本文旨在提出一种更简洁、理论上干净的观测手段。

Method: 定义单点电荷关联子（one-point charge-correlator, OPCC），通过末态带电粒子的电荷符号和方向测量电荷流与质子横向自旋之间的方位角关联。在小横向分离b≪Λ_QCD⁻¹区域，利用电荷守恒实现因子化（factorization），将Sivers分布与微扰可计算的荷电权重喷注函数（charge-weighted jet function）分离，避免非微扰碎裂函数。

Result: 证明OPCC观测量是红外与共线（IRC）安全的；在固定阶QCD水平验证了因子化方案；给出非极化分布N³LL精度与Sivers不对称性N²LL精度的重求和（resummation）预言。

Conclusion: OPCC建立了一种仅利用电荷与角度信息的自旋测量新范式，为未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）提供理论上干净、实验上简单的Sivers效应探针。

Abstract: We propose a one-point charge-correlator (OPCC) probe of the Sivers effect in back-to-back deep-inelastic scattering. This measurement uses only the signs and directions of charged tracks, with no calorimetric or particle-identification information required. The observable weights the final state by its electric charge and measures the azimuthal correlation between the charge flow and the transverse spin of the proton. This probe is shown to be IRC finite and admits a factorization involving the usual Sivers distribution and a perturbatively calculable charge-weighted jet function for small transverse seperation $b\ll Λ_{\rm QCD}^{-1}$, with no reliance on non-perturbative fragmentation functions or track functions due to charge conservation. We validate the factorization against the full fixed-order QCD and present resummed predictions at N\(^3\)LL accuracy for the unpolarized distribution and N\(^2\)LL for the Sivers asymmetry. The OPCC provides a theoretically clean and simple experimental measurement, and establishes a charge-and-angle measurement paradigm for spin physics at a future Electron-Ion Collider.

</details>


### [4] [Predicting Three Generations of Fermions: Discovery Prospects of the Bilepton Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15286)
*Andreas Crivellin,Paul H. Frampton,Ahmed Hammad*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究双电荷双轻子对（doubly-charged bilepton）的产生机制及其在HL-LHC（高亮度大型强子对撞机）上的发现潜力，通过直接双轻子对产生和经由重夸克衰变中介的产生两条互补通道，确定其质量参数空间的可探测范围，发现HL-LHC可在m_D≤2.5 TeV（几乎不依赖m_Y）或m_Y≤2 TeV的条件下实现5σ发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估双电荷双轻子对在HL-LHC高积分亮度下的发现潜力，弥补Run-2数据只能覆盖较低质量参数空间的局限。

Method: 考虑两条互补的产生通道：(i)直接双轻子对产生（direct bilepton pair production）和(ii)经由重夸克衰变中介的双轻子产生（bilepton production mediated through heavy-quark decays），后者在重夸克质量m_D主导下可显著增强截面并产生区别于背景的LHC信号。

Result: 直接产生通道主要对双轻子质量m_Y敏感，而重夸克中介通道主要依赖m_D。Run-2数据仅在m_D≤1 TeV时可发现信号；HL-LHC可在m_D≤2.5 TeV（几乎独立于m_Y）或m_Y≤2 TeV（即使D夸克较重）的条件下实现5σ发现。

Conclusion: 两通道互补地覆盖参数空间，结合四轻子末态的本质近似零背景（background-free）特性，HL-LHC较Run-2显著扩展了双电荷双轻子的探测质量上限。

Abstract: We study the production of pairs of doubly-charged bileptons and assess their discovery potential in light of the integrated luminosities available at the High-Luminosity LHC. The production rates are governed primarily by the bilepton mass, $(m_Y)$, and the mass of the exotic heavy quarks, $(m_D)$. We consider two complementary production channels: (i) direct bilepton pair production and (ii) bilepton production mediated through heavy-quark decays. Notably, the latter typically yields significantly enhanced cross sections and gives rise to distinctive LHC signatures, even when the bileptons are produced off-shell. The two mechanisms therefore probe complementary regions of parameter space, with direct production being predominantly sensitive to $m_Y$, while the heavy-quark-mediated channel depends mainly on $m_D$. Owing to the essentially background-free signature of four energetic leptons at the LHC, we show that Run-2 data allow a discovery only for $m_D \lesssim 1\,\mathrm{TeV}$, whereas the HL-LHC can achieve a $5σ$ discovery up to $m_D \lesssim 2.5\,\mathrm{TeV}$ (nearly independently of $m_Y$) and/or for $m_Y \lesssim 2\,\mathrm{TeV}$ (even if $D$ is heavy).

</details>


### [5] [Numerical Study of MRW-Type Unintegrated Double Parton Distribution Functions from Non-Factorized DPDFs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15853)
*R. Kord Valeshabadi,S. Rezaie,K. Azizi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对双部分子散射（double parton scattering）中从非因子化共线双部分子分布函数（DPDF）构建的未积分双部分子分布函数进行了数值研究，分析了多种MRW-inspired横向动量生成方案（包括DMKMRW、DVO-MRW及匹配版本）的归一化、横向动量依赖、味依赖及纵向关联敏感性，发现非因子化效应表现出强烈的道依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双部分子散射（double parton scattering）是探测强子内部多部分子关联（multi parton correlations）的灵敏探针，但非因子化双部分子分布函数（DPDF）的横向动量依赖（transverse momentum dependence）构造尚需系统研究。

Method: 使用GS09 DPDF作为输入，通过数值双DGLAP演化框架（numerical double DGLAP evolution framework）将其演化至不等标度，并通过动量求和规则（momentum sum rule）验证框架有效性；在此基础上，研究了三种MRW-inspired横向动量生成方案：双修正KMRW方法（DMKMRW）、双虚度有序MRW模型（DVO-MRW）及其归一化匹配版本。

Result: DMKMRW模型天然保持归一化，DVO-MRW模型存在显著归一化偏差，匹配版本可消除该偏差；非因子化效应强烈依赖于道（channel）：DMKMRW中主要通过纵向DPDF关联体现，虚度有序模型中则同时改变横向动量形状；最大偏差出现在双部分子运动学边界附近及受价数（valence-number）和夸克-反夸克关联影响的道中。

Conclusion: 所提出的MRW-inspired方案可直接应用于完整共线DPDF（包括非齐次分量），避免了传统LO-MRW构造中分段处理的复杂性，为双部分子散射的唯象研究提供了有效的理论工具。

Abstract: Double parton scattering provides a sensitive probe of multi parton correlations inside hadrons. In this work we present a numerical study of unintegrated double parton distribution functions constructed from non-factorized collinear DPDFs. As input we use the GS09 DPDFs and evolve them to unequal scales with a numerical double DGLAP evolution framework, which is validated through the corresponding momentum sum rule.
  We investigate MRW-inspired prescriptions for generating transverse momentum dependence in the double parton case. In particular, we study the double modified KMRW approach (DMKMRW), the double virtuality ordered MRW (DVO-MRW) model, and a normalization-matched version of the latter. These prescriptions can be applied directly to the full collinear DPDF, including its non-homogeneous component, and avoid the piecewise treatment required in the conventional LO-MRW construction.
  We analyze the normalization, transverse momentum dependence, flavor dependence, and sensitivity to longitudinal DPDF correlations of the resulting distributions. The DMKMRW model is normalization preserving by construction, while the DVO-MRW model shows nontrivial normalization deviations that are removed in the matched version. Non-factorized effects are strongly channel dependent: in DMKMRW they enter mainly through longitudinal DPDF correlations, whereas in the virtuality ordered models they also modify the transverse momentum shape. The largest deviations occur near the double parton kinematic boundary and in channels affected by valence-number and quark-antiquark correlations.

</details>


### [6] [Inclusive charm and bottom quark pair production cross sections at hadron colliders at next-to-next-to-leading-order accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16019)
*David d'Enterria,Felix Hekhorn,Ilkka Helenius,Van Dung Le,Hannu Paukkunen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文系统收集了质子-质子、质子-反质子和质子-核碰撞中粲夸克对（c\bar{c}）和底夸克对（b\bar{b}）产生的遍举截面数据，覆盖质心能量约10 GeV至400 TeV。利用新的固定阶开源代码MaunaKea，在次次领头阶（NNLO）精度下进行计算并与数据对比，发现NNLO截面相比次领头阶（NLO）增强最多达两倍，理论标度不确定性也相应减半，从而在整个能量范围内与实验数据保持一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重味夸克对产生截面是检验量子色动力学（QCD）微扰论计算的重要探针，且现有数据覆盖能量范围极广，但此前缺乏系统性的次次领头阶（NNLO）精确对比。该研究旨在通过新的MaunaKea开源代码对不同质子碰撞体系中的粲和底夸克对产生数据统一进行NNLO分析，以评估高阶修正的影响并探索对部分子分布函数（PDF）和底夸克极质量（pole mass）的约束能力。

Method: 研究收集了质心能量约10 GeV至14 TeV范围内所有已有的实验数据，使用新开发的固定阶开源代码MaunaKea在次次领头阶（NNLO）精度下进行计算，并采用不同组部分子分布函数（PDF）进行对比。同时还将NNLO结果与SACOT-m_T通用质量可变味数方案（general-mass variable-flavour-number scheme）下的NLO预测进行了比较。

Result: 与次领头阶（NLO）预言相比，NNLO截面最多增强约两倍，而理论标度不确定性相应减半，使得计算结果在整个碰撞能量范围内均与实验数据吻合。尽管理论和实验不确定性仍然较大，多TeV能量下的c\bar{c}截面可为全局PDF分析中极低x区域的胶子密度提供额外约束；在底夸克扇区，低能量（约10–100 GeV）下的更精确截面测量有助于约束底夸克极质量（pole mass）。

Conclusion: NNLO高阶修正显著改善了重味夸克对产生截面的理论预言精度，弥补了此前NLO计算与实验数据之间的差距。粲夸克对产生的高能数据有望为胶子PDF提供新的约束，而底夸克对的低能精确测量则有助于更准确地确定底夸克极质量。

Abstract: The inclusive cross sections for charm ($\mathrm{c}\overline{\mathrm{c}}$) and bottom ($\mathrm{b}\overline{\mathrm{b}}$) quark-antiquark pair production in proton-proton, proton-antiproton, and proton-nucleus collisions are studied over a wide range of center-of-mass energies, $\sqrt{s}\approx 10$ GeV--400 TeV. All existing data over $\sqrt{s}\approx 10$ GeV--14 TeV are collected and compared to calculations at next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) accuracy using the new fixed-order MaunaKea open-source code for varying sets of parton distribution functions (PDFs). Relative to next-to-leading-order (NLO) predictions, the NNLO cross sections are enhanced by up to a factor of two, with the associated theoretical scale uncertainties reduced by the same amount, leading to agreement with experimental data over the full range of collision energies. The NNLO results are also compared with NLO predictions obtained within the SACOT-$m_{_\mathrm{T}}$ general-mass variable-flavour-number scheme. Despite still sizable theoretical and experimental uncertainties, $\mathrm{c}\overline{\mathrm{c}}$ cross section at multi-TeV energies can provide extra constraints on the gluon density at very small-$x$ in global PDF analyses. In the bottom sector, more precise cross section measurements at low energies, $\sqrt{s}\approx 10$--100 GeV, can help constraint the bottom-quark pole mass.

</details>


### [7] [Interactions of exotic neutralino dark matter with nucleons in $U(1)$ extensions of the MSSM originating from $E_6$ GUTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15316)
*M. G. Belyakova,R. B. Nevzorov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于E₆群 inspired 的U(1)扩展超对称标准模型（E₆ inspired U(1) extensions of MSSM）中，最轻的奇异中性微子（lightest exotic neutralino）作为冷暗物质（cold dark matter）与核子（nucleons）的相互作用，并结合当前直接探测实验（direct detection experiments）的约束分析了其耦合参数的限制。结果可推广至其他带有额外U(1)规范对称性的E₆型超对称模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保反常消除（anomaly cancellation）的E₆启发的U(1)扩展超对称标准模型（MSSM）引入了额外的奇异物质（exotic matter）。其中，最轻的奇异中性微子可能是稳定的，贡献于冷暗物质（cold dark matter）密度，因此需要研究其与核子的相互作用及当前实验约束。

Method: 以带有额外U(1)ₙ规范对称性的MSSM特定扩展模型（SE₆SSM）为例，考察最轻奇异中性微子与核子（nucleons）的相互作用，并结合当前直接探测实验（direct detection experiments）的现有实验界限（experimental bounds）分析其耦合约束。

Result: 给出了该奇异中性微子态耦合参数受当前直接探测实验界限约束的具体限制条件。

Conclusion: 所得结果可推广至其他带有额外U(1)规范对称性的E₆启发超对称模型（E₆ inspired SUSY models）。

Abstract: To ensure anomaly cancellation the $E_6$ inspired $U(1)$ extensions of the minimal supersymmetric (SUSY) standard model (MSSM) involve extra exotic matter. The lightest exotic neutralino in these models can be stable contributing to the cold dark matter density. We consider the interactions of such neutralino with nucleons within a specific extension of the MSSM with an additional $U(1)_N$ gauge symmetry (SE$_6$SSM). The constraints on the couplings of this state, which are set by the present experimental bounds caused by the direct detection experiments, are examined. The obtained results can be generalised to other $E_6$ inspired SUSY models with extra $U(1)$ gauge symmetry.

</details>


### [8] [Impact of spectator fields and non-minimal couplings in spontaneous baryogenesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16212)
*Mattia Dubbini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了自发重子生成（spontaneous baryogenesis）模型在两种扩展背景下的表现：一是引入引力与暴胀子（inflaton）的非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling），二是加入与暴胀子存在双二次耦合（biquadratic coupling）且与引力非最小耦合的复标量旁观场（complex scalar spectator field）。两种扩展均增强了背景模型，但仅前者能产生与宇宙学观测一致的净重子不对称性（baryon asymmetry），后者预测的重子-熵比（baryon-to-entropy ratio）仍小于实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在自发重子生成的标准框架之外，通过引入引力与暴胀子的非最小耦合以及额外复标量场，能否更有效地解释观测到的宇宙重子不对称性（baryon asymmetry）。

Method: 在暴胀子-引力非最小耦合模型中，通过增大暴胀子的有效质量平方（effective mass squared），使其在再加热（reheating）期间更倾向于通过重子数不守恒过程（baryon-number violating processes）衰变为费米子-反费米子对。同时，在复标量旁观场模型中，考虑其与暴胀子的双二次耦合以及与引力的非最小相互作用。

Result: 引入引力-暴胀子非最小耦合后，计算得到的整体重子不对称性与宇宙学观测一致。加入复标量旁观场虽能显著增强背景模型，但预测的重子-熵比仍低于实验数据。

Conclusion: 引力与暴胀子的非最小耦合是提升自发重子生成模型有效性的可行途径，而仅添加复标量旁观场不足以完全解释观测到的重子不对称性。

Abstract: We investigate the model of spontaneous baryogenesis, considering two extensions to the background paradigm. Firstly, we introduce a non-minimal coupling between gravity and the inflaton, increasing the effective mass squared of the latter. In this way, the inflaton decays more likely into fermion-antifermion pairs during reheating, through baryon-number violating processes. Accordingly, we obtain an overall baryon asymmetry consistent with cosmological observations. Then, we consider a complex scalar spectator field interacting with the inflaton through a biquadratic coupling and non-minimally with gravity, and analyze the impact in terms of baryon asymmetry production. In this scenario too, the background model results significantly enhanced, but the predicted baryon-to-entropy ratio remains smaller than the experimental data.

### [9] [Irreducible Graviton Floor from Reheating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16201)
*James M. Cline,Yong Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，暴胀子衰变过程中通过轫致辐射（bremsstrahlung）不可避免发射的引力子，在考虑宇宙学演化后形成不可约的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background）。基于温伯格软引力子定理（Weinberg's soft-graviton theorem），谱的红外分支由Ω_GW ∝ f固定，与暴胀子衰变的微观算符无关，信号在GHz以上频段可达Ω_GW h² ~ 10⁻¹⁷，构成微扰再加热（perturbative reheating）的引力子本底。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀子衰变在再加热（reheating）过程中会通过轫致辐射不可避免地产生引力子，这部分引力子发射带来的随机引力波背景尚未被系统量化，且其能否作为不可约的最低本底需要理论确认。

Method: 应用温伯格软引力子定理（Weinberg's soft-graviton theorem）固定软发射振幅，结合宇宙学演化计算引力波谱；针对暴胀子n体衰变（n-body decays）完成相空间积分，推导谱的最大值相对于n=2情形的标度关系。

Result: 软引力子发射的谱在红外分支满足Ω_GW ∝ f，归一化由硬暴胀子衰变率（hard inflaton decay rate）和相空间因子控制；n体衰变下谱的最大值按2/n标度；信号峰值在GHz以上频段可达Ω_GW h² ~ 10⁻¹⁷。

Conclusion: 该信号构成微扰再加热的引力子本底（graviton floor）：任何超过此本底的信号要么需要超越微扰轫致辐射的其他过程，要么需要超越传统单场慢滚（single-field slow roll）的暴胀图景。

Abstract: Inflaton decay inevitably emits gravitons through bremsstrahlung during reheating. We show that the soft part of this emission amplitude, fixed by Weinberg's soft-graviton theorem, becomes an irreducible stochastic gravitational-wave (GW) background after accounting for cosmological evolution. The theorem fixes the infrared branch of the spectrum, $Ω_{\rm GW}\propto f$, independently of the microscopic operator responsible for inflaton decay, while the normalization is controlled by the hard inflaton decay rate and by a phase-space factor. We carry this out for inflaton $n$-body decays, including the phase-space integrals, finding that the maximum of the spectrum scales as $2/n$ relative to the $n=2$ case. The signal can reach $Ω_{\rm GW}h^2\sim \mathcal O(10^{-17})$ at frequencies above the GHz scale. This predicts a stochastic graviton floor from perturbative reheating: a larger signal would require either other processes beyond perturbative bremsstrahlung or inflationary scenarios beyond conventional single-field slow roll.

</details>

### [10] [Peculiar-velocity distribution functions and 21-cm fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15287)
*Ryan Yuran Zhang,Marc Kamionkowski*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文纠正了先前工作中关于重子-暗物质相对速度平行与垂直分量相关性的简化假设，推导了两个空间点处本动速度平方的完整联合概率分布（joint PDF），并评估了该修正对宇宙学21厘米背景（cosmological 21-cm background）预测的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作在计算恒星形成率密度（SFRD）的空间关联时，忽略了两点间速度平行和垂直分量相关性的差异，这一简化假设可能导致对宇宙学21厘米背景涨落的预测产生误差。

Method: 推导了两个不同空间点处本动速度（peculiar velocity）平方的完整联合概率分布（joint PDF），从而精确计算重子-暗物质相对速度的平行与垂直分量相关性的差异。

Result: 忽略该细致差异所导致的21厘米涨落预测误差通常小于百分之几；但在某些波数（wavenumber）$k$和红移（redshift）$z$取值下，若总信号的不同贡献之间出现抵消，误差可能更大。修正后的表达式易于实现，仅使代码运行时间增加百分之几。

Conclusion: 该修正对预测精度具有统计上显著的改进，且计算成本极低，因此值得在未来的21厘米宇宙学模拟和分析中采用正确的表达式。

Abstract: Predictions for observables involving the cosmological 21-cm background require calculations of spatial correlations of star formation rate densities (SFRDs) which have a nonlinear dependence on the baryon-dark matter relative velocity. Prior work derived these SFRD correlations with a simplifying assumption that neglected the difference between the correlations of the components of the velocity parallel and perpendicular to the separation between the two points being correlated. Here we calculate the full joint PDF of the squares of the peculiar velocity at two different points. The error that arises in predictions for 21-cm fluctuations if this subtlety is overlooked is generally less than a few percent, but it can be larger for some values of wavenumber $k$ and redshift $z$ if there are cancellations between different contributions to the total signal. The correct expression is easily implemented and increases the run time of the code by only a few percent.

</details>


### [11] [Constraints on primordial black holes from the first part of LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA fourth observing run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15749)
*M. Andrés-Carcasona,A. J. Iovino,E. Vallejo-Pagès,V. Vaskonen,H. Veermäe,M. Martínez,Ll. M. Mir*

TL;DR: 利用原初黑洞双星（PBH binaries）的最先进模型，从LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4a数据推导出0.6–100 M⊙范围内对原初黑洞（PBH）丰度的最强约束，并展示了10⁻⁴–10⁴ M⊙范围内的灵敏度；联合天体物理黑洞拟合未发现PBH贡献的显著证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用最先进的原初黑洞双星（PBH binaries）建模方法，分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4a数据；约束来源包括可分辨的PBH并合事件（resolvable PBH mergers）及其关联的引力波背景（gravitational wave background）；进行PBH与天体物理黑洞（astrophysical black holes）的联合拟合（joint fit）。

Result: 在0.6–100 M⊙质量范围内得到了对PBH丰度的最强约束，并在10⁻⁴–10⁴ M⊙范围内展示了灵敏度；约束主要来自可分辨的PBH并合事件，引力波背景提供互补但较弱的限制；允许PBH解释部分已编录事件会略微放松约束；联合拟合未发现PBH贡献的显著证据。

Conclusion: 当前LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4a数据对0.6–100 M⊙范围内的PBH丰度施加了最强约束，但不存在PBH贡献的显著统计证据，PBH不能有效解释已观测到的引力波事件子集。

Abstract: We analyze PBH populations using state-of-the-art modeling of PBH binaries, deriving the strongest bounds on PBH abundance in the $0.6-100 M_\odot$ range from LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4a data and demonstrating sensitivity in the $10^{-4}-10^4 M_\odot$ range. The constraints are dominated by resolvable PBH mergers, while the associated gravitational wave background provides complementary but weaker limits. Allowing PBHs to account for a subset of the cataloged events slightly relaxes these bounds. However, a joint fit with astrophysical black holes shows no compelling evidence for a PBH contribution.

### [12] [Study of dark interactions through strong gravitational lenses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16155)
*F. Villalobos,J. Magana,T. Verdugo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）数据，分析了三种符号可变相互作用模型（sign-changeable interaction models），其中耦合项 $Q$ 依赖于减速参数 $q$ 并与不同能量密度（暗物质、暗能量、总能量密度）成正比。结果表明所有模型均给出负的相互作用强度 $\beta$，且 $\beta$ 绝对值显著大于先前基于 Ia 型超新星、CMB 和 BAO 的报告。强透镜约束显示的宇宙加速转变红移（$z_t \sim 1.8-2.1$）高于 $\Lambda$CDM 模型预测，表明强引力透镜数据可作为检验相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy）场景的独立且具有竞争力的宇宙学探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙暗组分（暗物质与暗能量）之间的可能相互作用是标准 $\Lambda$CDM 宇宙学模型（cosmological model）的一个有吸引力的替代方案。当前研究旨在利用强引力透镜数据，探索此类交互作用模型的新约束。

Method: 本研究分析三种符号可变相互作用模型（sign-changeable interaction models），其耦合项 $Q$ 明确依赖于减速参数（deceleration parameter）$q$，并分别正比于暗物质能量密度、暗能量能量密度和总能量密度。为约束模型，作者合并了两个互补尺度的强引力透镜数据：早期型星系（early-type galaxies）样本作为透镜，以及星系团 Abell 1689。

Result: 所有模型均得到负的相互作用强度（interaction strength）$\beta$，表明存在暗相互作用（dark interaction）场景。本工作得到的 $\beta$ 绝对值显著大于先前使用 Ia 型超新星（Type Ia supernovae）、CMB 和 BAO 的报告。强透镜约束显示宇宙加速转变（transition to cosmic acceleration）发生在比 $\Lambda$CDM 模型预测更早的红移处（$z_t \sim 1.8-2.1$），但在重建的置信区域内与宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometer）测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，强引力透镜数据能够作为一种独立且具有竞争力的宇宙学探针（cosmological probe），用于检验相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy）场景。透镜可观测量对膨胀历史的敏感性使其能够获取超出标准宇宙学探针的关于暗区动力学（dark-sector dynamics）的互补信息。

Abstract: The possible interaction between the dark components of the Universe (dark matter and dark energy) stands as an attractive alternative to the standard $Λ$CDM cosmological model. In this work, we present a novel analysis of three sign-changeable interaction models whose coupling term $Q$ depends explicitly on the deceleration parameter $q$ and is proportional to different energy densities: dark matter, dark energy, and total energy density. To constrain these models, we combine strong gravitational lensing data on two complementary scales: a sample of early-type galaxies acting as lenses and the galaxy cluster Abell 1689.
  Our results show that the interaction strength $β$ depends on the choice of the coupling term $Q$, with all models yielding negative values of $β$, indicative of a dark interaction scenario. The $β$ values obtained in this work are significantly larger in magnitude than those previously reported using Type Ia supernovae, CMB, and BAO. The strong-lensing constraints indicate a transition to cosmic acceleration at earlier redshifts ($z_t \sim 1.8-2.1$) than that predicted by the $Λ$CDM model, while remaining consistent with cosmic chronometer measurements within the reconstructed confidence regions. Therefore, our study shows that strong gravitational lensing data provide an independent and competitive cosmological probe capable of testing interacting dark energy scenarios. The sensitivity of lensing observables to the expansion history enables access to complementary information about dark-sector dynamics beyond standard cosmological probes.

</details>

### [13] [Reweighting free energy profiles between universal machine learning interatomic potentials for fast consensus building](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15630)
*Sauradeep Majumdar,Miguel Steiner,Johannes C. B. Dietschreit,Swagata Roy,Daniel Willimetz,Lukaš Grajciar,Rafael Gómez-Bombarelli*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种系统化、可扩展的重加权（reweighting）框架，用于仅通过一次源机器学习原子间势（MLIP）采样，高效重建多个目标MLIP的平均力势（PMF），并成功应用于锂离子在纳米限域电解质中的传输体系，实现了接近密度泛函理论（DFT）精度的热力学性质预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）精度的平均力势（potential of mean force, PMF）计算成本极高。通用机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）虽能大幅降低计算代价，但其准确性受训练数据影响，对于特定体系存在不确定性。因此需要一种高效方法，在不进行重复模拟的前提下，评估不同MLIP之间的热力学一致性。

Method: 提出一种系统化重加权（reweighting）框架：以一个源MLIP（source MLIP）初始采样PMF，利用平均能量-间隙近似（mean energy-gap approximation）等解析修正，克服传统直接指数重加权（direct exponential reweighting）因势能面之间相空间交叠（phase-space overlap）过低导致的统计崩溃问题，从而高效地将PMF重加权至多个目标MLIP（target MLIPs）。

Result: 在包含601个原子的Li⁺纳米限域电解质传输体系中，该方法成功恢复了多个DFT参考级别（PBE+D3、PBE-sol、r²SCAN、r²SCAN-D4）的高保真热力学性质，仅需全模拟计算成本的一小部分。热力学分析显示，所研究的MLIPs根据训练数据分为两个不同簇，即使相空间交叠极低时，该方法仍能成功恢复反应自由能和活化自由能。

Conclusion: 该重加权框架建立了一种重要的诊断协议，能够在无需冗余、高资源消耗模拟的前提下，实现对材料化学性质的跨模型共识（cross-model consensus）评估，为高效获取可靠的热力学信息提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Free energy profiles serve as a fundamental bridge between microscopic atomic fluctuations and macroscopic thermodynamic observables. Estimating the free energy profile along a reaction coordinate, referred to as the potential of mean force (PMF), with density functional theory (DFT) accuracy is computationally expensive. Universal machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) drastically reduce this cost, but their accuracy is strongly determined by their training data and hence can be uncertain for a given system. In this work, we present a systematic and scalable framework for reweighting PMFs, initially sampled with a single 'source' MLIP, across a representative suite of target MLIPs. Because traditional direct exponential reweighting fails for large system sizes due to low phase-space overlap between potentials, we deploy robust analytical corrections. Applying this to a complex 601-atom system of Li$^+$ transport in a nanoconfined electrolyte, we demonstrate that a mean energy-gap approximation effectively bypasses statistical collapse, producing a highly stable PMF matching the target PMF. Using this approach, we recover high-fidelity target thermodynamics across multiple DFT reference levels (PBE+D3, PBE-sol, r$^2$SCAN,r$^2$SCAN-D4) at a fraction of the computational cost of full simulations. Furthermore, thermodynamic analysis reveals that the studied MLIPs partition into two distinct clusters driven by their training data. Our reweighting framework successfully recovers target thermodynamic properties--specifically, reaction and activation free energies--even when the phase-space overlap between potentials is critically low. Ultimately, this approach establishes a vital diagnostic protocol to achieve affordable cross-model consensus on materials chemistry properties without redundant, resource-intensive simulations.

</details>

### [14] [Stochastic Safety Limits and Scale-Dependent Power Fluctuations in Nuclear Reactors: A Critical Scaling Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15283)
*V. V. Ryazanov*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文探讨了随机风险过程（random risk processes）的边界泛函（boundary functionals）在核安全（nuclear safety）问题中的应用，重点关注首次到达某一水平的通过时间（first-passage time），为定向渗流（directed percolation）理论与工程保护参数计算之间提供了数学桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在反应堆启动等场景下，中子行为发生变化，中子团簇（neutron clustering）效应变得重要，中子分布从正态高斯分布（Gaussian distribution）转变为稳定极限分布（stable limiting distributions）。需要一种数学工具来准确计算随机事件的统计量、反应堆功率峰行为以及灾难性功率激增的概率，从而保障反应堆安全。

Method: 采用随机风险过程中的边界泛函方法，尤其是首次通过时间（first-passage time）这一特例，来建模和分析反应堆中中子行为的随机特性。

Result: 边界泛函能够准确计算随机事件的统计量，确定反应堆功率峰的行为、灾难性功率激增的概率以及其他对反应堆安全至关重要的量。

Conclusion: 边界泛函方法在抽象定向渗流理论与工程保护参数计算之间建立了数学联系，为核安全问题提供了一种有效的分析工具。

Abstract: Applying boundary functionals of random risk processes to various physical problems makes it possible to determine many important characteristics of these problems. For example, a special case of boundary functionals is the time to first reach a level, which is widely and successfully applied to a variety of problems. We consider the application of boundary functionals to solving nuclear safety problems. In situations such as reactor startup, as well as for certain types of reactors, neutron behavior changes. Neutron clustering begins to play an important role, and the distributions characterizing neutron behavior change. The normal Gaussian distribution is replaced by stable limiting, distributions to which the sums of random variables converge. Boundary functionals allow us to accurately calculate the statistics of random events, determine the behavior of reactor power peaks, the probabilities of catastrophic power surges, and other quantities important for reactor safety, providing a mathematical bridge between the abstract theory of directed percolation and engineering calculations of protection parameters. This article examines the first-passage time to reach a certain level.

</details>


### [15] [Solving Classical and Quantum Spin Glasses with Deep Boltzmann Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15899)
*Luca Leone,Arka Dutta,Markus Heyl,Enrico Prati,Pietro Torta*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出深度玻尔兹曼量子态（Deep Boltzmann Quantum States），一种基于深度玻尔兹曼机（deep Boltzmann machine）的神经量子态，结合高效块吉布斯采样（block Gibbs sampling）与退火式训练策略（包括自然梯度更新和哈密顿量硬度插值），在经典/量子伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）模型及NP难的作业车间调度问题（Job Shop Scheduling Problem）上匹配或超越了当前最优解，展示了深度神经网络在硬组合优化和量子多体系统研究中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分神经网络模型在求解量子多体系统的基态问题中取得了显著成功，但面对经典和量子自旋玻璃（spin glass）时，由于无序和能量阻挫（frustration）导致的指数级局域能量极小值及高能垒，传统的基于Metropolis的蒙特卡洛方法效率低下。因此，亟需一种能够有效处理此类硬优化和强阻挫问题的方法。

Method: 引入Deep Boltzmann Quantum States，一类受深度玻尔兹曼机启发的神经量子态（neural quantum states），继承了高效的块吉布斯采样（block Gibbs sampling）。训练算法包含两个关键进步：一是将自然梯度更新（natural-gradient updates）与最先进的随机优化器结合；二是通过从易解区域到难解区域的哈密顿量硬度插值逐步调整问题难度，无需在中间时刻紧密近似瞬时绝热态。

Result: 在多个具有无限程相互作用（infinite-range interactions）及数百个自旋的经典和量子伊辛自旋玻璃模型实例上，该方法匹配了精确解或当前最佳估计。此外，还解决了超出当前量子退火硬件（quantum annealing hardware）极限的NP难作业车间调度问题（Job Shop Scheduling Problem）实例。

Conclusion: 具有高效全局更新规则（global update rules）的深度神经架构，结合退火式方案进行训练，为解决现实世界中困难的组合优化问题以及研究阻挫量子多体系统提供了强大框架。

Abstract: Variational neural network models have achieved remarkable success in solving ground-state problems of quantum many-body systems. However, addressing classical and quantum spin glasses remains challenging, as disorder and energy frustration give rise to an exponentially large number of local energy minima separated by high-energy barriers, hindering the efficiency of conventional Metropolis-based Monte Carlo methods. To bridge this gap, we introduce Deep Boltzmann Quantum States, a class of neural quantum states inspired by deep Boltzmann machines that inherit efficient block Gibbs sampling. We also propose two key advances in the training algorithm. Firstly, we combine natural-gradient updates with state-of-the-art stochastic optimizers. Secondly, we gradually tune the hardness of the problem Hamiltonian by interpolating from an easy to a hard regime, without the need to closely approximate the instantaneous adiabatic state at intermediate times. We match the exact solution or the best available estimate for several instances of classical and quantum Ising spin-glass models with infinite-range interactions and hundreds of spins. We also solve instances of the NP-hard Job Shop Scheduling Problem exceeding the current limitations of quantum annealing hardware. To summarize, deep neural architectures with efficient global update rules and trained within an annealing-like scheme, provide a powerful framework for solving real-world hard combinatorial optimization and for investigating disordered quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [16] [Machine learning potential as a guide for eutectic in ultra-refractory multicomponent ceramics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16091)
*V. E. Valiulin,A. V. Mikheyenkov,N. M. Chtchelkatchev,E. A. Levashov*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）和神经网络（neural network）的新判据，用于确定超难熔合金（ultra-refractory alloys）的共晶点成分（eutectic point concentration），并在Ti-B-C体系中验证了其有效性。该方法无需固体合金晶体结构信息，直接在液相中运行，计算精度接近第一性原理（ab initio）方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统共晶点实验测定法对熔点超过3000 K的超难熔材料成本极高、技术挑战巨大，亟需一种低成本的先导性计算方法来指导实验。

Method: 提出一种基于神经网络（neural network）的机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）算法，作为共晶点浓度判据；该算法在液相中运行，无需固体合金晶体结构信息，并在目前研究最充分的三元难熔体系Ti-B-C上进行验证。

Result: 该机器学习原子间势算法实现了与第一性原理（ab initio）方法相当的精度，成功确定了Ti-B-C体系的共晶点成分。

Conclusion: 所提出的判据可作为高效先导工具，在超难熔合金体系中指导共晶点的实验测定，有效降低实验成本和难度。

Abstract: The experimental determination of eutectic points is a long-established and widely used technique, but it is generally only practical for systems with relatively low melting points. Many modern, promising materials, however, are ultra-refractory, with melting points exceeding 3000 K. For these systems, conventional melting experiments become prohibitively expensive and technically challenging. Advanced AI modeling can serve as a powerful precursor to guide successful experimentation in such cases. This work proposes a novel criterion for determining the eutectic point concentration in ultra-refractory alloys. The approach is verified using the Ti-B-C system - the most thoroughly studied three-component refractory system to date. The core of the algorithm is a machine-learning interatomic potential, based on a neural network, which achieves accuracy comparable to ab initio methods. Crucially, the algorithm operates effectively in the liquid phase, eliminating the need for information about the solid alloy's crystalline structure to estimate eutectic points.

### [17] [ColPackAgent: Agent-Skill-Guided Hard-Particle Monte Carlo Workflows for Colloidal Packing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15625)
*Lijie Ding,Changwoo Do*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ColPackAgent，一种通过模型上下文协议（MCP）工具服务器与智能体技能（agent skill）自主运行胶体堆积蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟的智能体框架。该框架将领域Python包与MCP工具和可移植智能体技能相结合，将模拟工具包转化为智能体辅助的研究工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用大语言模型（Large Language Model, LLM）智能体在缺乏专用模拟工具和工作流指令时，倾向于描述工作流而非可靠地执行模拟任务。因此，需要一种能够自主且结构化地执行胶体堆积模拟的智能体框架。

Method: ColPackAgent基于MCP工具服务器和智能体技能（agent skill）构建。MCP服务器封装了一个自定义的colpack Python包，该包基于HOOMD-blue硬粒子蒙特卡罗（hard-particle Monte Carlo）实现；智能体技能则编码了一个四阶段工作流合约（four-stage workflow contract）。系统支持人机交互反馈、端到端提示词自主执行以及按程序文件自动研究（autoresearch）三种运行模式。

Result: 在三维立方体粒子、二维圆盘与胶囊二元体系以及二维硬圆盘冻结相变自动研究等多个胶体堆积模拟示例中验证了系统有效性。此外，通过17个阶段特定提示词（stage-specific prompts）在多个LLM上进行了模型性能对比基准测试，评估了不同模型在设置、规划与分析工作流中的可靠性。

Conclusion: 将领域Python包与MCP工具和可移植智能体技能配对，是推动模拟工具包向智能体辅助研究工作流（agent-assisted research workflow）转化的实用路径。

Abstract: We introduce ColPackAgent, an agent framework that autonomously runs Monte Carlo simulations of colloidal packing through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) tool server and an agent skill, whether as a standalone agent or inside an existing agent system. By harnessing the MCP server and agent skill, ColPackAgent executes a structured workflow for colloidal packing simulations, which are central to studies of phase behavior, self-assembly, and materials design. Without dedicated simulation tools and workflow instructions, general-purpose Large Language Model (LLM) agents tend to describe such workflows rather than execute them reliably. The MCP server exposes a custom-built colpack Python package that wraps HOOMD-blue hard-particle Monte Carlo, and the skill encodes a four-stage workflow contract. ColPackAgent can carry out the workflow interactively with human feedback, autonomously from an end-to-end prompt, or as autoresearch following a provided program file. We demonstrate the system in different modes with several colloidal packing simulation examples such as cube particles in 3D, a binary system of disks and capsules in 2D, and the 2D hard-disk freezing transition using autoresearch. We also compare model performance on this workflow across a panel of LLMs with 17 stage-specific prompts. This benchmark provides a stage-level check of how reliably different models follow the setup, planning, and analysis workflow. Together, these results show that pairing a domain Python package with MCP tools and a portable agent skill provides a practical route for turning a simulation toolkit into an agent-assisted research workflow.

### [18] [Surrogate Neural Architecture Codesign Package (SNAC-Pack)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16138)
*Jason Weitz,Dmitri Demler,Benjamin Hawks,Aaron Wang,Nhan Tran,Javier Duarte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SNAC-Pack 是一个开源 AutoML 框架，通过多目标神经架构搜索（multi-objective neural architecture search）、硬件代理模型（hardware surrogate model）和量化感知训练（quantization-aware training, QAT）等模块，实现硬件感知的神经网络架构协同设计，并支持端到端 FPGA 部署，在两个物理实验任务上显著缩短设计周期并提升资源效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经架构搜索（NAS）方法通常仅优化准确率，或采用比特运算量（bit operations, BOPs）等与硬件实际成本关联较差的代理指标。对于 FPGA 部署场景，硬件成本由查找表、DSP、触发器、BRAM 和延迟等多维预算决定，现有方法与实际硬件成本之间的差距尤为突出。

Method: SNAC-Pack 采用多目标全局搜索（multi-objective global search），结合 Optuna 和 NSGA-II 算法，通过共享 SQLite 存储支持跨计算节点的并行搜索。硬件代理模型（hardware surrogate model）在每次试验中输出资源和延迟估计，避免合成耗时。随后进行局部搜索（local search），结合量化感知训练（QAT）与迭代幅度剪枝（iterative magnitude pruning）形成压缩循环，最终通过 hls4ml 库将模型综合为 FPGA 固件。系统通过 YAML 配置和可选的智能体前端支持新数据集适配。

Result: 在大型强子对撞机喷注分类和超导量子比特读取两个任务上，SNAC-Pack 发现的紧凑架构在任务指标上达到或超越强基线（strong baselines），同时降低了 FPGA 资源利用率。在量子比特读取任务中，设计空间探索从数月的手动调优缩短至数小时的自动搜索。

Conclusion: SNAC-Pack 有效弥合了神经架构搜索与 FPGA 硬件部署之间的成本鸿沟，证明了基于硬件代理模型和多目标优化的协同设计策略能够在大幅加速设计流程的同时保持甚至提升任务性能。

Abstract: Neural architecture search (NAS) is a powerful approach for automating model design, but existing methods often optimize for accuracy alone or rely on proxy metrics such as bit operations (BOPs) that correlate poorly with hardware cost. This gap is particularly large for FPGA deployment, where cost is dominated by a multi-dimensional budget of lookup tables, DSPs, flip-flops, BRAM, and latency. We present the Surrogate Neural Architecture Codesign Package (SNAC-Pack), an open-source AutoML framework for hardware-aware neural architecture codesign and end-to-end FPGA deployment. SNAC-Pack runs a multi-objective global search with Optuna and NSGA-II, loading trials to a shared SQLite store that enables parallel workers across compute nodes. A hardware surrogate model outputs per-trial resource and latency estimates, avoiding the synthesis cost that would otherwise dominate the search loop. A local search stage then applies quantization-aware training (QAT) together with iterative magnitude pruning in a combined compression loop, after which the final model is synthesized to FPGA firmware via the hls4ml Python library. A YAML configuration and an optional agentic frontend let users run the pipeline on new datasets without modifying the framework. We demonstrate SNAC-Pack on jet classification at the Large Hadron Collider and superconducting qubit readout, discovering compact architectures that match or exceed strong baselines on the task metric while reducing FPGA resource utilization and, in the qubit readout case, reducing the design space exploration process from months of manual fine-tuning to hours of automated search.

</details>


### [19] [Variational Autoregressive Networks with probability priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16020)
*Piotr Białas,Piotr Korcyl,Tomasz Stebel,Dawid Zapolski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出在蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法中引入物理先验（physics-informed priors）作为训练起点，以缓解临界慢化（critical slowing down）和深度学习模型训练困难的问题。通过在伊辛模型（Ising model）和爱德华兹-安德森自旋玻璃模型（Edwards-Anderson spin glass model）上的实验，证明物理先验能够降低训练负担，并支持更大系统规模的模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒙特卡洛方法（Monte Carlo methods）在相变附近因临界慢化（critical slowing down）导致自相关时间急剧增加，效率严重下降。尽管深度学习方法被提出用于缓解此问题，但模型训练困难，部分原因是通用机器学习架构忽略了底层物理对称性（physical symmetries），迫使网络从零开始重新学习。

Method: 在已有整合自旋-自旋相互作用（spin-spin interactions）策略的基础上，提出一种利用先验概率分布（prior probability distribution）作为训练起点的框架。该框架将物理先验（physics-informed priors）嵌入模型，替代传统的“空白画布”（blank slate）模型。

Result: 在伊辛模型（Ising model）和爱德华兹-安德森自旋玻璃模型（Edwards-Anderson spin glass model）上的实验结果表明，采用物理先验模型能够减轻训练负担，并支持更大系统规模的离散自旋模型（discrete spin models）模拟。

Conclusion: 从“空白画布”模型转向物理先验模型，可有效降低训练难度，提升蒙特卡洛方法在离散自旋模型中的模拟效率。

Abstract: Monte Carlo methods are essential across diverse scientific fields, yet their efficiency is frequently hampered by critical slowing down-a sharp increase in autocorrelation times near phase transitions. Although deep learning approaches, such as neural-network-based samplers, have been proposed to alleviate this issue, they face another serious problem: the difficulty of training the models. This difficulty partially stems from the overly general nature of original machine-learning architectures, which often ignore underlying physical symmetries and force networks to relearn them from scratch. In this paper, we demonstrate that incorporating physical priors into the model significantly enhances performance. Building upon existing strategies that integrate spin-spin interactions, we propose a framework that utilizes a prior probability distribution as a starting point for training. Our results for the Ising model, as well as for the Edwards-Anderson spin glass model, suggest that moving away from `blank slate' models in favor of physics-informed priors reduces the training burden and facilitates the simulation of larger system sizes in discrete spin models.

### [20] [Multifractal and Ergodic Properties of Conductance Fluctuations under Strong Disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15447)
*Marcos A. A. de Sousa,Heitor R. Publio,Henrique A. de Lima,Adauto J. F. de Souza,Fernando A. Oliveira,Anderson L. R. Barbosa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过标准多重分形分析，揭示二维无序紧束缚模型中电导涨落随安德森无序强度增加从非遍历到遍历的转变，并发现多重分形性在两个区间均存在，但受无序强度影响表现出不同的时间关联与分布特征。结果对铅电极几何结构不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无序介观系统中电导涨落的随机性质是量子输运的基础问题。本研究旨在探究不同无序强度下电导涨落的多重分形（multifractal）与遍历（ergodic）特性及其转变机制。

Method: 对二维紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）在不同安德森无序（Anderson disorder）强度下生成电导的虚拟时间序列，采用标准多重分形分析，并结合电导关联函数（conductance correlation function）及序列混洗（shuffling）方法进行对比分析。

Result: 电导涨落随无序强度增加经历从非遍历（non-ergodic）到遍历行为的转变；多重分形性在两个区间均持续存在，但在强无序（遍历）区间对混洗不敏感，表明分布效应主导时间组织，而弱无序（非遍历）区间长程关联起重要作用。这些发现对铅电极几何结构（非对称与对称）具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该结果为无序量子输运中遍历性、多重分形性与稀有事件（rare events）之间的相互作用提供了新见解。

Abstract: Understanding the stochastic properties of conductance fluctuations in disordered mesoscopic systems is fundamental to quantum transport. In this work, we investigate the multifractal and ergodic properties of the fictitious time series of conductance in two-dimensional tight-binding models under varying Anderson disorder. Using standard multifractal analysis, we show that conductance fluctuations exhibit a transition from non-ergodic to ergodic behavior as the disorder strength increases, as evidenced by the decay of the conductance correlation function. Remarkably, multifractality persists in both regimes; however, it becomes insensitive to shuffling in the strong-disorder (ergodic) regime, suggesting that distributional effects dominate temporal organization. On the contrary, in the weakly disordered (non-ergodic) regime, long-range correlations play a significant role. These findings are robust against changes in lead geometry (asymmetric vs. symmetric). Our results provide new insights into the interplay between ergodicity, multifractality, and rare events in disordered quantum transport.

### [21] [Entropy Production from Spin--Vibrational Coupling in Endohedral-Fullerene Qubits Encapsulated in Suspended Carbon Nanotubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15521)
*Cristian Staii*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个混合量子开放系统模型，将碳纳米管（CNT）谐振器的驱动量子布朗运动与有效Jaynes-Cummings自旋-振动耦合相结合，分析了在CNT包裹顺磁性内嵌富勒烯（如N@C₆₀和P@C₆₀）构成的混合架构中熵的产生、不可逆性与信息流，并展示了自旋-振动杂化如何重新分配相干交换与耗散通道之间的不可逆性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在结构化量子环境中研究不可逆性与信息流提供可控平台，并建立混合碳纳米管-富勒烯架构中熵平衡与熵产生的理论框架。

Method: 基于相空间传播子（phase-space propagator）方法，将CNT动力学用Wigner函数及其高斯传播子解析表达；将自旋-力学耦合嵌入包含机械阻尼、自旋弛豫、纯退相和热激活激发的Lindblad主方程；推导熵平衡方程，分离熵流与非负熵产生项。

Result: 磁梯度增强的自旋-声子耦合、共振驱动和适中热占据可导致振荡器主导与自旋主导的熵产生区间之间的交叉；自旋-振动杂化重新分配了相干交换与耗散通道之间的不可逆性。

Conclusion: 该框架为利用CNT-内嵌富勒烯杂化体系作为纳米尺度平台，研究非平衡量子热力学、退相干及振动环境中的信息损失提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Hybrid carbon nanotube-fullerene architectures provide a controllable platform for studying irreversibility and information flow in structured quantum environments. We analyze entropy generation in a system where paramagnetic endohedral fullerenes, such as N@C$_{60}$ and P@C$_{60}$, are encapsulated inside a suspended carbon nanotube (CNT) resonator, with selected multi-level fullerene spin states forming an effective qubit coupled to quantized CNT flexural modes. Building on prior work on fullerene-filled CNTs, spin-phonon control in suspended nanotubes, and phase-space propagators for damped driven oscillators, we develop a hybrid open-system model combining driven quantum Brownian motion of the CNT with an effective Jaynes-Cummings spin-vibrational interaction. The resonator dynamics are represented by a Wigner function whose evolution is written analytically in terms of the initial Wigner distribution and a Gaussian propagator. This phase-space description separates drive-induced displacement, diffusion, and damping, and connects these processes directly to entropy flow. The coupled spin-mechanical dynamics are embedded in a Lindblad master equation including mechanical damping, spin relaxation, pure dephasing, and thermally activated excitation. Within this framework we derive the entropy balance, identify entropy flux and non-negative entropy production, and examine how spin-vibrational hybridization redistributes irreversibility between coherent exchange and dissipative channels. We show that magnetic-gradient-enhanced spin-phonon coupling, resonant driving, and moderate thermal occupation produce crossovers between oscillator-dominated and spin-dominated entropy-production regimes. The framework provides a basis for using CNT-PEF hybrids as nanoscale platforms to study nonequilibrium quantum thermodynamics, decoherence, and information loss in vibrational environments.

### [22] [Quantum Geometry-Driven Nonlinear Spin Currents in Floquet Non-Hermitian Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15541)
*Kai Chen,Jie Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过引入周期性光驱（periodic optical driving）和非厄米性（non-Hermiticity），建立了非厄米交错磁体（altermagnet）中非线性自旋电流的量子几何（quantum geometric）理论框架，揭示了光学偏振可主动调控甚至反转自旋电流方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体在自旋电子学（spintronics）中极具潜力，但如何动态调控其自旋响应仍是一个基本挑战。

Method: 推导了具有谱线隙（spectral line gap）的非厄米相中非线性自旋电流的普适解析表达式；将形式论应用于Floquet非厄米d波交错磁体进行分析。

Result: 非线性自旋电导率（nonlinear spin conductivity）主要由裸量子度量（bare quantum metric）主导；光学场的偏振能够主动调控甚至严格反转纵向和横向自旋电流的方向。

Conclusion: 该工作为先进磁性材料中非线性自旋输运（nonlinear spin transport）的光学操控建立了量子几何框架。

Abstract: Altermagnets are rapidly emerging as a highly promising platform for spintronics, yet dynamically controlling their spin responses remains a fundamental challenge. In this work, we demonstrate that introducing periodic optical driving and non-Hermiticity provides a powerful route to achieve tunable control over these systems. We derive a general analytical expression for nonlinear spin currents in non-Hermitian phases with a spectral line gap, revealing that the intrinsic response cleanly separates into quantum metric, Berry curvature, and Berry connection dipole contributions. Applying this formalism to a Floquet non-Hermitian $d$-wave altermagnet, we uncover that the nonlinear spin conductivity is overwhelmingly dominated by the bare quantum metric. Furthermore, we show that the optical field's polarization can actively tune -- and even strictly reverse -- the direction of both longitudinal and transverse spin currents. Our work establishes a quantum geometric framework for the optical manipulation of nonlinear spin transport in advanced magnetic materials.

### [23] [Topological property of graphene with triangular array of nanoholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15631)
*Yong-Cheng Jiang,Xing-Xiang Wang,Xiao Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文从理论上研究了具有C6v对称性规则排列纳米孔的石墨烯中的非平庸能带拓扑。研究发现，在3√3×3√3三角形纳米孔阵列中，费米能级附近的Γ点存在能隙和能带反转，而费米能级深处存在表现为受阻原子极限（OAL）的价带，导致费米能级处能隙拓扑平庸，但OAL的非平庸拓扑在带状结构中表现为两条平带及边缘局域态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有规则纳米孔阵列（C6v对称性）的石墨烯衍生物中可能存在的丰富拓扑行为，揭示其能带拓扑性质及边缘态特征。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究具有C6v对称性规则排列纳米孔的石墨烯体系，具体针对3√3×3√3三角形纳米孔阵列的能带结构、宇称（parity）指数变化及能带反转（band inversion）进行理论计算与分析。

Result: 在费米能级附近的Γ点存在能隙与能带反转，导致宇称指数变化；费米能级深处出现一系列表现为受阻原子极限（obstructed atomic limit, OAL）的价带，同样存在宇称指数不平衡。费米能级处的能隙拓扑平庸且无边缘态，而OAL的非平凡拓扑在带状结构中产生两条平带（flat bands）及相应的边缘局域电子态。

Conclusion: 石墨烯纳米孔阵列展现出丰富的拓扑行为，费米能级深处的OAL能带具有非平庸拓扑，并在边缘形成局域态，这为石墨烯衍生物中的拓扑现象提供了新的探索方向。

Abstract: The nontrivial band topology for graphene with regular arrays of nanoholes with $C_{6v}$ symmetry is investigated theoretically. For the case of $3\sqrt{3} \times 3\sqrt{3}$ triangular array of nanoholes, we find an energy gap at $Γ$ point around the Fermi level associated with a band inversion which induces change in parity indices, whereas deep below the Fermi level there are a bunch of valence bands characterized as obstructed atomic limit (OAL) which also accommodate imbalance in parity indices. This band structure renders the gap at the Fermi level topologically trivial and carrying no edge states, while the nontrivial band topology of the OAL manifests in two flat bands in the ribbon structure associated with localized electronic states at ribbon edges. The present results exhibit rich topological behaviors in graphene derivatives waiting for explorations.

</details>


### [24] [Stable magnetic nanodomains engineered via Ga+-ion irradiation for deterministic sequential switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15883)
*Gijs W. A. Simons,Rik F. J. van Haren,Bert Koopmans*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出通过空间剪裁各向异性梯度（anisotropy gradients）实现纳米尺度磁性畴（magnetic domain）的确定性控制，利用聚焦镓离子辐照（focused Ga+-ion irradiation）构建“各向异性阱”（anisotropy wells），替代传统缺陷介导的随机钉扎机制，从而实现可控的磁畴壁钉扎与双向顺序切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度的磁畴形成受限于随机缺陷介导（stochastic defect-mediated）和不稳定钉扎（unstable pinning），这些因素限制了自旋电子学架构（spintronic architectures）的可扩展性与可重现性。

Method: 采用聚焦镓离子辐照对磁性薄膜进行空间剪裁，构建包含纳米尺度“各向异性阱”的磁能量景观（magnetic energy landscapes）；建立描述梯度各向异性剖面（graded anisotropy profiles）中畴壁（domain-wall）能量的分析框架，并辅以微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulations）与实验验证。

Result: 实现了连续铁磁薄膜中可编程多畴构型（programmable multi-domain configurations），展示了750 nm区域稳健、可重现的切换，并初步实现了100 nm尺度的结果，接近畴壁宽度（domain-wall width）所设的理论极限。

Conclusion: 用工程化的能量景观替代不稳定的钉扎机制，建立了确定性磁态编程（deterministic magnetic-state programming）的可扩展材料策略，为高密度、低能耗的自旋电子学与可重构磁性纳米器件（reconfigurable magnetic nanodevices）开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Precise control of magnetic domain formation at the nanoscale remains constrained by stochastic defect-mediated and unstable pinning, limiting scalability and reproducibility in spintronic architectures. Here we demonstrate that spatially engineered anisotropy gradients provide a deterministic alternative. Using focused Ga+-ion irradiation, we pattern magnetic energy landscapes containing nanoscale "anisotropy wells" that confine magnetic domain walls and enable bidirectional sequential switching without reliance on difficult-to-control material disorder. An analytical framework describing domain-wall energetics in graded anisotropy profiles yields predictive design rules for depinning and stability, which are supported by micromagnetic simulations and experiments. We realize programmable multi-domain configurations in continuous ferromagnetic films and demonstrate robust, reproducible switching of 750 nm regions, while first results for 100 nm are shown, approaching the theoretical limit set by the domain-wall width. By replacing unstable pinning with engineered energy landscapes, this anisotropy landscape establishes a scalable materials strategy for deterministic magnetic-state programming and opens a pathway toward dense, energy-efficient spintronic and reconfigurable magnetic nanodevices.

### [25] [Tunable Crossed Andreev Reflection in Bipolar Magnetic Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15939)
*Polireddi Naveen,Abhiram Soori*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在双极磁性半导体（bipolar magnetic semiconductor, BMS）中通过独立调节两个区域的化学势，实现对交叉安德烈夫反射（crossed Andreev reflection, CAR）的可控增强或抑制，为非局域输运和自旋电子学器件应用提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交叉安德烈夫反射（CAR）是一种在超导体与两个空间分离的金属界面处产生的非局域量子输运现象，能够建立非局域的电子-空穴转换并产生量子纠缠。然而，如何实现对其可调谐控制仍是待解决的问题。本文旨在利用双极磁性半导体（BMS）中导带和价带具有相反自旋极化的特性，通过独立调节两个区域的化学势来实现对CAR的灵活操控。

Method: 通过在两个双极磁性半导体（BMS）引线中工程化自旋极化能带的排列方式，并独立调节两个区域（即两个金属端）的化学势（chemical potential），来实现对交叉安德烈夫反射（CAR）过程的选择性增强或抑制。

Result: 研究发现，通过调控自旋极化能带的对齐情况，CAR可以被选择性地增强或抑制。这种可调性使得对非局域输运和关联电子动力学的精确操控成为可能。

Conclusion: 该工作为自旋电子学（spintronics）和超导器件（superconducting device）应用提供了有前景的前景，实现了对非局域输运及相关电子动力学的精确操控。

Abstract: Crossed Andreev reflection (CAR) is a nonlocal quantum transport phenomenon that arises at the interface between a superconductor and two spatially separated metals. In this process, an electron incident from one metal combines with another electron originating from the other metal to form a Cooper pair in the superconductor. As a consequence, a hole is emitted into the second metal, establishing a nonlocal electron-hole conversion process. In contrast to local Andreev reflection -- where electron-to-hole conversion occurs within the same region -- CAR intrinsically links two spatially separated carriers, giving rise to nonlocal correlations and quantum entanglement. In bipolar magnetic semiconductors (BMSs), the conduction and valence bands possess opposite spin polarizations. We propose to achieve tunable control of CAR by independently adjusting the chemical potentials of the two regions. By engineering the alignment of spin-polarized bands in the two BMS leads, CAR can be selectively enhanced or suppressed. This tunability enables precise manipulation of nonlocal transport, and correlated electron dynamics, offering promising prospects for spintronic and superconducting device applications.

### [26] [Orbital Angular Momentum Textures and Currents in a Discrete Helix: Equilibrium and Linear Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15981)
*Danny Cordova,Bertrand Berche,Ernesto Medina*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过构建最小三轨道紧束缚模型（three-orbital tight-binding model）证明，在手性单螺旋链中，仅凭手性（chirality）即可产生动量依赖的轨道角动量织构（orbital-angular-momentum texture），无需原子自旋-轨道耦合（spin–orbit coupling）。该轨道织构在平衡态下平均为零，但可产生类持续轨道角动量流和手性依赖的末端磁化；在外加纵向电场下产生轨道埃德尔斯坦响应（orbital Edelstein response），并通过轨道-自旋转导（orbital-to-spin transduction）实现强于传统自旋埃德尔斯坦机制的自旋注入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来低维系统中非平衡轨道角动量（nonequilibrium orbital angular momentum）重新引起关注，但手性本身是否足以独立产生轨道角动量响应尚不清楚。本文旨在识别手性作为一维系统中轨道角动量响应的最小微观要素（minimal microscopic ingredient）。

Method: 引入由$p_r,p_φ,p_z$三个局域轨道组成的单螺旋链最小紧束缚模型，通过斯莱特-科斯特杂化（Slater–Koster hybridization）分析轨道织构的动量依赖性。研究包括：平衡态轨道织构的奇偶性分析、有限螺旋下的末端磁化、纵向电场下的轨道埃德尔斯坦响应和轨道电流电导率，以及引入自旋自由度后的轨道-自旋转导效应。

Result: 在单螺旋几何中，径向轨道织构恒为零，角向和纵向分量由动量奇函数部分产生，平衡态平均轨道织构因宇称（parity）而消失，但类持续轨道角动量流可能存在并导致手性依赖的末端磁化。纵向电场下产生有限轨道埃德尔斯坦响应，但投影纵向轨道电流电导率在线性区间内因宇称而消失。引入自旋后，轨道织构通过轨道-自旋转导产生自旋极化，其自旋响应由远大于裸相对论自旋-轨道耦合尺度的轨道重叠标度控制。

Conclusion: 手性是产生一维系统轨道角动量响应的最小编微观要素，无需原子自旋-轨道耦合即可实现轨道角动量效应。基于轨道-自旋转导的机制相比传统自旋埃德尔斯坦机制更强，为手性导体中的自旋选择性（spin selectivity）提供了轨道路径解释。

Abstract: Recently, nonequilibrium orbital angular momentum in low-dimensional systems has attracted renewed attention. Here we introduce a minimal three-orbital tight-binding model for a single helical chain and show that chirality alone generates a momentum-dependent orbital-angular-momentum texture through Slater--Koster hybridization in the local basis $(p_r,p_φ,p_z)$, without requiring atomic spin--orbit coupling. In the single-helix geometry, the radial orbital texture vanishes identically, while the azimuthal and longitudinal components remain finite and arise from the odd-in-momentum $(p_z,p_r)$ and $(p_r,p_φ)$ sectors. As a result, the equilibrium average orbital texture vanishes by parity, although persistent-like orbital angular momentum currents may still exist and imply chirality-dependent end magnetization in a finite helix. Under an applied longitudinal electric field, the system develops a finite orbital Edelstein response, whereas the projected longitudinal orbital-current conductivity vanishes in the linear regime by parity. When spin degrees of freedom are included, the orbital texture acts as a source of spin polarization through orbital-to-spin transduction. The resulting spin response is controlled by orbital overlap scales much larger than the bare relativistic spin--orbit scale, making it a stronger candidate for spin injection than the conventional spin Edelstein mechanism. These results identify chirality as the minimal microscopic ingredient for generating orbital angular momentum response in one-dimensional systems and support an orbital route to spin selectivity in chiral conductors.

</details>


### [27] [Transport signatures of valley polarization in graphene multilayers: In-plane linear magnetoconductivity vs anomalous Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16061)
*Fernando Peñaranda,Fernando de Juan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在二维材料中，面内线性磁导率（LMC）可作为谷极化（valley polarization）的替代探测手段，即使反常霍尔效应（AHE）为零时仍有效，并针对扭曲双层石墨烯和菱方石墨烯多层结构进行了理论预测与计算分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在时间反演对称性破缺的二维材料中，轨道磁体（orbital magnet）可通过反常霍尔效应（AHE）违反昂萨格关系（Onsager relations）来探测。然而，当AHE为零时，需要一种替代的输运探测手段来表征谷极化（valley polarization）。

Method: 通过自洽哈特里-福克方法（self-consistent Hartree-Fock）和半经典输运计算（semiclassical transport calculations），对扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）和菱方石墨烯多层结构（rhombohedral graphene multilayers）两类谷极化体系进行理论建模，预测其面内线性磁导率（LMC）行为。

Result: 在扭曲双层石墨烯中，LMC为有限值而AHE为零（除非存在来自衬底（substrate）的额外对称性破缺）；在菱方石墨烯多层结构中，LMC与AHE均随谷极化变化，因二者具有相同的对称性（symmetry）。多层结构中的效应源于层间隧穿（interlayer tunneling）所引发的面内轨道磁矩（in-plane orbital moments）和贝里曲率（Berry curvatures），且占主导地位并超越自旋响应（spin response）。

Conclusion: 奇场依赖的面内线性磁导率（odd-in-field in-plane LMC）可作为探测谷极化的有效替代手段，尤其适用于AHE消失的情形，并为近期相关实验提供了理论分析依据。

Abstract: In two-dimensional materials where interacting Fermi pockets occur in valleys related by time-reversal symmetry, a spontaneous valley imbalance results in a novel state known as an orbital magnet. Due to the breaking of time-reversal symmetry, this state can be probed in transport experiments by the violation of Onsager relations, most often done through the anomalous Hall effect (AHE). Here we propose that odd-in-field, in-plane linear magnetoconductivity (LMC) is an alternative probe of valley polarization which can occur even when the AHE vanishes. In multilayer structures, the effect originates from in-plane orbital moments and Berry curvatures enabled by interlayer tunneling and dominates over the spin response. After a classification of many recently studied multilayers, we focus on two valley polarized examples: twisted bilayer graphene, where LMC is finite but the AHE vanishes unless additional symmetry breaking from the substrate is present, and rhombohedral graphene multilayers, where LMC and AHE both track valley polarization because they have the same symmetry. Using self-consistent Hartree-Fock and semiclassical transport calculations, we present detailed predictions of LMR for these two examples and analyze the implications for recent experiments.

</details>


### [28] [In-situ correlative SEM/KPFM for semiconductor devices and 2D heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16062)
*Prabhu Prasad Swain,Nahid Hosseini,Eveline. S Mayner,Aleksandra Radenovic,Marcos Penedo,Georg E. Fantner*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文首次在扫描电子显微镜（SEM）内实现了基于自感测悬臂（self-sensing cantilevers）的单次扫描外差开尔文探针力显微镜（heterodyne Kelvin probe force microscopy, heterodyne KPFM）原位测量。通过解调激励与检测信号，克服了压阻式悬臂（piezo-resistive cantilevers）固有的容性串扰（capacitive crosstalk），实现了表面形貌（topography）与接触电势差（contact potential difference, CPD）的同时成像，并与成分分析（compositional analysis）关联。该方法在二维异质结构和半导体电路上验证了极佳的信号质量，并揭示了电子束扫描参数对表面电势衬度（surface potential contrast）的直接影响，为下一代半导体器件分析和材料科学建立了稳健的多功能原位关联成像模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关联纳米尺度表面表征（correlative nanoscale surface characterization）需要在同一环境下同时测量电子和结构性质，这对现代材料科学和半导体失效分析（semiconductor failure analysis）至关重要。自感测悬臂辅助的原位原子力显微镜-扫描电子显微镜（in-situ AFM-SEM）测量虽有巨大潜力，但受限于其固有的容性串扰问题，因此需要一种能够克服该限制的新方法。

Method: 采用压阻式悬臂（piezo-resistive cantilevers），首次在扫描电子显微镜内实现原位单次扫描外差开尔文探针力显微镜（single-pass heterodyne KPFM）。通过解调（demodulating）激励与检测信号，同时映射表面形貌和接触电势差，并将结果与成分分析关联。系统比较了该外差技术的不同操作模式，评估其空间分辨率（spatial resolution）、信号灵敏度（signal sensitivity）和信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）。

Result: 综合方法获得了卓越的信号质量，并揭示了电子束扫描参数可以直接影响表面电势衬度。该方法在二维异质结构（two-dimensional heterostructures）和半导体电路（semiconductor circuits）上成功验证了关联分析工作流程。

Conclusion: 该工作为在扫描电子显微镜内部进行原位开尔文力和形貌成像建立了一种稳健且通用的关联成像模式，适用于下一代半导体器件分析和材料科学研究。

Abstract: Correlative nanoscale surface characterization benefits from simultaneously measuring electronic and structural properties in the same environment, a capability that is essential for modern-day materials science and semiconductor failure analysis. In-situ AFM-SEM measurements facilitated by self-sensing cantilevers offer great potential here; however, they are limited due to their inherent capacitive crosstalk. Here, we demonstrate for the first time the in-situ implementation of single-pass heterodyne Kelvin probe force microscopy inside a scanning electron microscope, using piezo-resistive cantilevers. We overcome the capacitive crosstalk prevalent in piezo-resistive cantilevers by demodulating excitation and detection to simultaneously map surface topography and contact potential difference for correlation with compositional analysis. We systematically compare different operational modes of this heterodyne technique, elucidating their spatial resolution, signal sensitivity, and signal-to-noise ratio. The integrated approach yields exceptional signal quality and reveals how electron beam scan parameters can directly influence surface potential contrast. We demonstrate this correlative analysis workflow on two-dimensional heterostructures and semiconductor circuits. This work establishes a robust and versatile correlative imaging mode for in-situ Kelvin force and topography imaging inside a scanning electron microscope for next-generation semiconductor device analysis and materials science.

</details>


### [29] [Acoustic spin resonance in polariton condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16236)
*D. A. Saltykova,A. Kudlis,A. V. Yulin,I. A. Shelykh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了空间均匀自旋极化激元凝聚体中的声学自旋共振现象，揭示了声波驱动的应变有效磁场如何调控凝聚体赝自旋，并分析了非线性、耗散、迟滞及分岔等动力学特性，提出了相干声驱动作为极化激元赝自旋可控操控的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用纵向声波驱动的应变有效磁场，实现对空间均匀自旋极化激元凝聚体中赝自旋（pseudospin）的共振、非线性及可切换控制，从而为极化激元自旋动力学提供新的调控手段。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，构建声波诱导的时变应变有效磁场模型，研究其与静态面内线性极化分裂（linear-polarization splitting）的相互作用，并纳入自旋依赖相互作用、增益、库动力学、自旋弛豫及寿命各向异性等机制。

Result: 自旋依赖相互作用导致共振频移及非线性线形；增益、库动力学与自旋弛豫引入耗散与历史依赖效应，产生振幅迟滞（hysteresis）。寿命各向异性下凝聚体可出现具有有限圆极化的分岔稳态，声共振驱动可实现相应面外分支之间的切换。塞曼分裂（Zeeman splitting）提供额外的保守调谐旋钮。

Conclusion: 相干声驱动是实现极化激元赝自旋动力学共振、非线性及可切换控制的有效途径。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate acoustic spin resonance in a spatially homogeneous spinor polariton condensate. A longitudinal acoustic wave generates a time-periodic strain-induced effective magnetic field acting on the condensate pseudospin. When this field is transverse to the static in-plane linear-polarization splitting, it resonantly drives polarization oscillations. We show that spin-dependent interactions shift the resonance and produce nonlinear line shapes, while gain, reservoir dynamics, and spin relaxation make the response dissipative and history-dependent, producing amplitude hysteresis. In the presence of lifetime anisotropy, the condensate can develop a bifurcated stationary state with finite circular polarization, and a resonant acoustic drive can switch between the corresponding out-of-plane branches. A Zeeman splitting provides an additional conservative knob for tuning the resonance frequency. Our results identify coherent acoustic driving as a route to resonant, nonlinear, and switchable control of polariton pseudospin dynamics.

### [30] [Lattice-Spring Analogy for Isotropic Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15209)
*D. M. LI,Meng-Cheng HE*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种各向同性弹性晶格弹簧模型（IELSM），通过修正经典晶格弹簧模型（LSM）中的总应变能并引入额外的体积约束，突破了固定泊松比的限制，实现了对任意泊松比各向同性弹性材料的自洽模拟。该模型在数值稳定性、精度与收敛性方面优于标准有限元单元，并通过多种断裂力学算例验证了其在奇异应力场分析中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典晶格弹簧模型（Lattice Spring Model, LSM）受限于固定的泊松比，无法模拟任意泊松比的各向同性弹性材料。为解决这一根本性局限，有必要发展一种能够建立晶格参数与宏观弹性常数之间直接映射关系的改进模型。

Method: IELSM通过修正LSM中的总应变能（total strain energy），在经典轴向弹簧框架基础上引入额外的体积约束（volumetric constraints），建立模型参数与宏观弹性常数的直接精确映射。数值实现的核心是将体积约束分解为轴向、剪切和旋转弹簧（axial, shear and rotational springs）的等效组合。

Result: 特征值分析表明，IELSM的数值稳定性优于标准双线性四边形单元（bilinear quadrilateral element）和常应变三角形单元（constant strain triangular element）。单轴拉伸、纯剪切、圆孔应力集中及中心与十字形裂纹的应力奇异性分析验证了模型的高精度、收敛性与计算鲁棒性，在裂尖应力强度因子计算中表现优异。

Conclusion: IELSM弥合了晶格弹簧模型与连续介质力学（continuum mechanics）之间的鸿沟，建立了一个在保持理论一致性的同时兼具计算精度的类比框架（analog framework），可用于弹性边值问题的求解。该模型为基于离散方法的断裂模拟奠定了基础。

Abstract: This study introduces an innovative Isotropic Elastic Lattice Spring Model (IELSM) that addresses the fundamental limitation of classical lattice spring models: the constraint of fixed Poisson's ratio. By amending the total strain energy within the Lattice Spring Model (LSM), IELSM provides a self-consistent formulation for simulating isotropic elastic materials with arbitrary Poisson's ratios. The model's core innovation lies in augmenting classical axial spring frameworks with additional volumetric constraints, establishing a direct and exact mapping between IELSM's parameters and macroscopic elastic constants. This enables simulation across the full admissible Poisson's ratio: -1 < ν < 1 under plane stress and -1 < ν< 0.5 under plane strain conditions. Eigenvalue analysis indicates that the IELSM has better numerical stability compared to the standard bilinear quadrilateral element and the constant strain triangular element. The characteristic of the numerical implementation lies in directly decomposing the additional volumetric constraints into an equivalent combination of standard mechanical components (axial, shear and rotational springs), laying the foundation for the realization of fracture simulation based on discrete methods. Comprehensive validation through uniaxial tension, pure shear, stress concentration around a circular hole, and stress singularity analyses for central and crucifix-shaped cracks demonstrates IELSM's exceptional accuracy, convergence and computational robustness. The model exhibits excellent performance in stress intensity factor calculations at crack tips, validating its effectiveness for singular stress field analysis. This work bridges the gap between LSM and continuum mechanics, establishing an analog framework that maintains theoretical consistency while offering computational accuracy for the solution of elastic boundary value problems.

</details>

### [31] [Zitterbewegung velocity in semiclassical electron dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15292)
*Dimitrie Culcer*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文从量子刘维尔方程（Liouville equation）出发，识别出一种新的颤动速度（Zitterbewegung velocity），该速度涉及量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）的对称和反对称分量的异相振荡。该速度解决了位置偏移悖论（position-shift paradox），并直接关联到无质量狄拉克费米子（massless Dirac fermions）的最小电导率（minimum conductivity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半经典理论（semiclassical treatment）无法捕捉固体中电子动力学中的Zitterbewegung效应，需要新的理论框架来解释相关现象。

Method: 以量子刘维尔方程为起点，识别出量子几何张量的对称与反对称分量的异相振荡，从而导出一种新的Zitterbewegung速度。

Result: 新定义的Zitterbewegung速度能够通过积分半经典方程恢复场致电子位置偏移，从而解决位置偏移悖论；此外，该速度与无质量狄拉克费米子的最小电导率直接相关。

Conclusion: Zitterbewegung速度是连接量子几何效应与半经典输运现象的关键桥梁，为理解固体中电子动力学提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Zitterbewegung plays a major role in electron dynamics in solids, yet is not captured in conventional semiclassical treatments. Here, starting from the quantum Liouville equation, I identify a new Zitterbewegung velocity, which involves the symmetric and antisymmetric components of the quantum geometric tensor oscillating out of phase. The Zitterbewegung velocity resolves the position-shift paradox, recovering the field-induced shift in an electron's position by integrating the semiclassical equations, and is directly related to the famous minimum conductivity of massless Dirac fermions.

</details>

### [32] [Unveiling Magnetic Frustration via the Elastocaloric Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15274)
*Eric C. Andrade,Pedro M. Cônsoli,Matthias Vojta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过分析受挫磁体在单轴应变下的热力学响应，计算了弹性Grüneisen比率η，发现Ising模型在最大受挫点附近η在低温下可任意增大，这是广延基态熵的普遍特征；而自旋-1/2 Heisenberg模型则表现出多个零温相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受到量子材料压力与应变调控实验进展的启发，研究受挫磁体对单轴应变的响应。

Method: 研究了空间各向异性三角晶格（以及Kagome晶格）上的Ising模型和Heisenberg模型，计算了作为温度与应变函数的熵，并据此计算弹性Grüneisen比率η。

Result: Ising模型可通过应变调谐进出经典自旋液体相，η在低温下靠近最大受挫点时变得任意大；自旋-1/2 Heisenberg模型中度受挫，呈现多个零温相变，低温下η受相变主导。

Conclusion: 讨论了弹性Grüneisen比率用于推断相图的程度，并将结果与近期三角晶格磁体实验相联系。

Abstract: Motivated by experimental progress in pressure and strain tuning of quantum materials, we examine the thermodynamic response of frustrated magnets to uniaxial strain. Specifically, we study Ising and Heisenberg models on spatially anisotropic triangular (and, for the Ising model, also kagome) lattices. We determine the entropy as a function of temperature and strain, and use it to compute the elastic Grüneisen ratio $η$. The Ising models can be strain-tuned into and out of classical spin-liquid phases, and we show that $η$ can become arbitrarily large at low temperature $T$ near the point of maximal frustration, a universal hallmark of an extensive ground-state entropy. In contrast, the spin-$1/2$ Heisenberg model is moderately frustrated and displays multiple $T=0$ phase transitions. These transitions dominate $η$ at low $T$ while the intermediate-$T$ behavior is similar to that of the Ising model. We discuss the extent to which the elastic Grüneisen ratio can be used to deduce the phase diagram, and we connect our results to recent experiments on triangular-lattice magnets.

</details>


### [33] [Itinerant antiferromagnetism in the antagonistic pair compound Y$_4$Co$_3$Ag](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15495)
*Rafaela F. S. Penacchio,Nao Furukawa,Joanna M. Blawat,John Singleton,Zhouqi Li,Raquel A. Ribeiro,Sérgio L. Morelhão,Sergey L. Bud'ko,Paul C. Canfield,Tyler J. Slade*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用互斥对（antagonistic pair）概念，在原本不互溶的Co-Ag体系中引入Y，成功合成出新化合物Y₄Co₃Ag。该化合物具有单斜I2/m结构，由Y通道以及沿b轴延伸的一维之字形和六角形Co链构成。输运、磁性和比热测量表明其在T_N=14.9 K发生反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）有序，但有效磁矩（μ_eff=1.4 μ_B/Co）和有序磁矩（<0.2 μ_B/Co）均较小，熵变仅约0.1 R ln2，暗示体系中存在巡游磁矩（itinerant moments）和强涨落（strong fluctuations），是研究准一维系统中巡游磁性相互作用的候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维晶体学构型（low dimensional crystallographic motifs）被认为能增强量子涨落并促进关联现象，但目前缺少在准一维体系中研究巡游磁性相互作用的合适材料。本研究旨在通过合理的化学设计，发现并表征一种新型准一维反铁磁化合物，以填补这一空白。

Method: 采用互斥对（antagonistic pair）策略，在互不溶的Co-Ag二元体系中引入第三种元素Y，合成出Y₄Co₃Ag化合物。通过结构解析确定其晶体学构型，并综合运用输运（transport）、磁化（magnetization）和比热（specific heat）测量，结合直流场（DC fields up to 70 kOe at 1.8 K）和脉冲场（pulsed fields up to 600 kOe at 500 mK）下的磁化等温线，对该化合物的磁性和热力学性质进行表征。

Result: Y₄Co₃Ag具有单斜I2/m结构，包含由Y原子构成的通道，通道内填充着一维之字形和六角形Co链，Co与Ag之间无最近邻接触。该化合物在T_N=14.9 K发生反铁磁有序，有效磁矩μ_eff=1.4 μ_B/Co，但比热测量显示磁有序伴随的熵损失仅为约0.1 R ln2，且有序磁矩小于0.2 μ_B/Co。

Conclusion: 综合结果表明，Y₄Co₃Ag中存在小且巡游的磁矩以及强涨落，表明该化合物可能是研究准一维系统（quasi-one dimensional system）中巡游磁性相互作用的候选材料。这一发现为低维巡游磁性系统的实验研究提供了新的平台。

Abstract: Low dimensional crystallographic motifs have long been associated with desirable physical properties. The confinement of electrons to low dimensions is thought to enhance quantum fluctuations and may promote correlated phenomena. Here, using the antagonistic pair concept, we add Y to the immiscible Co-Ag pair to discover Y$_4$Co$_3$Ag. This compound adopts a monoclinic $I$2/$m$ structure consisting of Y channels that are filled by one-dimensional zigzag and hexagonal Co chains, which extend along the crystallographic $b$-axis with no nearest neighbor contacts between Co and Ag atoms. Transport, magnetic, and specific heat measurements reveal that Y$_4$Co$_3$Ag orders antiferromagnetically at $T_N=14.9$ K with an effective magnetic moment $μ_{\text{eff}}$ = 1.4 $μ_{\text{B}}$/Co. Specific heat measurements show only a small entropy loss on the order of $0.1\,R\ln2$ associated with magnetic order, and magnetization isotherms, in DC fields up to 70 kOe at 1.8 K and in pulsed fields up to 600 kOe at 500 mK, indicate a small ordered moment of less than 0.2 $μ_B$/Co. Taken together, our results imply the presence of small, itinerant moments and strong fluctuations in Y$_4$Co$_3$Ag, suggesting that Y$_4$Co$_3$Ag may be a promising candidate material to investigate itinerant magnetic interactions in a quasi-one dimensional system.
