### [34] [Thermodynamic signatures of a field-induced ordered intermediate phase in Na$_2$Co$_2$TeO$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15829)
*Prashanta K. Mukarjee,Sebastian Erdmann,R. Kalaivanan,R. Sankar,Kwang-Yong Choi,Alexander A. Tsirlin,Philipp Gegenwart*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过磁化强度、比热和磁卡效应测量，对蜂窝状钴酸盐Na₂Co₂TeO₆的低温柔高温相图进行了全面热力学研究。在平面内磁场下识别出三个场致相变（Bc1≈6 T, Bc2≈7.8 T, Bc3≈10.4 T），发现中间相的行为不符合预期的场致量子自旋液体（QSL）特征，而是表现出有序态特征，对QSL场景提出了严格的热力学约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Na₂Co₂TeO₆近期被提出可能是一种承载场致量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）行为的候选材料。本研究旨在通过全面的热力学测量，精确刻画其低温柔高温相图，并检验QSL假说的有效性。

Method: 采用磁化强度（magnetization）、比热（specific heat）和磁卡效应（magnetocaloric effect）测量，在低至1 K的温度和高达数十特斯拉的磁场条件下，系统研究了Na₂Co₂TeO₆的热力学性质。

Result: 零场下观测到微弱的剩余磁矩；在面内磁场（B ∥ a*）下识别出三个场致相变（field-induced transitions），临界场分别为Bc1≈6 T、Bc2≈7.8 T和Bc3≈10.4 T。磁Grüneisen参数（magnetic Grüneisen parameter）和比热清晰地揭示了这些连续相变的热力学特征，其中包裹着两个中间相。Bc2至Bc3之间的相并未表现出增强的磁熵，而是与一个不同的有序态（ordered state）行为一致。Bc3以上未观察到额外异常，表明进入常规的自旋极化（spin-polarized）区间。

Conclusion: 研究结果对Na₂Co₂TeO₆中提出的场致QSL场景施加了严格的热力学约束，表明中间相更可能为有序态而非自旋液体，呼吁进一步的微观研究以确定场致相的确切性质。

Abstract: The honeycomb cobaltate Na$_2$Co$_2$TeO$_6$ has recently been proposed as a candidate material for hosting field-induced quantum spin liquid (QSL) behavior. Here, we present a comprehensive thermodynamic study of its low-temperature, high-field phase diagram using magnetization, specific heat, and magnetocaloric-effect measurements down to 1 K. In zero field, we observe a weak residual moment that provides further insight into the nature of the magnetic ground state. For in-plane magnetic fields ($B \parallel a^*$), we identify three field-induced transitions at $B_{c1} \simeq 6$ T, $B_{c2} \simeq 7.8$ T, and $B_{c3} \simeq 10.4$ T. The magnetic Grüneisen parameter and specific heat reveal clear thermodynamic signatures of these successive phase transitions enclosing two intermediate phases. Contrary to expectations for a field-induced QSL, the phase between $B_{c2}$ and $B_{c3}$ lacks enhanced magnetic entropy but instead shows behavior consistent with a distinct ordered state. Above $B_{c3}$, the absence of additional anomalies indicates a crossover to a conventional spin-polarized regime. Our results place stringent thermodynamic constraints on the proposed QSL scenario in Na$_2$Co$_2$TeO$_6$, calling for further microscopic investigations to establish the precise nature of the field-induced phases.

</details>


### [35] [Lieb-Schultz-Mattis constraints for hyperbolic lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15974)
*G. Shankar,Joseph Maciejko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文将Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）定理推广到双曲晶格（hyperbolic lattices）上的量子多体系统，利用双曲能带论（hyperbolic band theory）和Oshikawa的通量穿通论证（flux-threading argument），推导了基态简并度的下界，并探讨了对双曲空间中对称自旋液体（symmetric spin liquids）等有隙相的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的LSM定理及其高维推广仅限于欧几里得晶格（Euclidean lattices）上的量子多体系统，尚未推广到具有负曲率的双曲晶格；本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 借鉴多体框架下的双曲能带论（hyperbolic band theory），将Oshikawa的通量穿通论证（flux-threading argument）适应到具有非欧几里得（Fuchsian）平移对称性的周期性双曲晶格上，计算基态简并度（ground-state degeneracy）的下界。

Result: 推导出基态简并度作为填充数（filling）和晶格几何（lattice geometry）函数的严格下界，并指出双曲类比正方晶格和三角晶格的阻挫自旋模型（frustrated spin models）是实现双曲空间对称自旋液体的有前景平台。

Conclusion: LSM定理可推广到双曲晶格体系，为理解和约束双曲量子物质中的有隙相（gapped phases）提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: The Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) theorem and its higher-dimensional extensions forbid the existence of a unique, symmetric, and gapped ground state at fractional fillings in quantum many-body systems with a conserved particle number (or spin angular momentum) and the conventional translation symmetry of Euclidean lattices. In this work, we propose a generalization of the LSM theorem to quantum many-body systems on hyperbolic lattices, i.e., regular tessellations of two-dimensional negatively curved space. By leveraging concepts from hyperbolic band theory in a many-body setting, we adapt Oshikawa's flux-threading argument to periodic hyperbolic lattices with a non-Euclidean (Fuchsian) translation symmetry and compute a lower-bound to the ground-state degeneracy as a function of filling and lattice geometry. We explore the consequences of LSM constraints for gapped phases of hyperbolic quantum matter and suggest frustrated spin models on hyperbolic analogs of the square and triangular lattices as promising platforms for realizing symmetric spin liquids in hyperbolic space.

</details>


### [36] [Charge-sensitive vibrational modes in BEDT-TTF salts: Signatures of charge ordering and site charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16012)
*Savita Priya,Martin Dressel,Jesse Liebman,Natalia Drichko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究BEDT-TTF基有机导体中C=C伸缩振动模式，评估其用于确定电荷有序（charge ordering）和绝对位点电荷（absolute site charge）的可靠性。发现电荷-频率关系存在约20 cm⁻¹的分布展宽，导致电荷不确定性达Δρ≈±0.045e，表明该方法更适用于估计电荷有序而非绝对电荷值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BEDT-TTF基有机导体中存在多种基态（从Mott绝缘体、电荷有序绝缘体到超导体），了解绝缘态分子位点上的电荷分布是理解这些基态起源的关键，因此需要评估C=C伸缩振动模式在确定电荷有序和绝对位点电荷方面的可靠性。

Method: 综述并讨论BEDT-TTF基分子导体中的C=C伸缩振动模式，重点分析已知BEDT-TTF$^{+0.5}$盐实例，评估这些振动模式用于确定电荷有序和绝对位点电荷的可靠性。

Result: 对于电荷有序态，频率偏移分别为141 cm⁻¹/e（ν₂₇(b₁ᵤ)模式）和98 cm⁻¹/e（ν₂(a_g)模式），但不同化合物间的频率分布展宽超过20 cm⁻¹。名义BEDT-TTF$^{+0.5}$化合物的共振分布同样展宽约20 cm⁻¹，导致意外的较大电荷不确定性Δρ≈(±0.045)e，可能源于结构上的微小差异。

Conclusion: 电荷-频率关系在检测分子晶格位点上绝对电荷值的微小偏差方面存在局限性，应主要用于估计电荷有序而非绝对位点电荷。

Abstract: BEDT-TTF-based organic conductors host a number of ground states, tuned by electron repulsion from Mott and charge ordered insulators to superconductors. Knowing charge distribution on the molecular sites in the insulating state of these materials is a key to understanding the origin of these ground states. We survey and discuss the C=C stretching modes in BEDT-TTF based molecular conductors. These molecular vibrations are extremely crucial in characterization of charge-ordered insulators, and are recently linked to superconductivity in some compounds. Focusing on the known examples of BEDT-TTF$^{+0.5}$ salts, we analyse the reliability of the C=C stretching modes for the determination of charge ordering and absolute site charge. Considering the charge-ordered states, a prominent shift in frequency of 141 cm$^{-1}$ per elementary charge $e$ for $ν_{27}(b_{1u})$ and 98 cm$^{-1}$$e$ for $ν_2$($a_g$) can be clearly realised, however, the distribution resulting from different compounds span over 20 cm$^{-1}$. For nominal BEDT-TTF$^{+0.5}$ compounds, the distribution of the resonance also extends around 20 cm$^{-1}$, yielding an unexpected large uncertainty of $Δρ~\approx~(~\pm~0.045)e$, which is presumably due to the influence of small differences in the structure. This highlights the limitations of charge-frequency relations to detect small deviations in absolute charge values on molecular lattice sites, and emphasises on the use of the relations to estimate charge-ordering, rather than absolute site charge.

</details>


### [37] [Spherically symmetric approaches in the theoretical study of low-dimensional magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16059)
*A. F. Barabanov,V. E. Valiulin,A. V. Mikheyenkov,P. S. Savchenkov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维磁性系统的传统分析可能会遇到理论定理（Mermin-Wagner和Marshall定理）以及格点自旋约束（site spin constraint）带来的困难，因此需要开发一种能够妥善处理这些约束的方法。

Method: 采用球对称自洽方法（spherically symmetric self-consistent approach）及相关理论算法，在研究中严格考虑Mermin-Wagner定理、Marshall定理以及格点自旋约束。

Result: 该方法成功避免了低维海森堡型自旋模型（包括阻挫系统）传统分析中可能出现的困难，并可推广至自旋-赝自旋模型，以及包含自由载流子的更复杂模型体系。

Conclusion: 球对称自洽方法为低维自旋系统的研究提供了一种鲁棒的理论框架，能够系统性地处理理论约束和模型扩展需求。

Abstract: The main ideas and some of the most important results of the spherically symmetric self-consistent approach and a number of related theoretical algorithms are presented. These methods make it possible to study low-dimensional Heisenberg-type spin models, including frustrated ones, with careful consideration of the theoretic (Mermin-Wagner and Marshall) theorems, as well as the site spin constraint. Thus, the difficulties that may arise in the traditional analysis of low-dimensional magnetic systems are avoided. The approach can also be applied to the spin-pseudospin model, and is also embedded in more complex constructions when considering spin models with free carriers, such as the basic and three-band Hubbard models, t-J and s-d models, and the Kondo lattice.

</details>


### [38] [Lattice Relaxation Flattens Chern Bands in Rhombohedral Graphene Stacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16218)
*Luca Nashabeh,Héctor Ochoa*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出并研究了一个模型，其中菱方石墨烯/六方氮化硼异质结中的莫尔势由层间剪切应变场定义。研究发现，晶格弛豫（lattice relaxation）在形成具有陈数|C|=1的谷极化哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）电子能带中起关键作用，挑战了传统莫尔效应观念，并揭示了长程库仑相互作用与晶格弛豫的耦合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期在菱方石墨烯（rhombohedral graphene）堆叠与六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）对齐结构中观测到整数和分数量子反常霍尔效应（Chern insulators）的实验启发，本文旨在澄清这类异质结中莫尔势（moiré potential）的物理起源，并研究晶格弛豫（lattice relaxation）对拓扑电子态的影响。

Method: 作者提出一个理论模型，将莫尔势定义为由晶格弛豫产生的层间剪切应变场（layer-shear strain fields）图案。通过考虑电子相互作用，采用哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）近似分析单电子能带结构和相互作用效应，特别关注远离接触层的“莫尔远区”（moiré-distant regime）行为。

Result: 尽管剪切应变场随层数呈指数衰减，但对远离接触层的电子仍有不可忽略的影响。在无位移场时，晶格弛豫放大了两种hBN堆叠的电子差异，该差异在莫尔远区仍然存在，并在引入电子相互作用后进一步增强。晶格弛豫在形成具有|C|=1陈数（Chern number）的谷极化（valley-polarized）平带（flat band）中起关键作用。

Conclusion: 该结果挑战了关于菱方石墨烯/hBN异质结中莫尔效应的传统观念，揭示了长程库仑相互作用与晶格弛豫的耦合机制，为通过调控扭转角（twist angle）和位移场（displacement field）探索不同参数区域以寻找拓扑态（topological states）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Motivated by recent observations of integer and fractional Chern insulators in rhombohedral graphene stacks aligned with hexagonal boron nitride (hBN), we propose and study a model in which the moiré potential is defined by the pattern of layer-shear strain fields produced by lattice relaxation in these heterostructures. Although these strain fields decrease exponentially with the number of layers, their imprints on electrons residing away from the contact layer are non-negligible. In the absence of a displacement field, lattice relaxation effects amplify the electronic differences among the two different stackings with hBN. These differences, although attenuated at the single-electron level, survive in the so-called moiré-distant regime and are further enhanced with the inclusion of electron interactions. We find that lattice relaxation plays a crucial role in flattening and isolating a valley-polarized Hartree-Fock electron band with $|C|=1$ Chern number. Our results challenge the conventional wisdom on moiré effects in these heterostructures by illustrating the intertwined effects of long-range Coulomb interactions and lattice relaxation, and opens the door to explore different regimes of twist angles and displacement fields for the search for topological states.

</details>

Abstract: For neutrino physics and rare event searches, background related to cosmic muons poses a notable challenge, and must be identified and rejected. We proposed a cosmic ray detection module with liquid scintillator and wavelength-shifting fibers for its reasonable cost and performances. The outcomes of this study hold significant potential for applications in cosmic ray observation experiments and underground rare-event detection, providing a viable option for future large-scale observatories. This work highlights the feasibility of liquid scintillator-based detectors in addressing current and emerging challenges in particle physics and astrophysics.

### [40] [Active Model B$^-$ from Mass-Conserving Reaction-Diffusion Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15903)
*Davide Toffenetti,Beatrice Nettuno,Henrik Weyer,Erwin Frey*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发现最小三组分质量守恒反应-扩散系统（three-component mass-conserving reaction–diffusion system）的晚期动力学可约化为标量主动场论——主动模型 B⁻（Active Model B⁻, AMB⁻），其中密度依赖的界面系数 κ(φ) 在高密度时变负，导致有限波长不稳定性（finite-wavelength instability）并稳定微相分离图案（microphase-separated patterns），与两组分系统的无界粗化行为形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多组分质量守恒反应-扩散系统在晚期动力学中是否能够产生与经典两组分系统不同的有序结构，特别是微相分离图案的稳定机制。

Method: 通过理论推导，将最小三组分质量守恒反应-扩散系统的晚期动力学约化为标量主动场论形式，即主动模型 B⁻（AMB⁻），并分析其中密度依赖的界面系数 κ(φ) 的符号变化对系统稳定性的影响。

Result: AMB⁻ 中密度依赖的界面系数 κ(φ) 在高密度时变负，驱动有限波长不稳定性，从而稳定微相分离图案，而非如两组分系统那样发生无界粗化（unbounded coarsening）。

Conclusion: 与主动模型 B⁺（Active Model B⁺）不同，AMB⁻ 保留了作为状态函数的化学势（chemical potential），该化学势继承自底层守恒律，但不存在关于压力的状态方程（equation of state）。

Abstract: We show that the late-time dynamics of a minimal three-component mass-conserving reaction--diffusion system reduce to a scalar active field theory, Active Model B$^-$ (AMB$^-$), in which a density-dependent interfacial coefficient $κ(φ)$ turns negative at high density. This drives a finite-wavelength instability and stabilises microphase-separated patterns, in contrast to the unbounded coarsening of two-component mass-conserving systems. Unlike Active Model B$^+$, AMB$^-$ retains a chemical potential that remains a state function, inherited from the underlying conservation law, but admits no equation of state for the pressure.

</details>


### [41] [Actin cross-linking organizes basal body patterning through anomalous diffusion transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15912)
*Raghavan Thiagarajan,Younes Farhangi Barooji,Poul-Martin Bendix,Mandar M. Inamdar,Jakub Sedzinski*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究结合定量成像与理论建模，揭示了多纤毛细胞（MCCs）中基体（BBs）从扩散运动到受限运动的动态转变，并证明顶端肌动蛋白（actin）网络的渐进式交联（cross-linking）是驱动这一转变、实现基体均匀空间排布及纤毛定向排列的关键机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚细胞蛋白复合物和细胞器表现出异常动力学（anomalous dynamics），但不同运动模式之间的转变如何影响亚细胞空间模式（pattern formation）尚不清楚。本研究旨在阐明扩散与异常运动状态的转变在细胞结构组织中的具体作用。

Method: 使用定量共聚焦（confocal）、高分辨率及高速全内反射荧光（TIRF）成像，结合理论建模，追踪非洲爪蟾（Xenopus laevis）胚胎多纤毛细胞（multiciliated cells, MCCs）顶端表面基体（basal bodies, BBs）的轨迹。

Result: 基体轨迹在时间上呈现扩散运动与异常运动之间的转变，且不同运动模式与顶端表面扩张阶段相关。早期肌动蛋白重塑提供低限制环境促进基体散布；后期肌动蛋白网络交联增强，限制了基体运动并促进均匀间距。破坏α-辅肌动蛋白-1（α-actinin-1）会削弱顶端肌动蛋白网格完整性、减弱基体限制并破坏空间排布。

Conclusion: 渐进式顶端肌动蛋白交联协调基体定位并调控其动态状态，引导从扩散运动到受限运动的转变。这一动力学转变使得均匀的基体模式得以形成，进而确保运动纤毛的定向排列，为有效的定向流体流动提供必要条件。

Abstract: Subcellular protein complexes and organelles exhibit diverse dynamic behaviors that reflect the mechanical constraints and organization of the intracellular environment. Although some structures follow classical Brownian motion, many display anomalous dynamics. The transitions between these regimes are increasingly recognized as critical for subcellular organization, yet how they influence pattern formation remains unclear. Here, we investigate the spatial arrangement of cilia on the apical surface of multiciliated cells (MCCs) in developing Xenopus laevis embryos, where coordinated ciliary beating depends on the precise organization of hundreds of centriole-derived basal bodies (BBs). Using quantitative confocal, high-resolution and high-speed TIRF imaging together with theoretical modeling, we show that BB trajectories undergo time-resolved transitions between diffusive and anomalous motion, with distinct regimes that correlate with apical surface expansion. During the early stages, actin remodeling facilitates the dispersal of BBs by providing a permissive, low-confinement environment. As development progresses, the actin network becomes increasingly cross-linked that constrains BB movement and promotes uniform spacing across the apical domain. Disruption of $α$-actinin-1, a major actin cross-linking protein, impairs the integrity of the apical actin meshwork, weakens BB confinement, and disrupts regular spatial patterning, ultimately compromising the arrangement of BBs required for proper cilia alignment. Together, we show that progressive apical actin cross-linking coordinates BB positioning and regulates their dynamic state, guiding the shift from diffusive to confined motion. This transition in dynamics enables the emergence of a uniform BB pattern, which in turn ensures the aligned deployment of motile cilia necessary for effective directional fluid flow.

</details>


### [42] [Biophysical Considerations for Rational Antibody and ADC Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16070)
*Alberto Ocana,Jorge R. Espinosa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文论证了计算生物物理学（computational biophysics）可作为连接抗体药物分子相互作用与生物学结果的关键框架，指出整合分子动力学、粗粒化模拟和自由能计算等方法，能够揭示缀合位点、连接子化学和药物-抗体比率（drug-antibody ratio）对构象景观（conformational landscapes）的影响，从而减少经验性迭代并降低转化风险，有望成为下一代抗体药物偶联物（ADC）设计的核心驱动力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于抗体的治疗药物（包括抗体药物偶联物、双特异性抗体及新型格式）正重塑肿瘤学领域，但其疗效、安全性和可制造性的关键决定因素往往在缀合（conjugation）和制剂（formulation）之后才显现。现有流程存在显著的滞后性，缺乏从分子层面提前预测和优化这些性质的手段。

Method: 本文提出利用计算生物物理学框架，具体通过分子动力学（molecular dynamics）、粗粒化模拟（coarse-grained simulations）和自由能计算（free energy calculations）等方法，分析缀合位点、连接子（linker）化学性质和药物-抗体比率如何重塑抗体-连接子-载荷系统的构象景观，并考察三者之间的结构耦合（structural coupling）。

Result: 计算模拟揭示出缀合位点、连接子化学和药物-抗体比率对构象景观的显著影响，以及抗体、连接子和载荷之间的结构耦合，这些特征与抗原结合（antigen binding）、内化（internalization）和可开发性（developability）密切相关。

Conclusion: 将基于物理学的建模整合到开发流程中，并辅以实验验证，可减少经验性迭代并降低转化风险。随着力场（force fields）和混合物理-机器学习（hybrid physics-machine learning）方法的进步，该领域有望成为下一代ADC设计的核心驱动力。

Abstract: Antibody-based therapeutics-including antibody-drug conjugates (ADCs), bispecific antibodies, and novel formats-are reshaping oncology, yet key determinants of efficacy, safety, and manufacturability frequently emerge after conjugation and formulation. We argue that computational biophysics provides an underexploited framework to address this gap by connecting molecular interactions to biological outcomes. We highlight how molecular dynamics, coarse-grained simulations, and free energy calculations reveal how conjugation site, linker chemistry, and drug-antibody ratio reshape conformational landscapes. We emphasize structural coupling between antibody, linker, and payload, with implications for antigen binding, internalization, and developability. We propose that integrating physics-based modeling into development pipelines-alongside experimental validation-can reduce empirical iteration and de-risk translation. As force fields, and hybrid physics-machine-learning methods improve, this field is poised to become a central driver of next-generation ADC design.

### [43] [Observation of flat-bottom U-shaped energy gap in high-Tc nickelate (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15703)
*Zhen Liang,Tianheng Wei,Wei Ren,Haoran Ji,Zheyuan Xie,Yanzhao Liu,Ziqiang Wang,Jian Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用超低温扫描隧道显微镜/光谱学（STM/S）和电输运测量，首次在常压环境下生长的Ruddlesden-Popper双层镍氧化物薄膜(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇中观测到能量对称的平底U形超导能隙，该能隙在升温时迅速填充为V形，在14T磁场下被抑制，表明存在无节点（nodeless）的超导能隙函数，为理解高温超导机制提供了新线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压下Ruddlesden-Popper（R-P）双层镍氧化物中发现高温超导（high-Tc superconductivity）后，迫切需要理解其超导机制并寻求更高Tc的超导体；近期常压环境下R-P双层镍氧化物薄膜超导的实现（起始Tc>40K），使得利用多种实验工具研究非常规高温超导成为可能。

Method: 采用超低温扫描隧道显微镜/光谱学（ultra-low temperature scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy, STM/S）结合电输运测量（electrical transport study），对生长在SrLaAlO₄衬底上的(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇薄膜进行同一样品的原位表征。

Result: 首次观测到能量对称的平底U形能隙（energy-symmetric, flat-bottom U-shaped gap），费米能级（Fermi level）处剩余态密度为零；同一样品输运测量显示起始Tc>40K、零电阻Tc>20K；该U形能隙随温度升高迅速填充为V形能隙（V-shaped gap），且在14T c轴磁场下被抑制。

Conclusion: 能量对称的U形能隙及其对磁场和温度的依赖关系与超导能隙行为一致，表明超低温下存在无节点能隙函数（nodeless gap function）；该发现为理解高温超导本质提供了新视角，并为在常压或零压下实现液氮沸点以上Tc的镍氧化物超导给出了有希望的启示。

Abstract: The discovery of high transition temperature (high-Tc) superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper (R-P) bilayer nickelates under high pressure has stimulated extensive work to understand the underlying mechanism and search for superconductors with higher Tc. The recent realization of superconductivity in R-P bilayer nickelate thin films with onset Tc above 40 K at ambient-pressure enables the use of a wide array of powerful experimental tools to investigate the unconventional high-Tc superconductivity in bilayer nickelates. Here, using ultra-low temperature scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy (STM/S) and electrical transport study, we report the first successful observation of an energy-symmetric, flat-bottom U-shaped gap with zero residual density of states around the Fermi level in the high-Tc nickelate (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 thin film grown on SrLaAlO4 substrate. Before and after STM/S studies, transport measurements on the same sample reveal consistent superconducting behaviors showing zero resistance, with an onset Tc above 40 K and zero resistance Tc above 20 K. The tunneling spectra exhibit highly unconventional temperature evolution, characterized by a rapid filling of the U-shaped energy gap to a V-shaped gap as the temperature increases. Furthermore, the U-shaped energy gap is reduced under a c-axis magnetic field of 14 T. The energy-symmetric U-shaped gap, taken together with its dependence on magnetic field and temperature, is consistent with the behavior of a superconducting gap, suggesting a nodeless gap function at ultra-low temperatures. Our findings shed new lights on the nature of high-Tc superconductivity and provide an encouraging and thought-provoking hint for a local superconductivity with Tc above liquid nitrogen boiling temperature in nickelate superconductors at ambient or zero pressure.

### [44] [Equidistant resonance jumps in superconducting coplanar resonators driven by Abrikosov vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15751)
*Dmitrii S. Kalashnikov,Denis Yu. Vodolazov,Ruslan I. Kinzibaev,Andrei G. Shishkin,Vasily S. Stolyarov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究铌四分之一波长共面谐振器在垂直磁场（18 mK–5 K，最高40 Oe）下的传输参数 S₂₁，观察到可逆Meissner区之外的阶梯状跳跃现象，并将其归因于多涡旋（vortex）的进入与退出事件，同时发现谐振频率和内部品质因子的非比例响应揭示了涡旋与反涡旋（antivortex）构型的复杂贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导共面谐振器（superconducting coplanar resonator）是低温微波电路的关键组件，但其在垂直磁场下的性能最终受到阿布里科索夫涡旋（Abrikosov vortex）的限制。本文旨在实验探究该限制的具体表现与机制。

Method: 实验测量了铌（niobium）四分之一波长共面谐振器的传输参数 S₂₁ 随垂直磁场（0–40 Oe）和温度（18 mK–5 K）的变化，通过分析磁场扫掠过程中谐振峰的阶梯状跳跃行为及反向扫掠时的准等距序列，并结合理论估算进行解释。

Result: 在可逆Meissner区之外，谐振峰出现随磁场的突变式阶梯跳跃；反向扫掠时跳跃间距约为1.7–1.8 Oe，呈准等距分布。谐振频率与内部品质因子的响应不成比例，表明存在涡旋与反涡旋构型的复杂贡献。

Conclusion: 阶梯跳跃现象被解释为多涡旋进入与退出事件的信号，与理论估算一致。实验结果有望推动对大型涡旋-反涡旋系统（vortex-antivortex system）的进一步研究，尤其是对其离散性质的明确考虑。

Abstract: Superconducting coplanar resonators are key building blocks of cryogenic microwave circuits, yet their performance in perpendicular magnetic fields is ultimately limited by Abrikosov vortices. In this work we investigate the dependence of the transmission parameter $S_{21}$ of niobium quarter-wave coplanar resonators on perpendicular magnetic fields up to 40 Oe and at temperatures between 18 mK and 5 K. Beyond the reversible Meissner regime, the entire resonance peak exhibits abrupt, staircase-like jumps as a function of magnetic field. Upon reversal of the field sweep, these jumps form an almost equidistant series with spacing 1.7-1.8 Oe, which, in agreement with theoretical estimates, we interpret as signatures of multiple-vortex entry and exit events. Additionally, we observe the non-proportional responses of the resonant frequency and the internal quality factor that indicate a complex contribution of vortex and antivortex configurations. We believe that our results will stimulate further studies of large vortex-antivortex systems, explicitly accounting for their discrete nature.

</details>


### [45] [Effective increase of a superconducting critical temperature in a high-entropy electron mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15834)
*Viktoriia Kornich*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 理论研究表明，通过利用导带与价带电子形成的高熵混合，并借助金属陷阱移除准粒子激发，可使库珀对浓度成为混合熵的动态变量，从而有效提高超导临界温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索能否通过在高熵混合（high-entropy mixture）的电子体系中引入混合熵（entropy of mixing）来提升超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature, Tc）。

Method: 提出使用一个金属陷阱（metallic trap）从超导体中移除准粒子激发（quasiparticle excitations），使库珀对（Cooper pair）的浓度成为混合熵的动态变量，进而修改金茨堡-朗道泛函（Ginzburg-Landau functional）以降低其第一展开系数。

Result: 该方法能有效增加超导临界温度。

Conclusion: 通过金属陷阱将准粒子从超导体中移除，可使混合熵参与到超导相动力学（superconducting phase dynamics）中，从而提升临界温度。

Abstract: We show theoretically that a superconducting critical temperature can be effectively increased in a high-entropy mixture of electrons belonging to conduction and valence bands. In order to employ the entropy of mixing into the superconducting phase dynamics, we suggest to use a metallic trap that removes quasiparticle excitations from the superconductor. This makes the concentration of Cooper pairs a dynamic variable of the entropy of mixing, and thus affects the Ginzburg-Landau functional of the superconductor effectively reducing the first expansion coefficient or, in other words, increasing the critical temperature.

</details>

### [46] [Quantum game theory for 2 2 games: a mathematical framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15747)
*Gloria Ferraris,Veronica Umanità*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为量子博弈论（quantum game theory）中的静态2x2博弈建立了严格的数学框架，通过不动点论证证明了连续量子混合策略下纳什均衡（Nash equilibrium）的存在性，将经典纳什定理推广至量子情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典博弈论中的纳什均衡存在性定理在量子博弈（quantum game）中尚未得到严格推广，现有研究缺乏对连续纯量策略空间（SU(2)群上的概率测度）下均衡存在的数学证明。

Method: 采用Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein（EWL）协议作为量子2x2博弈的标准实现框架，将经典策略空间扩展至酉操作（unitary operation）构成的连续群SU(2)，并利用概率测度（probability measure）定义混合策略（mixed strategy），通过不动点（fixed-point）论证证明纳什均衡的存在性。

Result: 证明了当玩家可选用连续量子混合策略（即SU(2)群上的概率测度）时，量子2x2博弈中纳什均衡必然存在。

Conclusion: 该结果将经典纳什定理（classical Nash theorem）完整地推广至量子博弈（quantum game）领域，为量子博弈论的数学基础提供了严格的形式化支撑。

Abstract: We develop a rigorous mathematical framework for quantum game theory applied to static 2x2 games, extending classical concepts to the quantum setting where players may employ arbitrary unitary operations (pure strategies) or probability measures over the continuous group SU(2) (mixed strategies). The Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein protocol is introduced as the standard implementation of quantum 2x2 games. We prove the existence of Nash equilibria for continuous quantum mixed strategies via a fixed-point argument, generalising the classical Nash theorem to the quantum case.

### [47] [Fast convergence of Dynamic Capacities of GNS-Symmetric Quantum Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15953)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对GNS-对称信道（GNS-symmetric channel）这一特定类别（涵盖Pauli信道等），利用熵性质（entropic properties）推导经典容量（classical capacity）与量子容量（quantum capacity）的指数收敛界（exponential convergence bounds）。

Result: 给出了GNS-对称信道下经典容量和量子容量的显式指数收敛界，并说明这些结果可用于量化主动纠错（active error correction）与被动纠错（passive error correction）方案的性能。

Conclusion: 所提指数收敛界为量子信道容量随时间演化的行为提供了理论刻画，并为主动与被动纠错两种策略的性能比较提供了定量分析框架。

Abstract: We consider a quantum system described by a quantum channel $Φ$ that is applied at every time step and study the time evolution of its information capacities. When $Φ$ is a GNS-symmetric channel (this includes Pauli channels, for example), we give explicit exponential convergence bounds for the classical and quantum capacities. These bounds are in terms of entropic properties of $Φ$. We further illustrate how these results help quantify the performance of active versus passive error-correction setups.

### [48] [Coherent States of Non-Null Torus Knots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15420)
*Gabriel Canadas da Silva,Ion Vasile Vancea*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了对应于真空中麦克斯韦方程经典非零环面纽结解（torus knot solutions）的量子化电磁场相干态（coherent states），通过位移算符（displacement operators）建立经典场与相干态振幅的关系，并在Hopfion相干态特例中计算了多种可观测量（observables）的期望值，确立了这类真空拓扑电磁系统的量子-经典对应（quantum-classical correspondence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典真空电磁场中的环面纽结拓扑解（如Hopfion）推广到量子化电磁场，建立对应的相干态描述，从而探索拓扑电磁系统在量子层面的性质。

Method: 从经典场与相干态振幅的一般关系推导位移算符；通过直接计算验证相干态的定义性质；将可观测量的期望值表达为经典解整数参数$(n,m,l,s)$的函数。

Result: 成功构造了对应于经典环面纽结解的量子相干态，推导了位移算符，计算了场期望值、能量密度、Poynting矢量（Poynting vector）、螺旋性（helicity）、光子数、正交分量不确定度（quadrature uncertainties）及相关函数（correlation functions）的期望值，并以Hopfion相干态为例展示了具体构造。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了这类真空拓扑电磁系统的量子-经典对应关系，为拓扑电磁场结构的量子化研究提供了基础。

Abstract: We construct coherent states for the quantized electromagnetic field that correspond to the classical non-null torus knot solutions of Maxwell's equations in vacuum. We derive the displacement operators from the general relation between classical fields and coherent state amplitudes and verify the defining properties of coherent states through direct computation. We determine the observables of the model: field expectation values, energy density, Poynting vector, helicity, photon number, quadrature uncertainties, and correlation functions, and calculate their expectation values in the knotted coherent states in terms of the integer parameters $(n,m,l,s)$ of the classical solutions. As an example, we particularize the construction in the case of the Hopfion coherent state. These results establish the quantum-classical correspondence for this type of vacuum topological electromagnetic systems.

### [49] [A reason why we do not observe Schrödinger's cats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16148)
*Fabio Siringo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个可能的原因，解释为何真实世界中不存在宏观态的叠加：在量子宏观态是微观态统计系综的假设下，普通薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）能在极短时间内约化任何宏观态叠加，并推导出玻恩规则（Born rule），而无需将其作为公设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释现实世界为何观测不到宏观态叠加这一量子力学基本问题，并试图在不引入额外公设的前提下，从量子力学内部解决测量问题（measurement problem）。

Method: 将宏观态视为微观态的统计系综，在薛定谔方程中解耦宏观与微观自由度，得到宏观变量的有效随机方程（effective stochastic equation），其中微观振幅的系综平均充当自生内部白噪声（self-generated internal white noise）。

Result: 在满足一般因果条件时，该随机方程被证明是约化伊藤方程（reducing Itô equation），预测任何宏观叠加在形成后都会极快坍缩，坍缩概率满足玻恩规则。

Conclusion: 在冯·诺伊曼测量方案（von Neumann measurement scheme）框架下，该结果为测量问题提供了一种简单的动力学解法。

Abstract: A reason is discussed (may be not the only one) for why we do not see any superposition of macroscopic states in the real world. Under the general assumption that quantum macrostates are statistical ensembles of microstates, it is shown that any superposition of macrostates is reduced in a very short time by the unitary dynamics of the ordinary Schrödinger equation, deducing the Born rule without having to postulate it. In more detail, the macroscopic and microscopic degrees of freedom are decoupled in the Schrödinger equation, yielding an effective stochastic equation for the macroscopic variables, with the ensemble average of the microscopic amplitudes that acts as a self-generated internal white noise. The stochastic equation is shown to be a reducing Itô equation if some general causality conditions are met, predicting a very quick collapse of any macroscopic superposition upon formation, with probabilities which satisfy the Born rule. In the context of the von Neumann measurement scheme, the relevance of the result is discussed as a simple dynamical solution of the measurement problem.

</details>


### [50] [Interface Piezoelectric Loss in Superconducting Qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15554)
*Haoxin Zhou,Kangdi Yu,Yashwanth Balaji,Sanjit Shirol,Leo Sementilli,Zi-Huai Zhang,Adam Schwartzberg,Alp Sipahigil*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验观测到超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）中由界面压电效应（interface piezoelectricity）引起的能量耗散，证实了界面压电性是一个独立的损耗通道，并在高频条件下可能超过双能级系统（two-level systems）引起的损耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耗散（dissipation）是提升超导量子电路性能的主要障碍，但常用材料平台中损耗的微观起源尚未被完全理解。该研究旨在揭示界面压电性是否为一种此前未被充分认识的重要损耗机制。

Method: 在超高阻硅（high-resistivity silicon）上制备transmon量子比特，其并联电容器同时作为嵌入声表面波谐振器（surface acoustic wave resonator）中的叉指换能器（interdigital transducer）。通过将量子比特跃迁频率调谐至与离散机械模式共振，测量量子比特寿命的衰减。

Result: 当量子比特与机械模式共振时，量子比特寿命（qubit lifetime）下降多达两倍，表明量子比特与机械模式之间通过铝-硅界面处的压电耦合发生能量交换。结合多物理场仿真（multiphysics simulations），发现界面压电损耗在高频条件下可超过双能级系统引起的损耗。

Conclusion: 该研究为界面压电性作为超导量子比特中一个独立的损耗通道提供了直接实验证据。这一发现有助于更深入地理解超导量子电路的耗散机制，并为未来优化器件设计以减少损耗提供了方向。

Abstract: Dissipation remains a central obstacle to improving superconducting quantum circuits, yet the microscopic origins of loss in widely used materials platforms are not fully understood. Here, we report the observation of interface piezoelectricity-induced dissipation in superconducting qubits fabricated on high-resistivity silicon. Our devices use a transmon qubit with a shunt capacitor that simultaneously serves as an interdigital transducer embedded in a surface acoustic wave resonator. By tuning the qubit transition into resonance with discrete mechanical modes, we observe up to a factor-of-two reduction in qubit lifetime, consistent with energy exchange between the qubit and mechanical modes mediated by piezoelectric coupling at the aluminum-silicon interface. Our findings provide direct evidence for interface piezoelectricity as a distinct loss channel in superconducting qubits. Combined with multiphysics simulations, these findings suggest that interface piezoelectric loss can dominate over loss from two-level systems at sufficiently high frequencies.

</details>


### [51] [Dynamical aspects of steady-state subradiance: Detailed balance and its breakdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15785)
*Athreya Shankar,Simon B. Jäger,Jarrod T. Reilly,Raphael Kaubruegger,Murray J. Holland,Walter Hahn*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究耗散多体量子系统（dissipative many-body quantum systems）中出现的马尔可夫链（Markov chain）经典描述，重点分析坏腔激光器（bad-cavity laser）中亚辐射（subradiant）区域发生的耗散相变（dissipative phase transition）与马尔可夫链性质之间的联系。研究发现，在一种相中马尔可夫链趋近细致平衡（detailed-balance）并变得时间可逆，而在另一相中出现时间不对称的概率流（probability currents）和宏观内熵产生率（internal entropy production rate），并导致腔光输出自脉动（self-pulsing）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耗散多体量子系统的动力学有时可被马尔可夫链经典描述，但系统状态空间包含高度纠缠态（highly entangled states），理解这种经典描述的涌现机制及其与量子相变的关系是一个重要的理论问题。

Method: 以坏腔激光器为范例系统，将其动力学表述为由集体角动量态（collective angular momentum states）张成的二维状态空间上的马尔可夫链，并研究在大原子数极限下亚辐射区域中耗散相变与马尔可夫链性质之间的关联。

Result: 在一种相中，随原子数N增大，马尔可夫链趋近细致平衡，变得有效时间可逆，这是由集体原子发射过程将链降至一维所致；在另一相中，二维状态空间出现时间不对称的概率流，标志细致平衡被破坏，伴随宏观内熵产生率随N呈广延标度（extensive scaling），并可观测到腔光输出的自脉动现象。

Conclusion: 耗散多体量子系统的相变与底层马尔可夫链的时间可逆性/不可逆性转变密切相关，概率流和内熵产生可作为相变可观测的实验特征。

Abstract: The dynamics of dissipative many-body quantum systems sometimes admit an emergent classical description in terms of a Markov chain even though the corresponding state space contains highly entangled states. In particular, a bad-cavity laser is a paradigm system whose dynamics can be formulated as a Markov chain in a two-dimensional state space spanned by collective angular momentum states. In this article, we investigate the connection between a dissipative phase transition that occurs in the subradiant regime of this system in the large atom number limit, and the properties of the underlying Markov chain. In one of the phases, the Markov chain approaches the detailed-balance condition with increasing atom number $N$ and hence becomes effectively time-reversible. This is caused by a collective atomic emission process that effectively reduces the Markov chain to one dimension. In the other phase, we find the emergence of time-asymmetric probability currents in the two-dimensional state space that signals a breakdown of detailed balance. This is accompanied by a macroscopic internal entropy production rate in the Markov chain that scales extensively with the atom number $N$. An observable consequence of the probability currents is a self-pulsing of the cavity light output in this phase, which can be detected as an anti-correlation dip in the intensity correlation function.

</details>


### [52] [Quantum mechanics for classical transport equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15969)
*Christof Wetterich*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，带有概率初始条件的经典输运方程在离散形式下可等价于概率自动机，其时间局域概率信息由经典波函数编码，并满足薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的幺正演化（unitary evolution）。量子力学（quantum mechanics）的标志性特征——如波函数叠加、干涉、相位重要性、非对易算符（non-commuting operators）及幺正时间演化——均可由经典概率输运方程实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立经典概率输运方程（classical transport equations）与量子系统之间的形式等价性，揭示量子力学的基本特征实际上可由概率性经典动力学自然实现，从而弥合经典统计与量子理论之间的概念鸿沟。

Method: 将离散版本的经典输运方程视为概率自动机（probabilistic automata），通过引入经典波函数（classical wave function）编码时间局域概率信息，使其满足薛定谔方程形式的幺正演化。此外，为该量子系统构造了一个复泛函积分（complex functional integral），用以描述经典概率输运方程。

Result: 经典输运方程在概率初始条件下能够完整复现量子力学的核心特征：波函数叠加、干涉效应、相位的重要性、非对易算符（如统计可观测量与经典可观测量对应的算符不对易），以及幺正时间演化。量子能量函数或量子角动量函数等守恒量可表示为与经典可观测量不对易的算符。

Conclusion: 量子力学并非必须依赖特定的物理系统（如微观粒子），而是可以由概率性经典输运方程在数学形式上自然实现。这表明量子现象的概率结构可能比通常认为的更具普遍性，为理解经典与量子理论之间的关系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Classical transport equations with probabilistic initial conditions can be viewed as quantum systems.
  In a discrete version they are probabilistic automata. The time-local probabilistic information is encoded in a classical wave function.
  Its unitary evolution obeys a Schrödinger equation.
  Statistical observables are represented by operators which do not commute with the ones associated to classical observables.
  Examples are functions of the quantum energy or the quantum angular momentum. They are important conserved quantities.
  We construct a complex functional integral for the quantum system which describes the probabilistic classical transport equation.
  The characteristic features of quantum mechanics, as the superposition of wave functions, interference, the importance of phases,
  non-commuting operators or a unitary time evolution, are realized by probabilistic classical transport equations.

</details>


### [53] [Thermodynamic Networks: Harnessing Non-Equilibrium Steady States for Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15985)
*Patryk Lipka-Bartosik,Gianmichele Blasi,Javier Lalueza Puértolas,Géraldine Haack,Martí Perarnau-Llobet,Nicolas Brunner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出热力学网络（thermodynamic networks）框架，利用非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady states）实现自主的、基于物理的计算。负微分电导（Negative Differential Conductance, NDC）被识别为决定网络计算表达能力的关键物理性质：缺乏NDC的网络只能计算单调函数，而具备NDC的网络则能实现通用函数逼近。基于量子点网络和酶反应网络两种平台的实验验证了该方法在标准基准测试中的高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算范式多依赖传统电子硬件，而利用非平衡物理系统直接进行计算的理论框架尚不完善。本文旨在建立非平衡稳态与计算表达能力之间的严格理论联系，并识别出决定计算能力的核心物理属性。

Method: 将计算系统建模为一组有限尺寸的储能节点（reservoirs），这些节点在交换守恒量（如电荷或分子数）的过程中弛豫至非平衡稳态，该稳态编码了计算问题的解。利用系统自然趋向平衡的特性设计训练协议。

Result: 识别出负微分电导（NDC）是决定热力学网络计算表达能力的关键物理性质：无NDC的网络局限于计算单调函数，而含NDC的网络可实现通用函数逼近。在量子点网络和酶反应网络两种平台上，通过工程化引入NDC，网络在正弦函数逼近和MNIST手写数字分类等标准基准测试中取得了高性能。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了非平衡稳态与计算表达能力之间的严格联系，为基于物理的自主计算提供了通用框架，并指明了NDC作为关键设计原则在物理计算系统中的应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce thermodynamic networks, a general framework for autonomous, physics-based computation using non-equilibrium steady states. These networks are modeled as a collection of finite-size reservoirs that exchange conserved quantities--such as electric charge or molecular number--while relaxing to a non-equilibrium steady state, which encodes the solution of a computational problem. We identify Negative Differential Conductance (NDC) as the critical physical property governing the computational expressivity of the thermodynamic network. While networks lacking NDC are restricted to computing monotonic functions, the presence of NDC enables universal function approximation. For the training of the network, we use protocols that take advantage of the natural tendency of the system to equilibrate. We illustrate the versatility of our approach via two different platforms: quantum dot networks and enzymatic reaction networks. Both systems can be engineered to have NDC, enabling high performance in standard benchmarks, including sine function approximation and MNIST digit classification. Overall, our work establishes a rigorous link between non-equilibrium steady states and computational expressivity.

</details>


### [54] [Born-rule statistical dynamical quantum phase transitions under measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16029)
*Guan-Hua Chen,Guo-Yi Zhu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过统计系综方法刻画量子淬火后一维量子伊辛链中所有可能的后测量态分布，建立了统计动力学量子相变（statistical DQPTs）框架，展示了临界时间附近杨-李-费雪零点的消失与非解析行为，并提出了基于测量量子计算的实验验证方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动力学量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transition, DQPT）依赖于返回概率（return probability）的非解析变化，但演化后期初始波函数振幅呈指数小，使单一后测量态难以反映相变全貌。因此需要从统计角度对所有符合玻恩规则（Born's rule）的后测量态进行系统性表征。

Method: 对量子淬火后的一维量子伊辛链（quantum Ising chain）进行抽样，将后测量态分布映射为统计模型，引入平均动力学自由能（average dynamical free energy）以建立统计DQPT框架；通过解析延拓到复时间平面分析杨-李-费雪零点（Yang-Lee-Fisher zeros）的消失行为；提出基于单量子比特测量的二维簇态（cluster state）量子计算协议以模拟幺正演化。

Result: 在高阶矩平均下恢复出DQPT信号；在临界时间附近观测到能级分布的去局域化（delocalized level distribution）；通过复时间解析延拓发现杨-李-费雪零点消失并出现能级交叉（level crossing）。

Conclusion: 统计DQPT框架为实验上在量子器件中研究动力学相变提供了可行途径，揭示了DQPT视角下的结构化电路采样（structured circuit sampling）机制，并将退相干导致的混合态（mixed state）理解推广到非平衡情形。

Abstract: Dynamical quantum phase transitions (DQPTs) occur at times when a quantum state exhibits a nonanalytic change in its return probability. This can be viewed as the probability of collapsing the evolved state to the initial state by quantum measurement. However, the initial wave function usually has exponentially small amplitude in the late time evolved state. Here we perform statistical characterization for all the possible post-measurement states distributed according to the Born's rule, by sampling a one-dimensional quantum Ising chain after a quantum quench dynamics. The statistical ensemble can also be viewed as a mixed state when the time evolved state is subjected to maximally dephasing noise in a certain basis. We map the distribution to a statistical model and characterize its effective "energy" spectrum, and introduce the average dynamical free energy, establishing a framework for the statistical DQPTs. We show the recovering of DQPT under high-moment average and a delocalized level distribution following critical times. Through analytic continuation into the complex time plane, we demonstrate the vanishing of Yang-Lee-Fisher zeros and the emergent level crossing near critical times. Finally, we propose a measurement-based quantum computation protocol to simulate the unitary evolution via single-qubit measurements on a two-dimensional cluster state. Our results provide a way for experimentally investigating statistical DQPTs in quantum devices, shedding light on the structured circuit sampling with insights from DQPT and generalizing the understanding of mixed state due to decoherence beyond equilibrium.

</details>


### [55] [Extensive mixed-state entanglement in kinetically constrained superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16131)
*Lucas Winter,Jan Kumlin,Thomas Pohl,Andreas Nunnenkamp*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明在量子发射器（quantum emitters）体系中引入局域动力学约束（local kinetic constraint）可以在保持Dicke超辐射（Dicke superradiance）所有关键特征的同时产生大量混合态纠缠（mixed-state entanglement），并给出了可解析推导的发射率下界及峰值强度、峰值时间的标度律。该机制利用希尔伯特空间碎裂（Hilbert-space fragmentation）生成指数级分叉的衰变树与暗态（dark states）层级，且纠缠生成对原子衰变和集体退相（collective dephasing）具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Dicke超辐射中，量子发射器系综会产生集体辐射脉冲，但其混合态中并不存在纠缠。作者旨在寻找一种方式，在保留超辐射集体增强特性的同时，引入混合态纠缠，为耗散工程制备纠缠态提供新途径。

Method: 在发射器之间添加局域布尔约束（local Boolean constraint），形成动力学约束；利用希尔伯特空间碎裂导致Dicke阶梯（Dicke ladder）的指数级分叉衰变树；通过解析推导给出发射率下界，并建立暗态层级的层次结构。

Result: 对于任意局域布尔约束，解析推导出发射率的下界，得出峰值强度∝N²、峰值时间∝(log N)/N的标度律。该机制可超辐射加速制备纠缠暗态（entangled dark states），并产生指数级数量的长程纠缠单重态暗态（long-range entangled singlet dark states）。在原子衰变和集体退相下纠缠生成具有鲁棒性，且可在中性原子阵列耦合光学腔的实验条件下被观测。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种普适框架和实验上可行的方案，用于在超辐射增强下进行纠缠暗态的耗散工程（dissipative engineering of entangled dark states）。所提出的纠缠见证（witness）简单易行，可在现有实验条件下实现。

Abstract: Dicke superradiance by an ensemble of quantum emitters produces a collective burst of radiation, but no entanglement in the mixed state of the emitters. We show that adding a local kinetic constraint between the emitters generates extensive mixed-state entanglement, while otherwise preserving all key features of Dicke superradiance. Specifically, for any local Boolean constraint, we analytically derive a lower bound for the emission rate which implies a peak intensity $\propto N^2$ and a peak time $\propto (\log N)/N$ with number of spins $N$. This effect enables the superradiantly accelerated preparation of entangled dark states. Hereby, Hilbert-space fragmentation of the Dicke ladder leads to an exponentially branching decay tree that generates a hierarchy of dark states. Importantly, these disconnected manifolds include exponentially many long-range entangled singlet dark states. The explored kinetic constraints and superradiant dynamics can be realized in neutral-atom arrays coupled to an optical cavity, and we suggest a simple and accessible witness to detect the predicted mixed-state entanglement in such experiments. Moreover, we show that entanglement generation is robust against atomic decay and collective dephasing, and should be observable under recently reported experimental conditions. Our results, thereby, offer a general framework and experimentally viable approach for the dissipative engineering of entangled dark states enhanced by superradiance.

</details>

### [56] [Thermodynamic Invariants of Coupled Channels: A Many-Channel Tolman-Ehrenfest Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15653)
*Benjamin Hamblin,Victor Calo,Klaus Regenauer-Lieb*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导出多热力学通道下的唯一n通道不变量ζ_i T_i = C，其中ζ_i为Ruppeiner联络的和乐性（holonomy）。在颗粒体积-应力系综中，Rowe剪胀比和能量限制被证明是度规非对角曲率g_{Vσ}的几何后果，并解决了困扰学界60年的状态依赖K_μ问题，同时给出跨剪切带的可实验检验预言ζ_Vχ=const。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将Tolman-Ehrenfest效应扩展到熵流形（entropy manifold），利用Ruppeiner联络（Ruppeiner connection）的几何结构，推导出多通道耦合系统中的n通道不变量ζ_i T_i = C。在颗粒体积-应力系综中，通过分析度规的非对角曲率分量g_{Vσ}，将Rowe剪胀比和能量限制重新解释为几何后果。

Result: 推导出唯一的n通道不变量ζ_i T_i = C，建立了多通道耦合系统中的几何守恒律。证明了在颗粒体积-应力系综中，Rowe剪胀比和能量限制源自度规的非对角曲率g_{Vσ}。揭示了状态依赖K_μ的起源：校正项ζ_V在接近堵塞（jamming）时达到O(1)量级。给出了跨剪切带的实验可检验关系ζ_Vχ=const。

Conclusion: 多通道热力学耦合效应可由Ruppeiner联络的和乐性统一描述，颗粒材料的行为本质上具有几何根源。该框架不仅解决了K_μ的长期谜题，还提供了可直接通过剪切带实验验证的定量预言，为颗粒物质的热力学几何化开辟了新途径。

Abstract: When multiple thermodynamic channels are coupled, single-channel equilibrium conditions fail. Extending the Tolman--Ehrenfest effect to the entropy manifold, we derive the unique $n$-channel invariant $ζ_i T_i = C$, where $ζ_i$ is the holonomy of the Ruppeiner connection. For the granular volume--stress ensemble, Rowe's dilatancy ratio and energy restriction emerge as geometric consequences of the off-diagonal curvature $g_{Vσ}$, and the 60-year puzzle of state-dependent $K_μ$ is resolved: the correction $ζ_V$ reaches $O(1)$ near jamming. The prediction $ζ_Vχ=\mathrm{const}$ across a shear band is experimentally testable.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 在13.6 TeV质子-质子对撞能量下，首次实现了W±W±和WZ与双喷注联合产生的电弱过程高显著性观测，为后续电弱物理精确检验和新物理搜索提供了实验依据。

Abstract: The production cross sections of W$^\pm$W$^{\pm}$ and WZ boson pairs in association with two jets in proton-proton collisions are measured at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV. The data sample corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 171 fb$^{-1}$, collected with the CMS detector during 2022$-$2024. The measurements are performed in the leptonic decay modes: W$^{\pm}$Z $\to$ $\ell^\pmν\ell^{\prime\pm}\ell^{\prime\mp}$ and W$^\pm$W$^{\pm}$ $\to$ $\ell^\pmν\ell^{\prime\pm}ν$, where $\ell, \ell'$ = e or $μ$. The electroweak productions of W$^\pm$W$^{\pm}$ and WZ bosons are each observed with a significance greater than five standard deviations from the background-only hypothesis. Differential fiducial cross sections as functions of several observables are also measured.

### [58] [Locating nuclear-powered submarines with antineutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15642)
*Sven-Patrik Hallsjö*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文重新审视基于反中微子（antineutrino）的核潜艇探测方案，将其类比为类SOSUS的“屏障”概念部署于战略海峡。通过解析标度关系和数值估算，评估了在直布罗陀海峡和GIUK等水域的探测可行性，指出探测能力主要依赖于最近距离、探测器深度和部署质量，并给出了不同场景下的基准得分（$Z_A$）与探测器数量需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拥挤水道中，核动力潜艇难以通过常规方法追踪。本文旨在重新评估基于反中微子的探测技术，作为一种屏障式概念（barrier concept），以弥补现有手段在战略海峡等关键水域的不足。

Method: 采用解析标度关系（analytic scaling relations）和数值估算方法，分析探测能力对最近距离（closest approach）、探测器深度（detector depth）和部署质量（deployed mass）的依赖关系。针对直布罗陀海峡和GIUK（格陵兰-冰岛-英国）等典型场景，设定代表性假设、泊松操作点（Poisson operating point）和阈值条件，计算基准得分$Z_A$。

Result: 在直布罗陀海峡，一个20千吨（kt）探测器在保守最坏情形下（100 MW热功率）达到$Z_A\simeq2.54$，对应$(P_\mathrm{FA},P_\mathrm{det})\simeq(5.5\times10^{-3},0.51)$（阈值$k=2$）；三个探测器组成的线阵将$Z_A$提升至4.66。对于GIUK等宽阔海域，基准最大通过距离（PDD$_{\max}$）为5 km时，约80个探测器仅达到$Z_A\sim1.6$。

Conclusion: 论文概述了第一代可行性评估所需的探测器技术选择、统计假设和部署约束。结果表明，反中微子探测在狭窄海峡具有潜在可行性，但在宽阔海域需要大量探测器，整体方案仍处于初步评估阶段。

Abstract: Nuclear-powered submarines are difficult to track with conventional methods in congested waterways. We revisit antineutrino-based detection as a barrier concept, analogous to a neutrino-enabled SOSUS-style fence in strategic straits. Using analytic scaling relations and numerical estimates, we show that detectability depends primarily on closest approach, detector depth, and deployed mass. For representative assumptions, a 20\,kt detector in the Strait of Gibraltar reaches a local benchmark score $Z_A\simeq2.54$ for an assumed 100\,MW thermal-power sensitivity-study case in a conservative worst-case transit (with Poisson operating point $(P_\mathrm{FA},P_\mathrm{det})\simeq(5.5\times10^{-3},0.51)$ at threshold $k=2$), while a three-detector line raises the mapped score to $Z_A\simeq4.66$. For broad ocean passages such as GIUK, required detector counts are substantially larger; in the baseline maximum passing distance $\mathrm{PDD}_{\max}=5$\,km geometry, about 80 detectors yield only $Z_A\sim1.6$. The paper outlines detector technology choices, statistical assumptions, and deployment constraints for a first-generation feasibility assessment.

### [59] [A general proof of integer Rényi QNEC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15272)
*Tanay Kibe,Pratik Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文证明了在具有半侧模包含（half-sided modular inclusion）结构的冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）中，对于所有整数Rényi参数n≥2，Rényi量子零能量条件（Rényi quantum null energy condition, Rényi QNEC）成立。该证明仅要求激发态相对于真空的夹层Rényi散度（sandwiched Rényi divergence, SRD）有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rényi量子零能量条件（Rényi QNEC）是对量子零能量条件（QNEC）的单参数推广，它假设在局域庞加莱不变量子场论中，激发态相对于真空的夹层Rényi散度（SRD）的第二零形状变分为非负。该条件尚需证明，本文旨在为具有半侧模包含结构的冯·诺依曼代数建立该猜想。

Method: 作者采用算子代数（operator algebra）方法，利用半侧模包含结构（half-sided modular inclusion structure）和冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）框架。核心证明策略是证明在零平移半群（null-translation semigroup）下，任意正常正泛函（normal positive functional）的Kosaki L^n范数（Kosaki L^n norm）具有对数凸性（log-convexity），其中要求该泛函的L^n范数有限。

Result: 对于所有整数Rényi参数n≥2，在携带半侧模包含结构的冯·诺依曼代数上，Rényi QNEC成立。证明的唯一条件是激发态相对于真空的夹层Rényi散度（SRD）有限。

Conclusion: 本文为Rényi量子零能量条件（Rényi QNEC）在算子代数框架下提供了严格证明，将其从原始QNEC推广至Rényi熵情形。这一结果增进了对量子场论中能量条件与模结构间关系的理解。

Abstract: The Rényi quantum null energy condition conjectures that the second null shape variation of the sandwiched Rényi divergence (SRD) of an excited state relative to the vacuum is non-negative in local Poincaré-invariant quantum field theory, giving a one-parameter generalization of the quantum null energy condition (QNEC). We prove Rényi QNEC for all integer Rényi parameters $n\geq 2$ for von Neumann algebras carrying a half-sided modular inclusion structure. The only assumption on the excited state is finiteness of its SRD relative to the vacuum. Concretely, for any $σ$-finite von Neumann algebra with such an inclusion, we prove log-convexity, under the associated null-translation semigroup, of the Kosaki $L^n$ norm of any normal positive functional with finite $L^n$ norm.

### [60] [Generating Rotation in a Snap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15258)
*Soumangsu Chakraborty,Pierre Heidmann,Gela Patashuri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种纯代数的新技术，可从任意渐近平坦的四维或五维静态解直接生成旋转解，无需求解爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）。该方法通过将静态解变换至AdS×S渐近形式、执行坐标旋转后再变换回渐近平直时空来实现。在五维最小超引力（minimal supergravity）中实现该构造，并成功从史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black holes）恢复出克尔黑洞（Kerr）和迈尔斯-佩里黑洞（Myers-Perry black holes），进而应用于静态Weyl解线性类，首次得到描述任意数量非极端旋转带电源的线性ansatz。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统构造旋转时空几何需要直接求解复杂的爱因斯坦场方程。本文旨在建立一种纯代数的、无需求解微分方程的系统性方法，能够从已知的静态解直接生成对应的旋转解。

Method: 方法为纯代数构造，分为三步：(1) 将渐近平直（asymptotically flat）的静态解通过变换转化为AdS×S渐近形式；(2) 执行坐标平移至均匀旋转系（uniformly rotating frame）；(3) 再将解变换回渐近平直时空。该构造在五维最小超引力框架中实现，但可推广至任何允许AdS×S几何和相应sigma模型变换的理论框架。

Result: 作为首次应用，该方法直接从史瓦西黑洞恢复出四维克尔黑洞和五维迈尔斯-佩里黑洞。进一步应用于静态Weyl解线性类，首次得到描述任意数量非极端（non-extremal）旋转带电线性源的ansatz。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种系统且简洁的代数路径，用于在四维和五维中构造非极端旋转几何，避免了求解爱因斯坦方程的传统复杂流程，并具有跨理论框架的适用性。

Abstract: We build a new technique to generate rotation from arbitrary static solutions that asymptote to four- or five-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. The method is purely algebraic and does not require solving Einstein equations. It proceeds by transforming the static solution to AdS$\times$S asymptotics, performing a coordinate shift to a uniformly rotating frame, and then transforming the solution back to asymptotically flat spacetime. We implement this construction in five-dimensional minimal supergravity, although it applies more broadly to any framework admitting AdS$\times$S geometries and relevant sigma-model transformations. As a first application, we recover simply the Kerr and Myers-Perry black holes directly from Schwarzschild black holes. We then apply the method to the linear class of static Weyl solutions and obtain the first linear ansatz describing an arbitrary number of non-extremal rotating and charged sources. This approach provides a systematic and simple route to constructing non-extremal rotating geometries in four and five dimensions.

</details>


### [61] [Ising anyons in the $SU(2)_2$ Chern--Simons theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15268)
*Artem Belov,Andrey Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了伊辛极小模型 $\mathcal{M}(4,3)$ 与 $SU(2)_2$ Chern-Simons 理论在可观测层面上的等价性，并重点分析了低阶张量积中表示结构的不匹配问题，指出这些差异不影响拓扑量子计算算法所依赖的可观测量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文通过比较伊辛极小模型与 $SU(2)_2$ Chern-Simons 理论在低阶张量积（tensor product）下的表示结构，系统性地分析了二者在此层面上的差异。

Result: 研究发现，尽管两种理论在表示结构上存在差异（如低阶张量积框架下的表示结构不同），但这些差异并不影响拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computation）算法所依赖的可观测量。

Conclusion: 伊辛极小模型与 $SU(2)_2$ Chern-Simons 理论在表示结构上的差异并不破坏二者在可观测层面上的等价性，因此不会对基于这些理论的拓扑量子计算应用构成实质性影响。

Abstract: The present work is motivated by the statement that the Ising minimal model $\mathcal{M}(4,3)$ is equivalent, at the level of observables, to the $SU(2)_2$ Chern--Simons theory. At first glance, however, these two theories appear to differ substantially. For instance, the number of irreducible highest-weight representations does not match the number of Ising anyons. For tensor products of low degree, these discrepancies are examined in this work. While representation structure differs, it does not affect the observables underlying topological quantum computation algorithms.

### [62] [Bordisms between 9d type IIB supergravities and commutator widths of duality groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15276)
*Camilo las Heras,Ignacio Ruiz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究9维规范超引力之间的边陲（bordism）的拓扑性质，发现当单值性（monodromy）变大时边陲被任意压制，与量子引力中全局对称性破缺的预期相矛盾。为此，作者提出了沼泽地边陲猜想（Swampland Cobordism Conjecture）的一个精炼版本，指出若对偶群（duality group）G的换位子宽度（commutator width）发散，则需要包含无穷多个实现对偶缺陷（duality defects）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中普遍预期全局对称性会被破坏，但研究发现通过引力孤子实现大单值性的边陲会被任意压制，这与上述预期矛盾，因此需要对现有的沼泽地边陲猜想进行修正。

Method: 利用从IIB型弦论在带有非平凡SL(2,Z)丛的S^1上紧化得到的9维规范超引力之间的边陲，分析其拓扑性质。通过[p,q]7-膜（7-branes）或具有非平凡拓扑的引力孤子（gravitational solitons）来描述这些边陲如何实现所需的单值性。

Result: 发现对于大单值性，边陲的拓扑变得极其复杂，导致相关边陲被任意压制。针对第一边陲群Ω_1(BG)（配备G对偶丛）提出精炼版沼泽地边陲猜想：即使引力孤子可以实现换位子子群（commutator subgroup）中元素对应的单值性，若所需换位子数量无界（即G的换位子宽度发散），则必须包含无穷多个实现G中元素的对偶缺陷。

Conclusion: 该精炼猜想在不同对偶群G上得到检验，并以非平凡的方式得到了验证。

Abstract: We study the topological properties of bordisms interpolating between different 9d gauged supergravities obtained from compactification of type IIB string theory on $\mathbb{S}^1$ with a non-trivial $\mathsf{SL}(2,\mathbb{Z})$ bundle. We describe how such bordisms implement the needed monodromies through stacks of $[p,q]$ 7-branes or gravitational solitons of non-trivial topology. For the later mechanism, we see that the topology of the bordism becomes increasingly complicated for large monodromies, which results in the associated bordisms being arbitrarily suppressed, against expectations on the breaking of global symmetries in Quantum Gravity. Motivated by this, we propose a refinement of the Swampland Cobordism Conjecture for the first bordism group $Ω_1({\rm B}G)$ with a $G$ duality bundle. We argue that even if gravitational solitons can realize the monodromies associated with elements of the commutator subgroup of $G$, if the number of needed commutators is unbounded (in other words, the commutator width of $G$ diverges) then an infinite number of duality defects realizing elements in $G$ need to be included. We test this proposal for different duality groups $G$, and see that our expectations are realized, often in non-trivial ways.

</details>


### [63] [Dimensional reduction of AdS3 Chern-Simons gravity: Schwarzian and affine boundary theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15293)
*Goffredo Chirco,Lucio Vacchiano,Patrizia Vitale*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过对称性约化将带环面边界的AdS₃/ℤ₂引力（表述为SO(2,2)陈-西蒙斯理论）降维为一个二维BF类模型加一维边界作用量，发现两种不等价边界扇区分别对应标准Drinfel'd–Sokolov约化（Schwarzian动力学）和变形Schwarzian泛函（Rindler型非极值区域），并给出两种扇区上的Kac–Moody扩展。

Method: 将AdS₃/ℤ₂引力表述为SO(2,2)陈-西蒙斯（Chern–Simons）理论，施加全局定义的对称性并限制规范联络在该对称流下不变，从而约化为二维BF类模型和一维诱导边界作用量；通过变分原理层面区分两种边界条件得到不同扇区。

Abstract: We study a symmetry-reduced sector of $AdS_3/\mathbb Z_2$ gravity formulated as an $SO(2,2)$ Chern--Simons theory on a 3D-manifold with toroidal boundary. The reduction is implemented by requiring a globally defined symmetry and restricting to the sector in which the gauge connection is invariant along the symmetry flow. The resulting theory reduces to a two-dimensional BF-like model together with an induced one-dimensional boundary action. We show that the reduced theory admits two inequivalent boundary sectors, originated by two different boundary conditions for the parent 3d theory at the level of the variational principle. On the boundary subspace $A_τ=Φ$, the universal one-dimensional action reproduces the standard Drinfel'd--Sokolov reduction in JT gravity which captures the Schwarzian boundary dynamics. On the generalized boundary $A_τ=λ'Φ+u^{-1}\partial_τu$, the same action instead yields a deformed Schwarzian functional with affine residual symmetry, naturally associated with a non-extremal or Rindler-type regime. We further show how the $\mathfrak{so}(2,2)$ algebra of the 3D Chern--Simons model naturally leads to current-dressed Kac--Moody extensions of both sectors.

### [64] [Comments on higher-derivative corrections in the AdS/CFT duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15478)

Method: 采用Gauss-Bonnet黑洞背景下的一类全息超导体作为具体案例，分析使用了不恰当"AdS/CFT字典"所带来的问题。

Result: 高阶导数修正会改变自发凝聚等物理量的定性行为；凝聚的增大或减小依赖于具体系统，不存在普适性。

Abstract: We point out that some works on higher-derivative corrections in the AdS/CFT duality use inappropriate "AdS/CFT dictionary." We illustrate the problem using a class of holographic superconductors in the Gauss-Bonnet black hole background. We also point out another problem in previous works. These modifications can change the qualitative behavior of physical quantities such as the spontaneous condensate. Whether the condensate increases or decreases under higher-derivative corrections depends on the system one considers, and there is no universality in this sense.

### [65] [Critical slowing down of black hole phase transition and universal dynamic scaling in AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15655)
*Mozib Bin Awal,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将自由能景观（free energy landscape）的随机框架拓展至Kerr-AdS黑洞，研究了反德西特时空中黑洞相变的动力学临界行为。通过分析熵的朗之万（Langevin）演化、福克-普朗克（Fokker-Planck）方程本征值及沿不同热力学路径的弛豫时间标度关系，发现弛豫时间在临界点附近满足$τ=|ε|^{-2/3}$的稳健标度律，且该标度指数在RN-AdS、Kerr-AdS和Bardeen黑洞中一致，暗示了不同黑洞系统间存在普适的动力学临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将自由能景观动力学（free energy landscape dynamics）的随机框架从RN-AdS黑洞拓展至Kerr-AdS黑洞，探究黑洞相变在临界点附近的动力学临界行为，并检验该行为是否具有跨系统的普适性（universality）。

Method: 分析熵（entropy）的朗之万方程（Langevin equation）演化（而非RN-AdS情况下的视界半径），结合福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）的最低本征值，考察温度、压力和角动量等不同热力学路径下趋近和远离临界点两个方向的弛豫时间标度关系。

Result: 系统在临界点附近表现出显著的临界慢化（critical slowing down），自相关时间（autocorrelation time）急剧增大。弛豫时间（relaxation time）在临界点附近遵循标度关系$τ=|ε|^{-2/3}$，且该标度指数在RN-AdS、Kerr-AdS和Bardeen黑洞中均相同。

Conclusion: 不同黑洞系统共享相同的动力学临界标度指数，表明黑洞热力学中存在普适的动力学临界现象。该结果建立了自由能景观几何、随机非平衡动力学与黑洞热力学中普适临界现象之间的联系。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical critical behaviour of black hole phase transitions in anti de Sitter spacetime by extending the stochastic framework of free energy landscape dynamics to Kerr AdS black holes. By analyzing the Langevin evolution of the entropy (in contrast to the horizon radius in the RN-AdS case) near criticality, we demonstrate that the system exhibits pronounced critical slowing down, characterized by a significant increase of the autocorrelation time as the critical point is approached. This behaviour is further confirmed by the lowest eigenvalue of the Fokker-Planck equation. By analysing the dynamics along different thermodynamic paths, including variations in temperature, pressure, and angular momentum, and considering both directions - towards and away from criticality, we find that the relaxation time obeys a robust scaling relation, $τ=|ε|^{-2/3}$ near criticality. The same scaling exponent is obtained for RN-AdS, Kerr-AdS, and Bardeen black holes, suggesting the existence of an underlying universal dynamical behaviour across distinct black hole systems. Our results establish a connection between the geometry of the free energy landscape, stochastic nonequilibrium dynamics, and universal critical phenomena in black hole thermodynamics.

TL;DR: 本文发现，在平坦开放实环面（flat open solid torus）上的共形场论（CFT）中，Weyl标架下的两点函数精确对应于一条完全位于AdS体内部的有界测地线（finite geodesic）。该对应关系是精确的，不需要大N、强耦合或重算子等条件，且标准边界锚定（boundary-anchored）关联是此精确对（exact pair）的奇异极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索AdS/CFT对偶中超越传统大N与强耦合近似下的精确对应关系，寻找边界算子两点函数与体内部测地线之间更一般的精确匹配机制。

Method: 在平坦开放实环面（flat open solid torus）上分析CFT_D的Weyl标架两点函数；对自由标量场沿S^1方向进行模式展开（mode expansion），得到H_{D-1}上的无穷维有效质量（effective masses）塔，并通过精确重求和（resummation）恢复为高维测地线表达式。

Result: CFT两点函数与AdS体内部有界测地线之间存在精确对应，无需大N、强耦合或重算子条件；标准边界锚定关联是该精确对的奇异极限；自由标量场的模式展开与传播子重求和精确复现了这一测地线描述。

Conclusion: 该发现与同一几何上发现的纠缠熵与缠绕熵截面（entanglement wedge cross-section）之间的另一精确对共同指向AdS/CFT中更广泛的“精确对”（exact-pair）纲领。

Abstract: We show that for a CFT$_D$ on a flat open solid torus, the two point function in the Weyl frame is exactly paired with a finite geodesic lying entirely in the AdS$_{D+1}$ bulk interior. This relation is exact and requires neither large $N$, strong coupling, nor heavy operators. The standard boundary-anchored relation is a singular limit of the exact pair. For the free scalar, a mode expansion along $S^1$ generates an infinite tower of effective masses on $H_{D-1}$, whose intricate propagators resum exactly to the same simple higher-dimensional geodesic expression. Together with another exact pair between disjoint entanglement entropy and entanglement wedge cross-section found on the same open solid torus, this result points toward a broader exact-pair program in AdS/CFT.

### [67] [Anomalous Transport from Effective Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15968)
*Rémy Larue,Amaury Marchon,Jérémie Quevillon,Diego Saviot*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论（Effective Field Theory）框架，通过路径积分在有限温度下积掉大质量狄拉克费米子，系统计算了手征效应及其反常，并统一了之前被分别处理的手征输运现象，同时揭示了各反常输运效应与反常之间的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征效应（chiral effects）在以往研究中往往被分别处理，缺乏统一的理论框架来揭示它们之间的内在联系及其与反常（anomaly）的深层次关系——包括质量修正以及反常为零但仍存在手征效应的配置。

Method: 采用有效场论（Effective Field Theory）框架，在有限温度下、存在矢量和轴矢背景场时，通过路径积分（path-integral）积掉一个大质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermion），从而计算流（currents）及其反常，并仔细处理正则化（regularisation）以获得确定的和协变的反常（consistent and covariant anomalies）。

Result: 在同一计算中自然地统一了之前被分别处理的手征效应，并发现了新的质量修正（mass corrections）。明确建立了每个反常输运效应（anomalous transport effect）与反常之间的联系，超越了仅识别系数的层面；发现即使在反常本身为零的配置中，手征效应仍可由理论的反常性质驱动。此外，物理流不能简单地从陈-西蒙斯项（Chern-Simons terms）中推断出来。

Conclusion: 该工作为手征效应及其反常起源提供了统一的理论描述，揭示了反常与输运效应之间超越系数对应关系的深层联系，并指出有限温度下物理流的来源不能仅由陈-西蒙斯项的反常发散行为来理解。

Abstract: A systematic study of chiral effects is presented using an Effective Field Theory framework. By integrating out a massive Dirac fermion at finite temperature in presence of vector and axial background fields, the currents and their anomalies are computed from the path-integral. Chiral effects previously considered separately naturally arise in a unified computation, including new mass corrections. The link between each anomalous transport effect and the anomalies is clearly established, beyond the identification of their coefficients. In particular, we can appreciate how these effects are sourced by the anomalous nature of the theory even in configurations where the anomaly itself vanishes. The consistent and covariant anomalies are both encapsulated in master formulae for the currents which result from a careful treatment of the regularisation. It is finally found that, at finite temperature, the physical currents cannot be inferred simply from the Chern-Simons terms whose divergence reproduce the chiral anomalies.

### [68] [Walking Sudakov: From Cusp to Octagon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16034)

Result: 发现了一种新的标度极限，在该极限下形状因子和散射振幅均表现出双对数行为，受行走反常维数控制。该行走反常维数在壳区域的尖端反常维数（cusp anomalous dimension）与离壳区域的八边形反常维数（octagon anomalous dimension）之间平滑插值。基于双圈结果提出了全阶形式的行走反常维数，但该表达式依赖于目前未知的‘t Hooft耦合函数。

Conclusion: Coulomb支上的Sudakov形状因子和四点散射振幅提供了一个可控框架，用于理解规范理论中壳与离壳区域之间的插值行为。行走反常维数的全阶形式已被提出，但其完整确定需要进一步研究未知的‘t Hooft耦合函数。

Abstract: We study the Sudakov form factor and the four-point scattering amplitude on the Coulomb branch of planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM as functions of the Coulomb-branch parameters and kinematic invariants. This setup provides a controlled probe of the interpolation between on- and off-shell regimes of infrared-sensitive quantities in gauge theories. We identify a novel scaling limit in which both observables exhibit double-logarithmic behavior governed by a walking anomalous dimension. As the mass scales are varied, this walking anomalous dimension interpolates between the cusp anomalous dimension of the on-shell regime and the octagon anomalous dimension of the off-shell regime. Based on the explicit two-loop result and the expected all-order structure, we propose an all-loop form for the walking anomalous dimension both for the form factor and for the four-point scattering amplitude. These all-loop expressions depend on new, presently unknown functions of the 't Hooft coupling.

### [69] [Boundary anomalous dimensions from BCFT: $φ^{3}$ theories with a boundary and higher-derivative generalizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16119)

Abstract: We consider the bulk $φ^3$ deformation of the free boundary conformal field theory in the $ε$ expansion. We determine the leading corrections to the scaling dimensions of boundary fundamental operators and some boundary operator expansion coefficients. Our procedure combines the conformal multiplet recombination with the boundary crossing symmetry. The results cover both the single field case and the multi-field case with $S_{N+1}$ global symmetry, which are associated with the Yang-Lee model and the $(N+1)$-state Potts model respectively. These semi-infinite models describe branched polymers, percolation, and spanning forest at a surface. We generalize these results to some higher derivative theories. In addition, we study the $φ^{2n+1}$ theories with $n>1$, but only obtain some boundary operator expansion coefficients.

### [70] [Non-Invertible Symmetries in Compactified Supergravities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16188)
*Fabián Caro-Pérez,María Pilar García del Moral,Álvaro Restuccia*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高维超引力理论中的非可逆对称性缺陷在低维紧化下的行为，以理解M理论与IIA型超引力之间对称性结构的对应关系。

Method: 从十一维超引力中非可逆缺陷的构造出发，在零模超引力区域（zero-mode Supergravity regime）沿M理论圆对缺陷（含辅助拓扑扇区）进行pushforward操作，并对十一维Bianchi扇区进行紧化分解。

Result: 七维Chern--Simons型辅助理论降维为六维BF型扇区；十一维Bianchi扇区紧化分解为可逆的H_{[3]}扇区与扭曲的非可逆\(\widetilde F_{[4]}\)扇区，满足\(d\widetilde F_{[4]}+H_{[3]}\wedge F_{[2]}=0\)；所得IIA型缺陷代数同时包含可逆Picard子群与非可逆BF修饰缺陷，带电荷探针可通过标准M理论/IIA型膜词典识别。

Conclusion: 非可逆高形式对称性缺陷的Kaluza--Klein约化在超引力层面是可行的，紧化后的对称性结构包含可逆与非可逆两部分，且与已知的膜对应关系一致。

Abstract: We study the \textit{Kaluza--Klein} descent of non-invertible higher-form symmetry defects from eleven-dimensional Supergravity to Type IIA Supergravity. Starting from the eleven-dimensional construction of non-invertible Supergravity defects, we show that the full defect, including its auxiliary topological sector, admits a pushforward along the M-theory circle in the zero-mode Supergravity regime. The seven-dimensional \textit{Chern--Simons}-like auxiliary theory descends to a six-dimensional \(BF\)-type sector. We also show that the compactification of the eleven-dimensional \textit{Bianchi} sector splits into an invertible \(H_{[3]}\)-sector and a twisted non-invertible \(\widetilde F_{[4]}\)-sector, controlled by \(d\widetilde F_{[4]}+H_{[3]}\wedge F_{[2]}=0\). The resulting Type IIA defect algebra contains both an invertible Picard subgroup and non-invertible \(BF\)-dressed defects, with charged probes identified through the standard M-theory/Type IIA brane dictionary.

</details>


### [71] [Supergravity flows, wormholes and their pseudo-Hermitian holographic duals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16168)
*Jose M. Begines,Antón F. Faedo,Carlos Hoyos,Daniele Musso*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现超引力（supergravity）一致截断中的解，将实标量场解析延拓至虚数值，同时确保时空度量保持实值。这些解包括连接两个渐近Anti-de Sitter时空的洛伦兹可穿越虫洞（Lorentzian traversable wormhole），以及提升到十维或十一维后仍保持实度量的流。全息对偶理论被论证为赝厄米（pseudo-Hermitian）且PT对称（PT-symmetric）的理论。虫洞解还可解释为两堆膜-反膜系统在快子凝聚（tachyon condensation）后的低能理论，其全息对偶为两拷贝理论之间的纠缠态。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超引力一致截断中实标量场解析延拓至虚值后仍保持实度量的解，并考察这些解在全息对偶（holographic duality）框架下的物理诠释，包括虫洞与纠缠结构的关系。

Method: 对超引力一致截断中的实标量场进行解析延拓（analytic continuation）至虚数值，保持度量为实数；基于所得解构建洛伦兹可穿越虫洞及高维提升后实度量的流；利用赝厄米性与PT对称性刻画全息对偶理论，并通过互信息（mutual information）计算和Goldstone玻色子识别来提供证据。

Result: 存在洛伦兹可穿越虫洞解，连接两个渐近Anti-de Sitter时空；存在提升至十维或十一维后度量仍为实的流；虫洞解可解释为两堆膜-反膜系统在快子凝聚后的低能理论；全息对偶为赝厄米且PT对称的理论，虫洞对应两拷贝理论之间的纠缠态。

Conclusion: 超引力中实标量场的虚值解析延拓可以在保持度量实性的前提下产生新的非平庸解，包括可穿越虫洞。这些解的全息对偶为赝厄米PT对称理论，虫洞的纠缠结构可通过互信息与对称性破缺（两个Poincaré对称性破缺至对角子群）得到验证。

Abstract: We find solutions to consistent truncations of supergravity where some real scalars are analytically extended to imaginary values, ensuring the metric remains real-valued. Among the solutions there are Lorentzian traversable wormholes connecting two asymptotically Anti-de Sitter spacetimes and flows that have a real metric also when uplifted to ten or eleven dimensions. We argue that the holographic duals are pseudo-Hermitian and $PT$-symmetric theories. Wormhole solutions also admit an interpretation as the low-energy theory of two stacks of branes and antibranes after tachyon condensation. The wormhole is then dual to an entangled state of two copies of the theory that lives on a stack of branes. We present some evidence by computing the mutual information between the theories at each boundary and by identifying the Goldstone bosons associated to the breaking of the two copies of Poincaré symmetry to their diagonal subgroup.

### [72] [Background-Equivariant BRST Observables and i-Particle Propagators from an Auxiliary Quartet in SU(3) Yang-Mills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16172)
*M. M. Amaral,V. E. R. Lemes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在 $SU(3)$ 杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）的朗道规范（Landau gauge）下构造了一个 BRST 精确四重态机制（BRST-exact quartet mechanism），通过引入一个与经典运动方程相容的 Cartan 取向背景（Cartan-oriented background），在不引入显式破缺项的情况下复现了早期副本模型中的 $i$-粒子传播子结构，并证明了该机制的完全量子化框架具有可重整化性（renormalizability）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 $SU(3)$ 杨-米尔斯理论的朗道规范下构建一个 BRST 精确四重态机制，使得四重态扇区在标准真空中上同调平凡（cohomologically trivial），从而保证与纯杨-米尔斯理论的等价性；同时，通过引入合适的背景场，在不破坏 BRST 对偶定理（BRST doublet theorem）的前提下，系统性地复现 $i$-粒子传播子结构。

Method: 构造了同时包含对易子（commutator）和反对易子（anticommutator）结构的变换规则，将场自由度从八个扩展至九个；在预设的 Cartan 取向背景（与经典运动方程兼容）下引入一个质量矩阵，该矩阵复现了早期副本模型中不同的 $i$-粒子传播子结构；通过将背景生成与可观测上同调（observable cohomology）分离以尊重 BRST 对偶定理；引入背景等变协变 Cartan 标架（background-equivariant covariant Cartan frame），证明滤波后的 $i$-粒子双线性形式是全体阶离壳 BRST 上循环（off-shell BRST cocycle）的最低阶微扰分量。

Result: 尽管基本传播子（elementary propagator）具有复极点（complex poles），其领先的两点函数仍保留了 Källén-Lehmann 表示（Källén-Lehmann representation），具有实的正阈值和正谱密度（positive spectral density）；完全量子化作用量提供了一个一致的可重整化框架，从而建立了一个从 BRST 精确四重态扩展至 $SU(3)$ 的、系统性地恢复 $i$-粒子传播子并识别 BRST 控复合可观测量的机制。

Conclusion: 该 BRST 精确四重态机制为在 $SU(3)$ 杨-米尔斯理论中系统性地生成 $i$-粒子传播子结构提供了严格的理论基础，同时确保了理论的等价性、上同调一致性和可重整化性。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a BRST-exact quartet mechanism in $SU(3)$ Yang-Mills theory in the Landau gauge. The quartet sector is cohomologically trivial in the standard vacuum, ensuring equivalence to pure Yang-Mills theory. The transformation rules carry both commutator and anticommutator structures, enlarging the field content from eight to nine degrees of freedom.
  Working in a prescribed Cartan-oriented background (compatible with the classical equations of motion), the theory induces a mass matrix reproducing the distinct $i$-particle propagator structure of earlier replica models without explicit breaking terms. To respect the BRST doublet theorem, we separate background generation from observable cohomology. Introducing a background-equivariant covariant Cartan frame, we show the filtered $i$-particle bilinear is the lowest perturbative component of an all-orders off-shell BRST cocycle. Despite the complex poles of elementary propagators, its leading two-point function retains a Källén--Lehmann representation with a real positive threshold and positive spectral density. The fully quantized action provides a consistent framework for renormalizability, establishing a systematic mechanism for recovering $i$-particle propagators and identifying BRST-controlled composite observables from a BRST-exact quartet extended to $SU(3)$.

### [73] [Fortuity and Complexity in a Simple Quark Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16254)
*Jackson R. Fliss,Vishnu Jejjala,Onkar Parrikar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文揭示了超对称理论中BPS算符的分类与QCD中规范不变夸克算符之间的结构相似性，并利用BRST上同调将重子态归类为偶然（fortuitous）算符、介子态归类为单调（monotone）算符。在Veneziano极限下，重子与介子在算符计数上呈现指数与多项式的二分法，且典型重子态在经典模拟复杂度上表现出超指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超对称理论中单调与偶然BPS算符的分类与QCD中规范不变夸克算符之间的结构相似性，并建立一种不依赖超对称性的广义分类框架。

Method: 利用BRST上同调（BRST cohomology）代替超对称性来定义偶然性（fortuity）；在Veneziano极限（大N_f、大N_c极限）下分析算符计数特征；引入玩具量子比特（qubit）模型进行明确验证；使用稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）作为经典模拟复杂度的代理指标。

Result: 重子态被归类为偶然算符，介子态被归类为单调算符；在Veneziano极限下，偶然算符与单调算符分别呈现指数增长与多项式增长的计数二分法；所有介子态显示幂律复杂度，典型重子态显示超指数复杂度。

Conclusion: 该分类框架在不依赖超对称性的条件下成功推广了BPS算符分类思想，并揭示了QCD中重子与介子在算符计数和经典模拟复杂度上的本质差异。

Abstract: We observe and elaborate on a structural similarity between the categorization of monotone and fortuitous BPS operators in supersymmetric theories and gauge invariant quark operators in $SU(N_c)$ QCD. Our designation of fortuity does not rely on supersymmetry and instead uses the BRST cohomology. We argue that within this designation, baryon states are fortuitous while meson states are monotone. We illustrate that in the Veneziano limit of large number of flavors and colors, this designation displays features resembling the fortuitous vs. monotone categorization of BPS operators, e.g., an exponential vs. polynomial dichotomy in the counting of operators. We explore these ideas explicitly in a toy qubit model of quarks. We further investigate the stabilizer Rényi entropy of meson and baryon states as a proxy for the complexity of classical simulation for these states. We show that all mesons display power law complexity and present evidence that typical baryons display super-exponential complexity in the Veneziano limit.

### [74] [Nonlocal Optical Response and Surface Susceptibilities: A Systematic Derivation via Spatial Moment Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15716)
*Frédéric Zolla*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个系统理论，将均匀介质的非局部响应核与任意弯曲界面上的有效表面磁化率联系起来。通过空间矩展开和分布薄层极限，推导出界面响应在领头阶可归约为单个标量表面磁化率 χ^s，并给出曲率修正的显式形式，推广了 Feibelman d-参数至任意弯曲界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非局部响应理论与界面效应之间存在鸿沟：Feibelman d-参数仅适用于平面界面，而实际界面常具有曲率；需要构建一个统一理论，将体非局部响应（bulk nonlocal response）与任意弯曲界面（arbitrary curved interface）的表面有效磁化率（effective surface susceptibilities）系统地连接起来。

Method: 从最一般的张量非局部本构关系（tensorial nonlocal constitutive relation）出发，结合空间矩展开（spatial moment expansion）和分布薄层极限（distributional thin-layer limit），推导出界面响应在领头阶归约为单个标量表面磁化率 χ^s；针对平面、球面、柱面和椭球面等界面，对高斯核（Gaussian）、Yukawa 核、张量 Lorentz 核等内核选择进行解析求解。

Result: 界面响应在领头阶可归约为单个标量表面磁化率 χ^s，该量对电场的切向和法向分量取相同形式；曲率修正与几何不变量平均曲率 H 和高斯曲率 K 成正比；建立了广义 Maxwell 边界条件（generalized Maxwell boundary conditions），并与经典 Fresnel 结果进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该理论为 Feibelman d-参数提供了到任意曲率界面的建设性推广（constructive generalization），为处理弯曲几何中非局部电磁响应提供了系统性框架。

Abstract: We present a systematic theory connecting the nonlocal response kernel of a homogeneous medium to its effective surface susceptibilities for an arbitrary curved interface. Starting from the most general tensorial nonlocal constitutive relation and combining a spatial moment expansion with a distributional thin-layer limit, we show that the full complexity of the interfacial response condenses, at leading order, into a single scalar: the surface susceptibility $χ^s$, equal for the tangential and normal components of the electric field. These quantities provide a constructive generalization of the Feibelman $d$-parameters to interfaces of arbitrary curvature, and the curvature corrections, proportional to the geometric invariants $H$ (mean curvature) and $K$ (Gaussian curvature), are derived explicitly. The formalism is illustrated on a comprehensive set of analytically tractable cases (planar, spherical, cylindrical, and ellipsoidal interfaces) for several kernel choices (Gaussian, Yukawa, tensorial Lorentz). Generalized Maxwell boundary conditions are established and compared with the classical Fresnel results.

### [75] [Average universal shower profile reconstruction using radio interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15762)
*J. Alvarez-Muñiz,W. R. Carvalho,R. Conceição,D. Dias*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用无线电干涉技术（radio interferometric techniques）基于蒙特卡罗模拟重建宇宙线广延大气簇射的平均纵向轮廓，并提取 Gaisser-Hillas 形状参数 (R, L)。结果表明，无线电导出的平均轮廓在区分初级质量成分（primary mass composition）和强子相互作用模型（hadronic interaction models）方面优于荧光等效轮廓，验证了无线电干涉技术可获取纵向发展高阶信息，提升对超高能宇宙线成分和相互作用研究的灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究聚焦于单个事件（event-by-event）的轮廓参数重建，但未能充分利用射电探测获取的广延大气簇射（extensive air showers）纵向发展信息。本研究旨在通过无线电干涉技术重建平均簇射轮廓（average USP），探索其对初级质量成分和强子相互作用模型区分能力的提升。

Method: 使用蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）生成射电数据，采用无线电干涉技术直接从射电数据中重建平均纵向轮廓，并提取 Gaisser-Hillas 形状参数 (R, L)。

Result: 无线电导出的平均轮廓对初级质量和强子相互作用模型的区分能力优于荧光等效纵向轮廓（fluorescence-equivalent longitudinal profiles）。

Conclusion: 无线电干涉技术能够获取纵向簇射发展中的高阶信息（higher-order information），利用平均通用簇射轮廓（Universal Shower Profile, USP）可显著提升对超高能宇宙线成分和强子相互作用研究的灵敏度。

Abstract: Radio detection of extensive air showers enables near-continuous observation and precise measurements of the shower geometry and the depth of shower maximum, $X_{\rm max}$. Beyond $X_{\rm max}$, the longitudinal shower development follows a Universal Shower Profile (USP), whose shape parameters contain information on primary mass composition and hadronic interaction models. While previous studies have focused on event-by-event reconstruction of profile parameters, in this work we investigate the reconstruction of the average USP using radio interferometric techniques.
  Using Monte Carlo simulations, we reconstruct the average longitudinal profile directly from radio data and extract the Gaisser-Hillas shape parameters $(R,L)$. We find that the radio-derived average profiles provide enhanced separation between primary masses and hadronic interaction models compared to that obtained from fluorescence-equivalent longitudinal profiles. These results demonstrate that radio interferometry can access higher-order information on the longitudinal shower development and that the use of the average USP significantly improves the sensitivity to composition and hadronic interaction studies at ultra-high energies.
