### [76] [Eccentric Stellar-mass Binary Black Holes: Population, Detectability, and Waveform Analysis in the LISA and LIGO Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15265)
*Zeyuan Xuan,Smadar Naoz,Kyle Kremer,Michael L. Katz,Bence Kocsis,Erez Michaely*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过构建动态形成并合双黑洞（eccentric BBHs）的模拟星表，预测了银河系及河外星系中大量高偏心率的恒星质量并合双黑洞源，分析了其对LISA和LVK等引力波探测器的可探测性、引力波波形收敛性以及全局拟合的影响，并公开了模拟星表及分析软件包LEAP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过动力学相互作用形成的偏心并合双黑洞（eccentric binary black holes）是引力波探测的重要潜在来源，但此前缺乏系统性的、包含多通道贡献的本地宇宙模拟星表来评估其可探测性及其对空间引力波天文台（如LISA）观测的影响。

Method: 构建了一个模拟星表，涵盖银河系银盘（飞越相互作用）、银核（偏心科兹艾-利道夫演化，eccentric Kozai-Lidov evolution）和球状星团（N体相互作用）三类动力学形成通道的恒星质量并合双黑洞，并扩展至宇宙学尺度以计算河外源的探测率与信号特征。

Result: 预测银河系内偏心并合双黑洞源计数在LISA 10年观测中随信噪比阈值递减（SNR>1时约36个，SNR>50时约1个）；河外星系源的合并率为 ~9 Gpc⁻³ yr⁻¹，SNR>1时约490个，但SNR>8时锐减至约1个。不同形成通道在LVK频段产生不同的偏心率分布。偏心信号在LISA全局拟合中可被独立探测其谐波，并可能通过系统偏置的啁啾质量（chirp masses）模仿圆并合双星。后牛顿波形（post-Newtonian waveforms）在mHz频段对质量≤10³ M⊙的偏心并合双黑洞可靠收敛。

Conclusion: 偏心并合双黑洞是未来空间引力波天文台普遍且极具前景的探测目标；模拟星表及配套分析软件包LEAP已公开供进一步研究使用。

Abstract: Eccentric binary black holes (BBHs) formed through dynamical interactions can significantly contribute to gravitational wave (GW) detections. In this work, we present a simulated catalog of dynamically-formed, stellar-mass BBHs in the local universe, incorporating contributions from the Galactic field (flyby interactions), Galactic nucleus (eccentric Kozai-Lidov evolution), and globular clusters (N-body interactions). Our results predict a wide, highly eccentric BBH population in the Milky Way (MW), with source counts of $\sim 36, 13, 4.7, 2.3, 1.0$ (for $\mathrm{SNR} > 1, 3, 8, 20, 50$, respectively) during a 10-yr LISA observation. Extending this model to cosmological populations, we show that different dynamical channels can produce distinct eccentricity distributions in the LVK band and can contribute hundreds of additional low-SNR mHz sources. Specifically, our model yields a merger rate of $Γ\sim 9 \mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ and $\sim 490$ extragalactic mHz BBHs with $\mathrm{SNR} > 1$. However, due to the lower mass and weaker GW signals of stellar-mass BBHs, this number declines sharply at higher detection thresholds (e.g., $\sim 1$ for $\mathrm{SNR} > 8$). We further highlight the impact of eccentric BBH signals on the LISA global fit, showing that their individual harmonics can be independently detected in the Milky Way, and may mimic circular binaries with systematically biased chirp masses. Lastly, we show that post-Newtonian waveforms converge reliably for eccentric BBHs with masses of $\lesssim 10^3 M_\odot$ in the mHz band. Overall, eccentric BBHs represent a prevalent and promising target for future space-based GW observatories. The simulated catalog and the LISA Eccentricity Astrophysics Package (LEAP) developed in this work are publicly available at https://github.com/zeyuanxuan/lisa-leap/.

### [77] [Disformal Kerr Imprints on BHL Accretion: Shock Morphology, PSD Signatures, and Observational QPO Counterparts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15686)
*Orhan Donmez,M. Yousaf,Imtiaz Khan,G. Mustafa*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了慢旋转畸变克尔黑洞（disformal Kerr black hole）背景下，时空参数对BHL吸积形态的影响。研究发现，即使微弱的畸变偏离克尔解，也会显著改变激波锥结构、增强激波后区域密度，并产生吸积率的相干振荡。该模型产生的准周期振荡（QPO）频率与银河系内外多个黑洞源（如GRS 1915+105、M82 X-1等）的观测结果吻合，为修正引力黑洞时空与可观测QPO现象学之间建立了联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时空参数（spacetime parameters）对BHL吸积形态的影响，并识别这些参数在流体动力学形态和吸积流时间行为上的可测量特征，从而建立修正引力黑洞时空与观测QPO现象之间的桥梁。

Method: 基于慢旋转畸变克尔黑洞几何，数值模拟BHL吸积过程，研究不同畸变参数下的激波结构、密度分布和吸积率时变行为，并通过逆质量标度（inverse-mass scaling）将数值频率与中等质量及超大质量黑洞的观测数据进行比较。

Result: 弱畸变偏离克尔解会改变激波锥结构、增强激波后区域密度并产生相干振荡；克尔模型产生42.99 Hz和68.13 Hz的相干峰值，与GRS 1915+105的高频QPO一致；弱偏离模型产生低频QPO且具有相干性；大偏离模型可解释更不规则、宽带且含多峰的观测结果。

Conclusion: 畸变克尔几何中的BHL吸积为连接修正引力黑洞时空与可观测QPO现象学提供了一个强有力的框架，并可依据模拟频率与观测频率之间的关系推断观测源的可能黑洞质量范围。

Abstract: We reveal the effect of the spacetime parameters on the accretion morphology formed through the BHL mechanism around a slowly rotating disformal Kerr black hole. Thus, we investigate the measurable signatures of these parameters on the hydrodynamical morphology and the timing behavior of the accreting flow. It is shown that even weak disformal deviations from the Kerr solution modify the shock-cone structure, enhance the density in the post-shock region, and produce coherent oscillations in the accretion rate. The Kerr model produces coherent peaks at 42.99 Hz and 68.13 Hz, and these frequencies are consistent with the high-frequency QPOs observed from the source GRS 1915+105. In the models where the deviations from the Kerr solution are weak, low-frequency QPOs are produced and found to be coherent. These frequencies also fall within the frequency range observed in Galactic black-hole binaries. On the other hand, the models with large deviations from Kerr can be used to explain observational results that are more irregular, broad-band, and contain multiple peaks. In addition, by using inverse-mass scaling in this work, the numerically calculated frequencies are also compared with observations of intermediate-mass and supermassive black holes. In particular, the disformal black-hole models are found to be consistent with the observational results obtained from the sources M82 X-1, NGC 5408 X-1, and RE J1034+396. This comparison also allows the possible black-hole mass range of observed sources to be inferred from the relation between simulated and observed frequencies. This makes BHL accretion in disformal Kerr geometry a powerful framework for connecting modified-gravity black-hole spacetimes with observable QPO phenomenology.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [78] [Large-$N$ scaling of Tan's contact for the harmonically trapped Tonks--Girardeau gas at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15994)
*Felipe Taha Sant'Ana*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文推导了简谐势阱中Tonks-Girardeau玻色子在有限温度下、大N极限的正则系综（canonical ensemble）中Tan接触（Tan's contact）的标度律，重点给出了次主导标度系数（subleading scaling coefficient）的显式表达式，并验证了其在全温度范围内的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强相互作用一维玻色子系统中，Tan接触是描述短程关联的核心物理量。已有工作主要基于巨正则系综（grand-canonical ensemble），而正则系综下的标度行为尚不明确，尤其次主导修正项与系综差异密切相关，需要系统推导。

Method: 从正则配分函数（canonical partition function）的围道积分表示出发，通过鞍点约化（saddle-point reduction）得到带有自洽标度化学势（self-consistent scaled chemical potential）的相空间积分，进而提取主导与次主导标度系数。次主导系数进一步表示为费米因子（Fermi factor）的普适相空间积分，并在Sommerfeld和virial极限下获得闭式形式。

Result: 主导标度系数复现了局域密度近似（local-density approximation, LDA）结果；次主导系数与正则–巨正则系综在固定平均粒子数下的差异等价。在高温Boltzmann区，次主导与主导系数之比坍缩为普适值，可归因于稀薄巨正则气体的泊松分布（Poissonian）粒子数统计。构建了Padé近似（Padé approximants），在从低温Sommerfeld到高温virial的全温度区间内均匀插值；次主导系数的近似形式在所述温度范围内一致精确，且渐近正确。

Conclusion: 本文建立了简谐势阱中Tonks-Girardeau玻色子正则系综Tan接触的完整标度律，次主导项揭示了系综涨落效应的本质，并基于正则围道积分数据在全温度范围验证了该标度律的正确性。

Abstract: We derive the canonical-ensemble scaling of Tan's contact for $N$ harmonically trapped Tonks--Girardeau bosons at finite temperature in the large-$N$ limit. The leading scaling coefficient reproduces the local-density-approximation result and is obtained from a contour-integral representation of the canonical partition function followed by a saddle-point reduction to a phase-space integral with a self-consistent scaled chemical potential. The subleading coefficient is the central new object of this work: it admits an explicit representation in terms of universal phase-space integrals of the Fermi factor, has closed-form Sommerfeld and virial limits, and is identified with the canonical-versus-grand-canonical ensemble difference at fixed mean particle number. In the high-temperature Boltzmann regime the ratio of subleading to leading coefficients collapses to a universal value, traceable to the Poissonian particle-number statistics of the dilute grand-canonical gas. We construct Padé approximants for both scaling functions that interpolate uniformly between the low-temperature Sommerfeld and high-temperature virial regimes; for the subleading coefficient we report a form that is uniformly accurate on our working range of temperatures and asymptotically correct beyond. The scaling law is verified against canonical contour-integration data across the full temperature range.

</details>


### [79] [Polariton BECs: Theory and Concepts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16256)
*Fabrice Laussy*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文综述了极化激元（polariton）凝聚体的形成、相干性与动力学理论，强调其作为弱相互作用、强干涉（WISI）粒子的独特性，并指出线性与非相互作用效应在极化激元物理中被低估，许多现象（包括玻色子关联与相干性建立）无需依赖强相互作用或真正的量子效应即可理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化激元凝聚体领域处于量子光学（quantum optics）、凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）以及驱动-耗散系统非线性动力学（nonlinear dynamics of driven, dissipative systems）的交汇点，但其与原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）之间的差异以及若干争议点尚未得到充分厘清。

Method: 本文采用综述（survey）方法，选取极化激元凝聚体在形成、相干性与动力学方面的关键理论概念进行系统梳理，并通过与原子凝聚体的对比分析来突出其独特性。

Result: 极化激元本质上是弱相互作用、强干涉（Weakly-Interacting, Strongly-Interfering, WISI）粒子；线性与非相互作用效应在极化激元物理中往往被低估，而玻色子关联（bosonic correlations）和相干性建立（coherence buildup）等核心现象在相当程度上可以不依赖于强相互作用或本真的量子效应（genuine quantum effects）来解释。

Conclusion: 极化激元凝聚体的核心现象学（phenomenology）在很大程度上可由线性与非相互作用机制主导，这一视角有助于厘清当前领域中的若干争议，并为理解此类驱动-耗散系统中的宏观相干行为提供更简洁的理论框架。

Abstract: Polaritons are a superposition of light and matter, that combine Strong Interferences (of light) with Weak Interactions (of excitons), making them WISI (Weakly-Interacting, Strongly-Interfering) particles. Their condensation is the main highlight of a field which occupies a unique position at the intersection of quantum optics, condensed matter physics and nonlinear dynamics of driven, dissipative systems. This chapter surveys selected theoretical concepts of polariton condensates' formation, coherence and dynamics, with an emphasis on their distinctions from their atomic counterparts and on points of ongoing controversy. We argue that linear and non-interacting effects are undervalued in polariton physics, and that a significant part of the phenomenology -- including bosonic correlations and coherence buildup -- can often be understood without invoking strong interactions or genuine quantum effects.

</details>

### [80] [A Finite-State Gibbs Construction from a Recognition Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15667)
*Megan Simons,Jonathan Washburn*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在有限结果空间上，提出以比率成本构造（ratio-cost construction）替代经典的香农熵最大化方法，通过规范化达朗贝尔二阶闭包——识别组合律（Recognition Composition Law, RCL）导出吉布斯权重（Gibbs weights）及热力学自由能-相对熵恒等式，并给出非渐近斯特林界（non-asymptotic Stirling bound）和实值成本的软壳约束型定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典统计力学中，正则吉布斯分布（canonical Gibbs distribution）通常通过在固定能量泛函均值下最大化香农熵（Shannon entropy）得到。本文旨在探索一种替代路径：基于比率成本构造（ratio-cost construction）而非外部能量泛函，在有限结果空间上恢复吉布斯权重，并考察该框架的数学后果与对比实例。

Method: 采用规范化的达朗贝尔（d'Alembert）二阶闭包——识别组合律（Recognition Composition Law, RCL），以参考比率处的单位对数曲率（unit log-curvature）校准，得到连续非平凡正分支 J(x)=½(x+x⁻¹)-1=cosh(log x)-1。基于诱导成本向量 X_ω=J(r_ω)，结合多项计数（multinomial counting）与凸对偶（convex duality）恢复有限状态吉布斯权重及恒等式 F_R(q)-F_R(p)=T_R D_KL(q‖p)。此外推导了非渐近斯特林界（non-asymptotic Stirling bound）和实值成本的软壳约束型定理（soft-shell constrained-type theorems）。

Result: 在有限结果空间和严格正权重的约束下，该框架成功从比率成本构造恢复了吉布斯权重，并建立了自由能差与相对熵（Kullback-Leibler divergence）的线性关系。三状态实例将吉布斯律与平方对数（squared-log）、亲和力作为能量（affinity-as-energy）及Tsallis替代方案在同一成本向量和均值成本约束下进行了对比，并给出了在固定RCL真实模型下的样本量功效计算。

Conclusion: 该比率成本框架在有限结果空间上为吉布斯分布提供了新的导出路径，但结果依赖于三个公理假设 (A1)—(A3)，且并未从更基本的原理推导组合律本身。框架适用范围严格限定于有限结果空间与正权重情形。

Abstract: On a finite outcome space, the canonical Gibbs distribution is usually obtained by maximizing Shannon entropy at fixed mean of an externally supplied energy functional. This paper studies the finite-state consequences of a ratio-cost construction instead: after adopting the normalized d'Alembert degree-two closure called the Recognition Composition Law (RCL), with unit log-curvature calibration at the reference ratio, the continuous nontrivial positive branch is $J(x)=\tfrac12(x+x^{-1})-1=\cosh(\log x)-1$. Given the induced cost vector $X_ω=J(r_ω)$, multinomial counting and convex duality recover the finite-state Gibbs weights and the identity $F_{\mathrm{R}}(q)-F_{\mathrm{R}}(p)=T_{\mathrm{R}}\,D_{\mathrm{KL}}(q\Vert p)$; the entropy-maximization steps are classical once the cost is fixed. New technical content includes a non-asymptotic Stirling bound and soft-shell constrained-type theorems for real-valued costs. A three-state example compares the Gibbs law to squared-log, affinity-as-energy, and Tsallis alternatives at the same cost vector and mean-cost constraint, with sample-size power calculations at fixed RCL ground truth. The framework is conditional on axioms (A1)--(A3) and restricted to finite outcome spaces with strictly positive weights; it does not derive the composition law from a more primitive principle.

</details>


### [81] [Short-time critical dynamics in the classical cubic dimer model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15730)
*Hu-Xiao Peng,Zheng Yan,Shuai Yin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过大尺度蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了三维立方晶格上经典二聚体模型（classical dimer model）在柱状有序相（columnar ordered phase）与无序库仑相（disordered Coulomb phase）之间连续相变附近的短时临界动力学（short-time critical dynamics），首次系统表征了该模型的非平衡短时临界性，并发现了一个异常的负临界初始滑移指数（critical initial slip exponent）θ = -1.052(5)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型的平衡临界性质已被广泛研究，但其非平衡临界动力学——特别是短时标度区——尚缺乏探索，而这一区域对理解超越朗道-金茨堡-威尔逊（Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson, LGW）范式的相变普适动力学特征具有重要意义。

Method: 采用大尺度蒙特卡洛模拟（large-scale Monte Carlo simulations），通过从有序和无序两种初始状态（初始关联长度为零）对系统进行淬火（quenching），分析了短时阶段序参量（order parameter）及其时间关联函数的标度行为，并依据短时动力学标度理论（scaling theory of short-time dynamics）提取临界参数。

Result: 精确测定了临界温度 T_c = 0.672(1) 和静态临界指数 β/ν = 0.581(5)，与先前平衡态研究高度吻合；提取了动态临界指数 z = 1.92(1)，并发现负的临界初始滑移指数 θ = -1.052(5)。

Conclusion: 负的 θ 值归因于临界点处涌现的 SO(5) 对称性（emergent SO(5) symmetry）和局域 U(1) 规范约束（Gauss law）的共同效应，后者强制了守恒扩散动力学（conserved diffusive dynamics）并增强了短时标度区的涨落。这一工作首次全面刻画了三维二聚体模型的非平衡短时临界性，为 LGW 框架之外的相变普适动力学特征提供了新见解。

Abstract: The classical dimer model on the cubic lattice hosts a columnar ordered phase and a disordered Coulomb phase, separated by a continuous phase transition that lies beyond the conventional Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson paradigm. While its equilibrium critical properties have been extensively studied, the nonequilibrium critical dynamics of this model--particularly in the short-time regime--remains largely unexplored. In this work, we investigate the short-time critical dynamics near the transition using large-scale Monte Carlo simulations. By quenching the system from both ordered and disordered initial states with vanishing initial correlation length, we analyze the scaling behaviors of the order parameter and its time correlation function in the short-time stage. From these scaling behaviors, we accurately determine the critical temperature $T_c = 0.672(1)$ and the static critical exponent $β/ν= 0.581(5)$ according to the scaling theory of the short-time dynamics. These results are in excellent agreement with previous equilibrium studies. Moreover, we extract the dynamic critical exponent $z = 1.92(1)$ and, notably, find a negative critical initial slip exponent $θ= -1.052(5)$. This unusual negative value contrasts sharply with the positive $θ$ typically observed in conventional critical dynamics. We attribute this anomalous behavior to the combined effects of the emergent SO(5) symmetry at criticality and the local U(1) gauge constraint (Gauss law), which enforces a conserved diffusive dynamics and enhances fluctuations in the short-time regime. Our results provide the first comprehensive characterization of nonequilibrium short-time criticality in the three-dimensional dimer model, shedding new light on the universal dynamical features of phase transitions beyond the Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson framework.

</details>


### [82] [Critical quench dynamics of Wegner's $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge model: a geometric perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15841)
*Ramgopal Agrawal,Leticia F. Cugliandolo,Marco Picco*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从几何视角研究了三维Wegner $\mathbb{Z}_2$规范模型在非平衡量子淬火中的临界动力学，发现渗透序参量的弛豫由动力学指数 $z_{\rm p} \simeq 2.6$ 支配，该指数与能量密度对应的指数 $z_{\rm c}$ 一致，且对初始淬火条件和几何对象选择具有鲁棒性；增长长度尺度 $\xi_{\rm p}(t) \sim t^{1/z_{\rm p}}$ 的动力学标度成立，尽管系统缺乏局域序参量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wegner $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范模型是纯格点规范理论（pure lattice gauge theory）的最早表述，其禁闭-退禁闭相变（confinement-deconfinement transition）具有拓扑本质。已有研究在平衡态下通过几何对象（如圈激发和Fortuin-Kasteleyn（FK）团簇）理解该模型的三维临界行为，但非平衡临界淬火动力学尚缺乏几何视角的系统研究。

Method: 采用时间依赖的有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis），研究从高温渗透相（percolation phase）和零温基态两种初始条件出发的淬火动力学，考察系统在临界点的非平衡弛豫行为。

Result: 渗透序参量的临界非平衡弛豫由动力学指数 $z_{\rm p} \simeq 2.6$ 支配，该值与能量密度对应的指数 $z_{\rm c}$ 一致；$z_{\rm p}$ 对初始淬火条件和几何对象（圈激发与FK团簇）的选择具有鲁棒性。从渗透相演化时，不同几何对象的动力学获得详细表征，且淬火动力学满足增长长度尺度 $\xi_{\rm p}(t) \sim t^{1/z_{\rm p}}$ 的动态标度（dynamic scaling），尽管系统不存在局域序参量。

Conclusion: 三维Wegner $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范模型的临界淬火动力学存在一个普适的动力学指数 $z_{\rm p} \simeq 2.6$，该指数独立于初始条件和几何对象，并且动态标度关系在缺乏局域序参量的情形下仍然成立，揭示了该拓扑相变的非平衡标度行为的深层几何本质。

Abstract: Wegner's $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge model is the earliest formulation of pure lattice gauge theory and predicts the topological nature of the confinement-deconfinement transition. In three dimensions ($D=3$), the equilibrium critical behavior of the model is understood in terms of geometrically defined objects, namely loop excitations and Fortuin-Kasteleyn (FK) clusters. This work investigates the critical quench dynamics of this model from a geometric perspective, following quenches from both a high-temperature percolation phase and the zero-temperature ground state. Using time-dependent finite-size scaling analysis, we find that the critical non-equilibrium relaxation of the percolation order parameter is governed by a dynamical exponent $z_{\rm p} \simeq 2.6$, consistent with that associated with the energy density, $z_{\rm c}$. Importantly, the value of $z_{\rm p}$ is robust with respect to the initial quench condition and the choice of geometrical objects. Furthermore, we provide a detailed characterization of the kinetics of different geometrical objects during the evolution from the percolation phase. Notably, we observe that the quench dynamics obeys dynamic scaling in terms of a growing lengthscale, $ξ_{\rm p}(t) \sim t^{1/z_{\rm p}}$, despite the absence of a local order parameter.

</details>


### [83] [Cycle affinity and winding localize eigenvalues of Markov generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15884)
*Artemy Kolchinsky,Naruo Ohga,Sosuke Ito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明了马尔可夫生成器的复特征值由非平衡循环局域化，揭示了热力学驱动、振荡与特征模衰减之间的基本权衡，并在单环与多环系统中推导了新的热力学界，同时证明了Uhl–Seifert椭圆猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马尔可夫生成器（Markov generator）的复特征值控制着弛豫、自相关和线性响应的振荡特性，但此前对这类特征值的局域化机制及其与热力学驱动的关系尚不明确。

Method: 证明每个复特征值被限制在由循环亲和力（cycle affinity）和某非平衡循环的特征向量“缠绕数（winding number）”共同决定的区域中。在单环（unicyclic）系统中，进一步证明缠绕数与有序特征值指标一致。

Result: 揭示了热力学驱动、振荡与特征模衰减之间的基本权衡；在单环系统中给出了弛豫最慢与最快模的新热力学界；在多环（multicyclic）系统中统一并推广了多项已有不等式，并证明了Uhl–Seifert椭圆猜想。

Conclusion: 马尔可夫生成器的非平衡循环对复特征值起到局域化作用，这一发现为理解非平衡系统的弛豫动力学提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: The complex eigenvalues of Markov generators govern oscillatory properties of relaxation, autocorrelation, and linear response. Here we show that these eigenvalues are localized by nonequilibrium cycles of the generator, thus revealing a fundamental tradeoff between thermodynamic driving, oscillation, and decay of eigenmodes. Specifically, we prove that each complex eigenvalue is confined to a region determined by the cycle affinity and the eigenvector ``winding number'' of some nonequilibrium cycle. In unicyclic systems, we also demonstrate that the winding number coincides with the ordered eigenvalue index, yielding new thermodynamic bounds on the slowest and fastest relaxation modes. In multicyclic systems, our approach unifies and extends several previous inequalities and proves the Uhl--Seifert ellipse conjecture.

</details>


### [84] [The Directed Abelian Sandpile Model on Cylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15914)
*Abdul Quadir,Nikita Kalinin,Ram Ramaswamy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维有向圆柱格点上阿贝尔沙堆模型（abelian sandpile model）的群结构及其与驱动动力学的周期性关系，通过将沙堆群（sandpile group）约化为横切问题（transverse problem）实现了循环分解的完整确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示有向沙堆模型中代数群结构与确定性/随机动力学之间内在的定量联系，弥补对定向格点上沙堆群循环分解认识的不足。

Method: 利用 Dhar 公式将沙堆群等同于约化有向拉普拉斯算子（reduced directed Laplacian）的余核（co-kernel）；通过将群结构精确约化为一个横切问题，实现对沙堆群循环分解（cyclic decomposition）的完整确定。

Result: 沙堆群结构可精确约化为横切问题，从而完全确定其循环分解；沙堆群的代数结构与驱动动力学的周期性之间存在直接联系。

Conclusion: 底层代数结构（algebraic structure）既支配确定性演化也支配随机演化，在有向沙堆模型中建立了群结构与动力学周期性的明确对应关系。

Abstract: We study the abelian sandpile model in two dimensions on a directed cylindrical lattice with periodic transverse boundary conditions in the transverse direction and dissipation at one boundary. Recurrent configurations form a finite abelian group, and repeated grain addition at a specific site generates deterministic dynamics on this group. Using Dhar's formulation, the sandpile group is identified with the co-kernel of the reduced directed Laplacian. We show that the group structure admits an exact reduction to a transverse problem, allowing complete determination of its cyclic decomposition. Our results establish a direct connection between the algebraic structure of the sandpile group and the periodicity of the driven dynamics, establishing the manner in which the underlying algebraic structure governs both deterministic and stochastic evolution in directed sandpile.

</details>


### [85] [Bak--Tang--Wiesenfeld model for various topologies and ranges of interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15930)
*P. Szczepaniak,K. Malarz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了Bak-Tang-Wiesenfeld模型在不同基底拓扑结构和邻域范围下的行为，通过计算机模拟发现，雪崩规模的概率分布幂律指数在不同条件下保持一致，约为1.208(39)，但需根据系统线性尺寸合理选择沉积颗粒数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视Bak-Tang-Wiesenfeld（BTW）模型在不同基底拓扑（substrate topology）和邻域范围（neighborhood range）下的行为，检验雪崩规模分布的幂律指数是否具有普适性（universality）。

Method: 采用计算机模拟（computer simulation）研究雪崩规模（avalanche size）的分布；使用Z分数（Z-score）统计方法验证指数的一致性；在多种基底拓扑和邻域条件下进行实验。

Result: 无论基底拓扑和邻域范围如何变化，雪崩规模概率分布所遵循的幂律（power law）指数保持不变，约为1.208(39)（括号内数字表示标准误差）。

Conclusion: BTW模型的雪崩规模幂律指数具有不依赖于基底拓扑和邻域范围的普适性，但该结论成立的前提是根据系统的线性尺寸（linear size）合理选择沉积颗粒数（number of deposited grains）。

Abstract: In this paper, the Bak--Tang--Wiesenfeld model for various substrate topologies and a variety of neighborhoods is reconsidered. With computer simulation, we study the distribution of avalanche sizes. Using the Z-score we confirm that independently of the substrate topology and the range of neighborhood, the exponent that governs the power law of the probability distribution of the size of avalanches is the same and approximately equal 1.208(39). However, this requires a smartly chosen number of deposited grains in relation to the linear size of the system.

### [86] [Staggering domino-like blast front motion in a one-dimensional cold gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16125)
*Taras Holovatch,Yuri Kozitsky,Krzysztof Pilorz,Yurij Holovatch*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究一维交替粒子系统在弹性碰撞下的动力学行为，发现当质量比 m/μ 取特定无穷序列 {ℳₖ} 时，系统从非随机等距初始位置出发，会呈现出与经典流体动力学预测截然不同的“交错多米诺骨牌”式运动，冲击前锋以恒定初始速度做弹道运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维交替粒子系统是连接气体介质中冲击波流体动力学与粒子牛顿动力学的桥梁。此前对 m/μ=2 且随机初始位置的研究已验证了欧拉流体动力学方程的预测，但非随机初始位置及其他质量比下的行为尚不明确。本文旨在探索不同质量比和等距初始位置下系统动力学的变化规律。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulation）与解析求解（analytical solution）相结合的方法。对于等距初始位置和不同质量比 m/μ，计算粒子在弹性碰撞（elastic collision）下的运动轨迹，并寻找精确解析解。

Result: (i) 对于 m/μ=2 且等距初始位置，结果与随机初始位置情形定性一致：冲击前锋位置按 t^δ (δ<1) 演化，部分粒子反弹进入负半轴。 (ii) 发现一个无穷序列 {ℳₖ}，当 m/μ=ℳₖ 时，系统行为发生剧变：任何时刻只有一组三重态 (m, μ, m) 在运动，其余粒子静止。 (iii) 此时冲击前锋以初始速度做弹道运动（ballistic motion），并给出了 ℳₖ 及粒子速度与位置的显式公式。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一维交替粒子系统中存在一类精确可解的质量比，其动力学行为完全偏离流体力学预期，呈现“交错多米诺骨牌”式的弹道运动模式。这为理解离散粒子系统中流体力学描述的适用边界提供了新的理论洞见。

Abstract: One-dimensional alternating particle systems are widely used to study interconnections between the hydrodynamics of blast waves in a gas-like medium and the Newtonian dynamics of its corpuscular constituents. We study the model in which point particles with masses $m,μ, m,μ,\dots, (m\geqμ)$ are distributed on the positive half-line $\mathbb{R}_{+}$. Their dynamics are initiated by giving a positive velocity to the leftmost particle; in its course, the particles undergo elastic collisions. For this model with $m/μ=2$, it has previously been established that the dynamics that start from random initial positions are consistent with predictions based on Euler's hydrodynamic equation. In particular, they have the following properties: (i) the position of the rightmost particle (shock front) evolves as $t^δ$ with $δ<1$; (ii) recoiled particles behind the front enter the negative half-axis; (iii) particles with locations $x\leq0$ move ballistically and eventually take over the total energy of the system. In this paper, we present numerical and analytical results for the dynamics of this model with nonrandom (typically equidistant) initial positions and various values of $m/μ$. For $m/μ=2$ and equidistant initial positions, our results qualitatively agree with those just mentioned. At the same time, we found an infinite family of numbers $\{\mathcal{M}_k\}$ such that, for $m/μ=\mathcal{M}_k$, the hydrodynamic behavior mentioned changes drastically to the following. At each moment, only a single triplet $m,μ, m$ is in motion, whereas all other particles are at rest. As a result, the shock front moves ballistically with an average velocity equal to the initial one. Such a `staggering domino-like' picture is obtained as an exact solution, which yields, in particular, explicit formulas for $\mathcal{M}_k$ and the particle velocities and positions.

</details>


### [87] [An agitated oscillator chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16209)
*Aaron Beyen,Christian Maes,Ion Santra*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 研究耦合了跑停粒子（run-and-tumble particles）浴的谐振子链的稳态动力学，发现高持久性下线性摩擦变负导致失稳，非线性效应抑制该反阻尼并产生类似瑞利振荡器（Rayleigh oscillator）的多体自持续波动行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究被动谐振子链在与活性物质（active matter）浴（即跑停粒子浴）耦合时，其稳态动力学如何被改变，特别是活性浴的持久性（persistence）对系统稳定性和涌现行为的影响。

Method: 假设时间尺度分离（time-scale separation），推导出诱导的朗之万链动力学（Langevin chain dynamics），并给出平流项（streaming term）、摩擦系数（friction coefficient）和噪声振幅（noise amplitude）的显式表达式。

Result: 在跑停粒子浴的高持久性下，线性摩擦变为负值（negative），引发失稳；非线性效应在长时间下抑制该反阻尼（anti-damping），类似于瑞利振荡器；活性浴的耦合使被动链转化为具有多体瑞利型动力学（many-body Rayleigh-like dynamics）的自持续波动介质。

Conclusion: 被动谐振子链通过与活性物质的耦合，可转变为一种自持续波动介质，表现为位移的脉动（pulsations）、空间振荡（spatial oscillations）以及沿链方向速度持久性（persistence in velocities）的涌现。

Abstract: We study how the stationary dynamics of an oscillator chain is modified when coupled to a bath of run-and-tumble particles. First, assuming time-scale separation, we derive the induced Langevin chain dynamics with explicit expressions for the streaming term, friction coefficient, and noise amplitude. At high persistence of the run-and-tumble particle bath, the linear friction turns negative, creating an instability. Second, we find that this anti-damping is arrested at long times due to nonlinear effects, reminiscent of a Rayleigh oscillator. We conclude that a passive harmonic chain can be transformed by its coupling to active matter into a self-sustained fluctuating medium with many-body Rayleigh-like dynamics. That transfer of activity results in pulsations of the displacements, spatial oscillations, and the emergence of persistence in velocities along the chain.

### [88] [Brownian motion: non-equilibrium states from equilibrium trajectories -- recovering hydrodynamic regimes from prepared displacement measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16247)
*Jason Boynewicz,Michael C. Thumann,Giuseppe Procopio,Massimiliano Giona*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用马尔可夫动力学（Markovian dynamics）的Chapman-Kolmogorov方程，将布朗粒子的平衡轨迹分解为不可数多个非平衡态的叠加，从而从单条布朗轨迹中提取微观尺度上流体-粒子相互作用的精细细节。通过仅考虑捕获条件下粒子位置的二阶矩，该方法隔离了热- hydrodynamic涨落力引起的加速度，并建立了短时位移统计与涨落热- hydrodynamic力关联性质之间的完全对应关系。结果不仅确认了Boynewicz等人（2026）发现的与流体惯性效应相关的$t^{5/2}$标度律，还指出在极短时间尺度上，考虑随机力相关性质后，该标度可能被$t^4$标度取代，后者与粒子速度实现的正则性有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从单个布朗粒子的平衡轨迹中解析微观尺度上流体-粒子相互作用的精细细节，尤其是热- hydrodynamic涨落力的贡献，并探究极短时间尺度下位移统计的新标度行为。

Method: 基于Chapman-Kolmogorov方程将布朗粒子的平衡轨迹视为不可数多个非平衡态的叠加；仅利用捕获条件下粒子位置的低阶（二阶）矩进行分析，分离出热- hydrodynamic涨落力引起的加速度，并通过涨落热- hydrodynamic力的关联性质完全确定短时位移统计。

Result: 确认了Boynewicz等人（2026）提出的与流体惯性效应相关的$t^{5/2}$标度律；同时发现，在极短时间尺度上，考虑随机力相关性后该标度可能被$t^4$标度所取代，后者与粒子速度实现的正则性相关。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种仅通过单条布朗轨迹和低阶矩分析即可揭示流体-粒子微观相互作用细节的途径，并揭示了极短时间尺度上位移统计的新的$t^4$标度行为，拓展了对涨落热- hydrodynamic力相关性质的理解。

Abstract: Owing to the Chapman-Kolmogorov equation for Markovian dynamics,any equilibrium trajectory of a Brownian particle in a solvent fluid can be viewed as the superposition of an uncountable number of non-equilibrium states. This property permits the unraveling of fine details of fluid-particle interactions at microscales defined by its non-equilibrium properties from the analysis of a single Brownian trajectory and to connect them to the hydrodynamics of the solvent fluid, simply considering the lower-order (second) moments of particle position in trapped conditions. In this way, the acceleration due to thermal-hydrodynamic fluctuational forces is isolated from the other factors and the short-time displacement statistics is completely determined by the correlation properties of the fluctuational thermal-hydrodynamic force. This approach not only confirms the $t^{5/2}$-law obtained by Boynewicz et al. (2026), related to fluid inertial effects, but indicates that this scaling may be superseded by a $t^4$-scaling at very short times once the correlated nature of the stochastic forcings is taken into account. The latter result is related to the regularity properties of particle velocity realizations.

</details>


### [89] [The fractal dimension of Brownian dynamics in liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16252)
*Michael C. Thumann,Jason Boynewicz,Giuseppe Procopio,Massimiliano Giona,Mark G. Raizen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论证明，流体惯性记忆效应改变了布朗运动速度涨落的经典分形维数，从马尔可夫假设下的 d_v = 3/2 变为非马尔可夫流体惯性噪声下的 d_v = 7/4，建立了有限密度流体介质中布朗运动的非平衡普适类（non-equilibrium universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典爱因斯坦-朗之万理论（Einstein-Langevin theory）假设热浴无记忆，为布朗运动速度涨落确立了普适分形维数 d_v = 3/2。本文旨在探究流体惯性记忆效应（fluid-inertial memory effects）是否会改变这一分形标度（fractal scaling）。

Method: 实验上对液体中布朗微球进行高分辨率测量，理论上结合非平衡短时动力学分析以及速度自关联函数（velocity autocorrelation function）的初始标度行为。

Result: 非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）流体动力学热噪声导致速度分形维数变为 d_v = 7/4，与经典马尔可夫假设下的 d_v = 3/2 存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 该结果确立了在具有有限非零密度的流体介质中，布朗运动属于一个不同的非平衡普适类，其分形标度由流体惯性记忆效应所主导。

Abstract: The classical Einstein-Langevin theory of Brownian motion assumes a memoryless thermal bath, establishing a universal fractal dimension of $d_v = 3/2$ for the velocity fluctuations of a particle. In this Letter, we demonstrate experimentally and theoretically that fluid-inertial memory effects fundamentally redefine the fractal scaling of these fluctuations. In analyzing highly resolved measurements of Brownian microspheres in liquids, we show that the non-Markovian hydrodynamic thermal noise establishes a distinct velocity fractal dimension of $d_v = 7/4$. Coupled with theoretical analysis of non-equilibrium short-time dynamics and the initial scaling of the velocity autocorrelation function, this result establishes the non-equilibrium universality class of Brownian motion in fluid media possessing a finite non-vanishing density.

</details>

### [90] [Dymnikova Black Holes in Unimodular Gravity: Maxwell Sources and Vacuum Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15255)
*G. Alencar,V. H. U. Borralho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在单模引力（unimodular gravity）框架下研究Dymnikova规则黑洞，通过允许能动张量协变守恒的受控破缺，使宇宙学常数成为径向函数Λ=Λ(r)，并证明该时空可在单模引力中由标准麦克斯韦电动力学一致生成，所得电场处处正则且渐近电荷为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单模引力框架下重新审视Dymnikova规则黑洞，探讨有效真空扇区（effective vacuum sector）在几何正则化中的作用，并澄清该时空能否由标准麦克斯韦电动力学而非非线性电动力学支持。

Method: 首先将Dymnikova时空重新解释为由非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）支持的带电构型，并导出对应的电、磁源；随后在单模引力中利用标准麦克斯韦电动力学重建同一几何，分析宇宙学常数Λ(r)的径向依赖性。

Result: 单模引力框架下Dymnikova规则黑洞可由标准麦克斯韦电动力学一致生成，所得电场处处正则（regular），对应局域化电荷分布且渐近电荷为零，表明该时空不表现为渐近带电物体。

Conclusion: 单模引力为构建规则黑洞几何提供了一种新途径，通过真空扇区的动态贡献避免了传统非线性电动力学的特殊假设，同时保持了时空的全局正则性。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the Dymnikova regular black hole within the framework of unimodular gravity, emphasizing the role of the effective vacuum sector in the regularization of the geometry. By allowing a controlled violation of the covariant conservation of the energy--momentum tensor, the cosmological contribution emerges dynamically as a radial-dependent function, $Λ=Λ(r)$. We first reinterpret the Dymnikova spacetime as a charged configuration supported by nonlinear electrodynamics and derive the corresponding electric and magnetic sources. Subsequently, we demonstrate that the same geometry can be consistently generated by standard Maxwell electrodynamics in unimodular gravity. In this construction, the resulting electric field is everywhere regular and corresponds to a localized charge distribution with vanishing asymptotic charge, indicating that the spacetime does not behave as an asymptotically charged object.

### [91] [Polarization Analysis of Ringdown Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15271)
*Nicole Khusid,Will Farr,Max Isi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了双黑洞并合后振铃阶段（ringdown phase）引力波信号的极化（polarization）结构，指出在赤道反射对称（equatorial reflection symmetry）条件下，准正规模（quasi-normal modes）的极化振幅与相位受到约束，可利用该约束模型测量圆极化（circular polarization）程度并推断源倾角（inclination angle），但在进动系统（precessing systems）中该模型会导致系统性偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 振铃阶段的引力波信号包含克尔残余黑洞（Kerr remnant）准正规模的信息，每个模式携带四个自由度。当模式具有赤道反射对称性时（如自旋与轨道角动量对齐或反平行的并合系统），对称性约束了其中两个自由度，使得极化振幅与相位之间的关系由观测倾角唯一确定。作者希望利用这种约束模型来测量振铃信号的圆极化程度和手性（handedness），并检验其在非进动和进动系统中的适用性。

Method: 采用受赤道反射对称性约束的极化模型，分别对非进动系统（如GW150914）和进动系统（如GW190521）的振铃信号进行拟合。通过仅使用两个LIGO探测器数据，测量圆极化程度并反推源倾角。同时，将约束模型与任意极化模型（arbitrary-polarization model）进行对比，评估在进动系统中使用错误极化模型导致的偏差。

Result: 对于非进动系统GW150914，即使仅有两个LIGO探测器，也能利用约束模型测量振铃信号的圆极化程度和手性，并据此推断源倾角。然而，对于进动系统GW190521，约束极化模型无法充分描述信号的极化结构，导致推断的模式频率和振幅出现偏差。利用约束模型拟合GW190521类注入信号时，预测精度低于任意极化模型，且存在显著的系统性偏差。

Conclusion: 在非进动系统中，赤道反射对称约束下的极化模型可用于测量圆极化并推断倾角，效果良好；但在进动系统中该模型不充分，会引入系统性偏差。随着探测器灵敏度提升，使用正确的极化模型对于避免振铃测量结果的偏差至关重要。

Abstract: Merging binary black holes exhibit a ringdown phase in which they primarily emit gravitational waves in the shape of damped sinusoids corresponding to quasi-normal modes of the Kerr remnant. In general, each mode carries four degrees of freedom encoding amplitude and phase information. When the modes are excited with equatorial reflection symmetry, as is the case for black hole mergers with spins (anti)aligned to the orbital angular momentum, the symmetry constrains two degrees of freedom. As a result, the relationship between polarization amplitudes and phases in each mode is fixed by the viewing (inclination) angle to the equatorial plane. We use such a constrained model to fit the ringdown signals of both non-precessing and precessing systems such as GW150914 and GW190521, respectively. We show that we can measure the degree of circular polarization and handedness of ringdown signals like those of GW150914, even if only the two LIGO detectors are available; such a polarization measurement can be translated into an inferred source inclination assuming the reflection symmetry above, again using the ringdown signal alone. On the other hand, the constrained polarization model is insufficient to capture the polarization structure of signals from precessing systems, leading to biases in the inferred mode frequencies and amplitudes. We explore the magnitude of this effect by fitting GW190521-like injections with the restricted model, finding weaker predictive accuracy relative to the arbitrary-polarization model and potentially significant systematic biases. As our detectors continue to improve, using the correct polarization model is increasingly important to avoid biased ringdown measurements.

</details>


### [92] [A metric solution for rotating black holes embedded in dark matter halos with central spikes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15330)
*Rui-Hong Yue,Yu-Qian Zhao,Wei-Liang Qian*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个解析度规（analytic metric），用于描述被一般暗物质晕（dark matter halo）包围的旋转黑洞。该度规是场方程的一个精确解，暗物质晕在黑洞附近具有中心密度尖峰（central density spike），其轮廓在接近视界处被截断，导致时空具有内在各向异性（intrinsically anisotropic）。该几何是渐近平坦的（asymptotically flat），并在适当极限下退化为多个已知情形，尤其是将Cardoso等人提出的球对称度规推广到了旋转黑洞情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究被暗物质晕包围的旋转黑洞的精确解析度规，以便更真实地描述黑洞在暗物质环境中的引力行为，弥补以往模型中忽略旋转效应或缺乏解析表达的不足。

Method: 基于场方程构造一个解析度规，暗物质晕采用包含中心密度尖峰的分布，并根据绝热不变量（adiabatic invariants）分析在视界附近截断能量密度与压强分布，从而保证度规的渐近平坦性及与已知球对称解的一致性。

Result: 所得度规是场方程的精确解，暗物质晕在黑洞附近产生密度尖峰并伴随度规不连续性（metric discontinuity），导致时空呈内在各向异性。该度规在适当极限下可退化为多个已知解，包括Cardoso等人的球对称度规。

Conclusion: 该工作为研究旋转黑洞与暗物质晕的相互作用提供了解析框架，通过对模型参数的物理解释及在具体引力系统中的应用，展示了该度规的实用性与泛化能力。

Abstract: We propose an analytic metric describing rotating black holes surrounded by generic dark matter halos. This metric is an exact solution of the field equations that incorporates a dark matter halo with a central density spike in the vicinity of the black hole. The dark matter profile is truncated at a radius close to the horizon, in accordance with analyses based on adiabatic invariants, so that the energy density as well as the radial and tangential pressures vanish identically beyond this point. The presence of the spike and the associated metric discontinuity implies that the spacetime is intrinsically anisotropic. The resulting geometry is asymptotically flat and reduces to several well-known cases under suitable limits. In particular, it generalizes the spherically symmetric metric proposed by Cardoso {\it et al.} to the case of rotating black holes. We discuss the physical interpretation of the model parameters and illustrate the metric by applying it to several specific gravitational systems.

</details>


### [93] [The cosmological inflation inside the cyclic model of the universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15374)
*Kanabar Jay,Maxim Khlopov,Jan Novák*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个包含两个标量场（scalar fields）的宇宙学图景，其中一个场控制宇宙的循环演化（cyclic evolution），另一个场在每个宇宙反弹（cosmological bounce）后驱动暴胀阶段（inflationary phase），从而表明暴胀可能是循环宇宙中反复出现的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用包含两个标量场的理论框架，其中一个场负责驱动宇宙的循环演化（膨胀与收缩交替），另一个场则负责在每个宇宙反弹之后驱动暴胀阶段。

Result: 两种标量场机制可以协同工作：循环场（cyclic field）确保宇宙经历多次膨胀与收缩的周期，而暴胀场（inflation field）则在每次反弹后产生一段加速膨胀阶段，从而生成原初扰动（primordial perturbations）。

Conclusion: 暴胀并非宇宙历史中一次性的事件，而可能是循环宇宙中反复出现的周期性特征，从而将暴胀宇宙学与循环宇宙学统一于同一个动力学框架中。

Abstract: Inflationary cosmology explains the homogeneity and large-scale structure of the universe through a brief epoch of accelerated expansion following the Big Bang. Cyclic cosmologies, in contrast, describe a universe undergoing successive phases of expansion and contraction and can generate primordial perturbations through alternative mechanisms while extending cosmic history beyond a singular beginning. Because these paradigms address different aspects of cosmic evolution, they are often treated separately. Here we explore the possibility that they may instead arise together. In a cosmological scenario involving two scalar fields, one field governs the cyclic evolution of the universe while the other drives an inflationary phase after each cosmological bounce, suggesting that inflation may be a recurring feature of a cyclic universe.

### [94] [Ringdown and echoes from compact objects: Debye series and Debye quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15429)
*Mohamed Ould El Hadj,Sam R. Dolan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了基于散射理论中德拜展开（Debye expansion）思想的新波形级数分解方法，用于分析无视界致密天体在弯曲时空（curved spacetimes）上受标量场扰动的时间域响应（time-domain response）。该方法将波形分解为直接外部传播、表面反射和内部多次透射，并通过德拜-准正规模（Debye-QNM）描述补充了标准QNM描述，能准确重构波形，尤其在中子星模型和超致密物体模型中揭示了回波（echo）结构的形成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准准正规模（quasinormal mode, QNM）描述在早期时间阶段收敛性差，且无法清晰区分波形中不同传播路径（如直接传播、表面反射和内部多次透射）的贡献。作者希望引入一种新的分解方法，以更直观地解释致密无视界天体（compact horizonless bodies）在标量场扰动下的时间域波形结构（time-domain waveform），并揭示回波（echo）类结构的起源。

Method: 借鉴散射理论中的德拜展开（Debye expansion）思想，将波形级数分解为直接外部传播、表面反射和内部多次透射项的叠加。通过分析每个德拜项的准正规模（QNM）内容，建立了德拜-QNM（Debye-QNM）描述。将该方法应用于两种“史瓦西星”（Schwarzschild star）致密天体时空——中子星类模型（\(R>3M\)）和超致密物体模型（\(R<3M\)）——对标量场传播进行数值验证。

Result: 德拜重构（Debye reconstruction）与精确波形高度吻合，且与标准QNM重构不同，它在早期时间也收敛，能准确描述包括即时响应（prompt response）在内的所有波形特征。在中子星情况下，低阶德拜项主要描述振铃（ringdown）和与亚阈值分支割线（sub-threshold branch cut）相关的非模态分量。在超致密情况下，德拜级数将波形组织为即时/振铃贡献，后接一系列分辨率较高的类回波波包（echo-like wavepackets）。

Conclusion: 德拜-QNM展开与标准QNM展开具有互补的谱解释：前者识别各传播通道中的独立模式（individual modes），后者描述前者的重求和（resummations）所得的整体共振（collective resonances）。这一区分阐明了回波结构如何通过内部重复传播（repeated interior propagation）产生，以及极点和分支割线贡献（pole and branch-cut contributions）如何进入时间域信号（time-domain signal）。

Abstract: We introduce a new series decomposition of the waveform constructed in the spirit of Debye expansions in scattering theory, and we use this to analyse the time-domain response of compact, horizonless bodies to scalar-field perturbations on curved spacetimes. The Debye decomposition separates out direct exterior propagation, surface reflection, and successive transmissions through the interior of a compact body, and it provides an intuitive interpretation of the waveform in terms of geodesic trajectories. By analysing the quasinormal-mode (QNM) content of individual Debye terms, we set out a Debye-QNM description that is complementary to the standard QNM description. With this framework, we examine a scalar field propagating on two illustrative `Schwarzschild star' compact-body spacetimes: a neutron-star-like model \(R>3M\) and an ultracompact object \(R<3M\). We show that the Debye reconstruction matches well with the exact waveform, and that (unlike the standard QNM reconstruction) it converges even at early times, giving an accurate description of all waveform features including the prompt response. In the neutron-star case, the low-order Debye terms mainly describe the ringdown and a non-modal component associated with the sub-threshold branch cut. In the ultracompact case, the Debye series organizes the waveform into a prompt/ringdown contribution followed by a succession of individually resolved echo-like wavepackets. The new Debye-QNM expansion and the standard QNM expansion have complementary spectral interpretations: the former identifies modes in individual propagation channels, whereas the latter describes collective resonances that are resummations of the former. This distinction clarifies how echo-like structures emerge from repeated interior propagation, and how pole and branch-cut contributions enter the time-domain signal.

</details>


### [95] [Charge-dependent scalarization of Einstein- Euler-Heisenberg black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15566)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 自发标量化（α⁺）出现在0<q<q_c=1.115且α>0时；新型标量化（α⁻）出现在q>q_c且α<0时。q=0.5时存在无穷多支标量化EEH黑洞解，但仅基态分支（n=0）径向稳定；q=2和q=20时分别仅有一个稳定的标量化分支。

Conclusion: EEH黑洞的标量化行为强烈依赖于磁荷q和耦合常数α的符号与大小，标量化黑洞的稳定性与分支结构呈现非平庸的荷依赖特征。

Abstract: Charge-dependent scalarization of the Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg (EEH) black hole is carried out in the EEH-scalar theory by introducing an exponential scalar coupling with $α$ coupling constant to the Maxwell and nonlinear electrodynamic terms. The bald black hole (EEHBH) is described by mass $M$ and arbitrary magnetic charge $q$ and has a single horizon when choosing the action parameter $μ=0.3$. The spontaneous scalarization ($α^+$) of this black hole is available for charge $0<q< q_c=1.115$ and positive $α$, whereas its new scalarization ($α^-$) occurs for $q> q_c$ and negative $α$. The former case of $q=0.5$ implies infinite branches of scalarized EEHBHs but its fundamental branch ($n=0$) is stable against radial perturbations, while the latter cases of $q=2,20$ show two stable single branches of scalarized EEHBHs.

### [96] [Regular black hole with sub-Planckian curvature and suppressed exponential mass inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15576)

Method: 采用静态球对称度规，构造具有闵可夫斯基核、非极值外视界（non-extremal outer horizon）以及表面重力为零的简并内视界的正则黑洞解，并在双零壳（double-null shell）和Ori模型中分析其动力学行为。

Abstract: We construct a static spherically symmetric regular black hole with a Minkowski core, and a degenerate inner horizon with vanishing surface gravity. The spacetime contains a non-extremal outer horizon and exhibits two notable features. Firstly, in the large-mass regime with $r_+=2M$, the Kretschmann scalar becomes nearly independent of the ADM mass and is mainly controlled by the inner horizon radius $r_-$, so that the curvature of spacetime remains sub-Planckian everywhere by choosing $r_-$ appropriately. Secondly, the near inner horizon amplification is softened from exponential to power-law behavior. In particular, within the double-null shell and Ori models, the internal Misner-Sharp mass remains finite at late times and approaches $r_-/2$.

### [97] [The role of Wigner rotation in estimating the specific angular momentum of a Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15600)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于由零测地线（null geodesics）定义的干涉臂构成的测地线干涉仪，分析单个光子在其中的传播；在慢旋转与弱场近似下，分别计算由引力时间延迟和偏振旋转引起的两种相位差（phase difference），进而得到输出端口的探测概率（detection probability）。

Result: 干涉仪输出端口的探测概率是两种相位差的函数，干涉可见度同时表征了引力时间延迟与偏振旋转这两种相对论效应；基于该探测概率可以获得比角动量的估计值并刻画其不确定性（uncertainty）。

Conclusion: 测地线干涉仪能够同时敏感于引力时间延迟和偏振旋转两种相对论效应，从而为克尔时空比角动量的估计提供了一种可行的干涉测量方案。

Abstract: We study the rotation of the polarization due to the gravitational field in the Kerr spacetime and the possibility of estimating the specific angular momentum that parameterizes this metric. Our approach is based on a geodesic interferometer, that is, a Mach-Zehnder interferometer whose arms are defined by null geodesics, and a single photon propagating within it. We show that the detection probability at the output ports of the interferometer is a function of two phase differences, one arising from the gravitational time delay and the other from the polarization rotation, both computed under the slow rotation and weak field approximations. Thereby, the interferometric visibility is a signature of two relativistic effects. Using the detection probability, we obtain an estimate for the specific angular momentum and characterize its uncertainty.

### [98] [Loop Quantum Kaluza-Klein Cosmology and Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15858)
*Shengzhi Li,Yongge Ma,Faqiang Yuan,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于五维圈量子卡鲁扎-克莱因宇宙学（loop quantum Kaluza-Klein cosmology），通过对称约化（symmetric reduction）推导了有效标量约束（effective scalar constraint），并纳入物质贡献分析了真空、标量场耦合、尘埃耦合三种有效情景。结果表明，大爆炸和潜在的大撕裂奇点（big rip singularities）由领头阶全息量子修正（leading-order quantum correction of holonomies）自然消除，宇宙在克服奇点后经历超暴胀相（super-inflationary phase），可在适当初始条件下实现55个e-fold。引入次领头阶量子涨落项作为常数时，所有有效情景在可见维中实现充分暴胀，并在大尺度上出现再坍缩行为（re-collapse behaviors），暗示宇宙暴胀可能源于紧致额外维（compact extra dimensions）与量子几何效应之间的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前特定情景下的五维圈量子卡鲁扎-克莱因宇宙学研究推广到更一般的情形，系统分析量子几何效应对宇宙早期演化的影响。

Method: 在正则形式（canonical）和路径积分（path-integral）两种框架下进行系统半经典分析（semi-classical analysis），将量子涨落作为次领头阶修正纳入，推导几何部分的有效标量约束；再通过纳入物质贡献构建三种有效情景。

Result: 有效标量约束正确恢复了量子系统的经典极限；三种有效情景中，领头阶全息量子修正自然消除了经典理论中的大爆炸和潜在的大撕裂奇点；可见宇宙在克服经典奇点后进入超暴胀相，可在适当初始条件下实现55个e-fold；引入次领头阶量子涨落常数项后，所有有效情景在可见维中实现充分暴胀，并在大尺度上出现再坍缩行为。

Conclusion: 宇宙暴脹可能源于紧缩额外维（compact extra dimensions）与量子几何效应之间的相互作用。

Abstract: We present the detailed analyses of five-dimensional loop quantum Kaluza-Klein cosmology based on the symmetric reduction of the connection formulation of the full theory. The previous results in a particular scenario are extended to more general cases. The effective scalar constraint for the geometric sector of the model is derived by the systematic semi-classical analysis in both the canonical and path-integral formulations, incorporating the quantum fluctuations as a subleading-order correction. The resulting effective scalar constraint not only exhibits the correct classical limit of the quantum system, but also serves as the basis for investigating the following three distinct effective scenarios through the incorporation of matter contributions: (i) vacuum, (ii) minimally coupling with a scalar field, and (iii) coupling with the dust. In all the three effective scenarios, the big bang and potential past big rip singularities in the classical model are naturally resolved by including the leading-order quantum correction of holonomies. Moreover, the visible universe undergoes a super-inflationary phase after overcoming the classical big bang singularity, during which the phenomenologically desired 55 e-folds can be achieved by appropriate initial conditions. In the case where the subleading-order quantum fluctuation term is included as a constant, the evolutions of the five-dimensional universe in all the three effective scenarios not only achieve sufficient inflation in the visible dimensions, but also exhibit re-collapse behaviors at certain large scales. Hence the cosmic inflation may originate from the interplay between compact extra dimensions and quantum geometric effects.

### [99] [Nonlinear stability of continuously self-similar naked singularities for the Einstein-scalar field equations II: linearized stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16095)

TL;DR: 本文针对球对称爱因斯坦-标量场方程中的连续自相似裸奇点（continuous self-similar naked singularity）解族，证明了在线性化扰动下的稳定性，揭示了正则性（regularity）在蓝移不稳定性机制（blue-shift instability mechanism）中的核心作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文通过对裸奇点时空进行线性分析（linear analysis），研究在具有与背景相同正则性（$C^{1,α}$）的扰动下系统的行为，并与已有的粗糙扰动不稳定性结果进行对比分析。

Abstract: This is the second part of a series of papers proving the nonlinear stability of a one-parameter family of continuous self-similar $C^{1,α}$ naked singularity solutions, with $0<α\ll1$, to the spherically symmetric Einstein-scalar field equations. These solutions were constructed by Christodoulou and are known to be unstable under sufficiently rough perturbations due to the blue-shift instability mechanism. In complete contrast to the previous instability results, we establish the linearized stability for those naked singularity spacetimes under perturbations of the same regularity as the background, revealing the central role of regularity in determining the strength of the blue-shift instability mechanism, and showing that it is not triggered at the regularity level of the background spacetime.
  The linear analysis carried out in this paper provides the foundation for the nonlinear stability result established in the companion paper [W. Zheng, Nonlinear stability of the continuous self-similar naked singularities for the Einstein-scalar field equations I: main results]. Together with that companion paper, this yields the nonlinear stability of these continuously self-similar naked singularities.

*Jose F. Rodriguez-Ruiz,Gabriel Gomez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文解析证明了具有四次自相互作用的非阿贝尔黑洞在线性扰动下的稳定性。利用吴-杨磁单极子（Wu-Yang magnetic monopole）构建的背景解是一个精确的黑洞解，携带由单一耦合参数χ控制的非阿贝尔磁荷Q²_NA，并包含两个分支。奇宇称扇区（odd sector）始终稳定；偶宇称扇区（even sector）中，分支I的有效势为正（稳定），分支II的有效势为负（不稳定）。分支II的不稳定性与其连接至扰动不稳定的爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯-赖斯纳-努德斯特伦解一致。分支I在确保解正则且无裸奇点的物理参数域χ内保持线性稳定。该结果证明了四维爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯理论中首个线性稳定的渐近平坦非阿贝尔毛状黑洞的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已知的非阿贝尔黑洞解（如爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯-赖斯纳-努德斯特伦解）在线性扰动下不稳定，而寻找稳定毛状黑洞是引力理论中的关键问题。本文旨在通过引入四次自相互作用项，构造并证明渐近平坦非阿贝尔毛状黑洞的线性稳定性。

Method: 采用吴-杨磁单极子拟设（Wu-Yang magnetic monopole ansatz）构造精确黑洞背景解，该解受单一耦合参数χ控制。将线性扰动分解为奇宇称扇区与偶宇称扇区，分别分析其有效势符号以判定稳定性。

Result: 奇宇称扇区始终稳定；偶宇称扇区中，分支I的有效势为正（稳定），分支II的有效势为负（不稳定）。分支II的不稳定性与其和已知不稳定爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯-赖斯纳-努德斯特伦解的关联一致。分支I在无裸奇点且解正则的整个物理参数域χ内保持线性稳定。

Conclusion: 首次证明了在四维爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯（Einstein-Yang-Mills）理论的最小耦合扩展中存在线性稳定的渐近平坦非阿贝尔毛状黑洞，即分支I。

Abstract: We analytically prove the linear stability of non-Abelian black holes with quartic self-interactions. The background, constructed from the Wu-Yang magnetic monopole ansatz, is an exact black-hole solution carrying a non-Abelian magnetic charge $Q_{\rm NA}^2$ controlled by a single coupling parameter $χ$, and admits two distinct branches. The odd sector is always stable, while in the even sector the effective potential is positive for branch I and negative for branch II, establishing stability and instability, respectively. The instability of branch II is consistent with its connection to the perturbatively unstable Einstein-Yang-Mills Reissner-Nordström solution. Branch I remains linearly stable throughout the physical domain of $χ$ where the solutions are regular and free of naked singularities. Our results prove the existence of the first linearly stable asymptotically flat non-Abelian hairy black holes in a minimally coupled extension of four-dimensional Einstein-Yang-Mills theory.

</details>


### [101] [Gaussian fluctuations in the tunneling probability of a closed universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16150)
*L. Salasnich*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path-integral）框架下，推导了封闭宇宙量子创生的隧穿概率（tunneling probability），在固定间隔微超空间（fixed-interval minisuperspace）表述中得到了包含指数压制项和精确高斯预因子（Gaussian prefactor）的解析表达式，从而提供了比以往研究更为精细的半经典成核率（nucleation rate）估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究对封闭宇宙隧穿概率的计算仅停留在半经典主导阶，缺乏对涨落贡献的精确解析处理。因此，本文的目标是在微超空间表述中纳入二次涨落（quadratic fluctuations）效应，以获得更自洽且透明的成核率估计。

Method: 采用欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path-integral）方法，在固定间隔微超空间（fixed-interval minisuperspace）表述中进行计算：哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）仅在经典瞬子（instanton）层面施加，而在超越半经典主导阶近似后不包含全拉普积分（full lapse integration）。通过计算瞬子周围的二次涨落，解析得到隧穿概率的高斯预因子。

Result: 得到了封闭宇宙隧穿概率的解析表达式，同时包含指数压制项（exponential suppression）和精确的高斯预因子（Gaussian prefactor）。该结果完善了先前关于半经典成核率（nucleation rate）的分析。

Conclusion: 本工作为封闭宇宙量子创生的半经典隧穿概率提供了透明且自洽的估计，通过纳入高斯涨落修正，提升了此前理论计算的精度。

Abstract: We consider the quantum creation of a closed universe within the Euclidean path-integral formalism. An analytical expression for the tunneling probability is derived, including both the exponential suppression and the exact Gaussian prefactor due to quadratic fluctuations around the instanton. The calculation is performed in a fixed-interval minisuperspace formulation, where the Hamiltonian constraint is imposed at the level of the classical instanton, while the full lapse integration is not included beyond the leading semiclassical approximation. The result provides a transparent and self-consistent semiclassical estimate of the nucleation rate, refining previous analyses with the inclusion of Gaussian fluctuations.

</details>


### [102] [Observational signatures of negative mass wormholes through their shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16177)
*Shin'ichi Nojiri,Sergei D. Odintsov,Diego Sáez-Chillón Gómez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了含负质量物体（NMO）的系统：正负质量双星系统存在束缚态，其引力波频率和振幅随时间下降；提出了Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的时间演化模型及消除鬼影的构型方法，并通过数值模拟给出了NMO的光学图像，在光子环亚结构上与史瓦西黑洞及Simpson-Visser虫洞存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对负质量物体（NMO）在引力系统（gravitational system）中的动力学行为及其可观测效应尚缺乏系统理解，尤其是其引力波特征和光学外观与已知致密天体（如黑洞、虫洞）的区别尚未被充分揭示。

Method: 采用理论分析与数值模拟相结合的方法：首先分析正负质量双星系统的束缚态条件及引力波演化特征；然后构建Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的时间演化模型，并提出消除该构型中出现的鬼影（ghost）的公式化方案；最后通过数值模拟计算NMO的光学图像，并与Schwarzschild黑洞及Simpson-Visser虫洞进行对比。

Result: 正负质量双星系统存在束缚态，但NMO对正质量物体施加的是排斥力（repulsive force）；该系统的引力波频率和振幅随时间递减；所提出的Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞模型能够消除鬼影；数值结果显示，NMO的光学外观与史瓦西黑洞及Simpson-Visser虫洞在光子环（photon ring）亚结构上存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 负质量物体（NMO）的引力行为与正质量系统截然不同，其独特的引力波衰减特征和光子环亚结构有望成为区分NMO与黑洞、虫洞等常规致密天体的可观测信号。

Abstract: We investigate systems containing objects with negative mass (NMOs). In a system consisting of one object with positive mass and one NMO, a bound state exists even though the force exerted by the NMO on the object with positive mass is repulsive. Unlike a standard system consisting of two objects with positive mass, the gravitational waves emitted from this system exhibit a decrease in frequency and amplitude over time. We propose a model of the time evolution of the Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole, along with a formulation that eliminates the ghost that appears when constructing the Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole, a candidate for an NMO. Furthermore, numerical simulations are performed to obtain the optical appearance of such NMOs. The observed luminosity is also compared with the Schwarzschild black hole and with the Simpson-Visser wormhole, leading to clear differences in the photon ring substructure around the central object.

</details>


### [103] [Detectability of avoided crossings in black hole ringdowns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16199)
*Hayato Imafuku,Naritaka Oshita,Hiroki Takeda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在贝叶斯框架下，利用三种波形模板研究黑洞准正则模（QNM）回避交叉（AC）的可探测性。结果表明，即便在乐观条件下，单独分辨两个近简并QNM频率仍很困难；但若AC相关模式主导环降（ringdown）信号且慢衰减模污染可忽略，则仍可通过互补波形描述识别AC的集体波形特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞光谱学中，准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）的回避交叉（avoided crossing, AC）会导致频率接近、振幅增强且相位近似相反的近简并模式，从而产生特征性干涉，但此类紧密间隔模式在观测上极难分辨。本文旨在评估在贝叶斯框架下，利用不同波形模型探测这类近简并QNM的可行性。

Method: 采用贝叶斯推断框架，使用三种波形模板（waveform models）对包含AC的近简并QNM信号进行分析。通过改变两个QNM复频率之间的分离程度以及模板波形的选择，系统考察复频率和振幅推断的依赖性。

Result: 即使在乐观条件下，单独分辨两个近简并QNM频率仍极其困难。然而，当AC相关模式主导观测到的环降（ringdown）信号，且来自更慢衰减模的污染（contamination）可忽略或被移除时，仍可通过互补的波形描述（complementary waveform descriptions）识别与AC相关的集体波形特征。

Conclusion: 对黑洞准正则模回避交叉的观测探测，重点应从单独分辨近简并频率转向识别AC的集体波形特征。在环降信号中AC模占主导且慢衰减模污染可控的条件下，互补波形描述提供了一条可行的探测路径。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes (QNMs) of black holes can exhibit avoided crossings (ACs), in which specific QNM frequencies approach each other while their amplitudes are enhanced and acquire nearly opposite phases, leading to characteristic interference. Resolving such closely spaced modes through black hole spectroscopy is observationally challenging. In this paper, we investigate the detectability of nearly degenerate QNMs in the presence of an AC within a Bayesian framework using three waveform models. We examine how the inference of the complex frequencies and amplitudes depends on the separation between the two QNM frequencies and on the choice of template waveform. We find that resolving the individual QNM frequencies is difficult even under optimistic conditions. On the other hand, collective waveform signatures associated with ACs may still be identified through complementary waveform descriptions, provided that the AC-related modes dominate the observed ringdown signal and contamination from more slowly damped modes is negligible or can be removed.

</details>


### [104] [Non-minimal fluid Lagrangian couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16220)
*Christian G. Boehmer,Erik Jensko,Eissa Al-Nasrallah*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对非最小耦合引力模型（涉及物质拉格朗日量与曲率的函数）进行了严谨的变分推导，给出了引力场方程和完整流体方程，并分析了非最小耦合对温度、化学势等热力学量的影响。同时指出 Schutz 与 Brown 的拉格朗日表述在该类模型中不等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，包含物质拉格朗日量（matter Lagrangian）与曲率（curvature）函数的非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）引力模型被广泛用于解释暗能量或暗物质，但其中物质为理想流体（perfect fluid）时的变分表述存在技术难点，亟需严格的推导和物理解释。

Method: 采用变分法（variational method）对非最小耦合引力模型进行严谨推导，得到引力场方程；并结合流体力学变分原理，推导出完整流体方程及热力学量（温度、化学势、数密度）的定义式。

Result: 得到了包含非最小耦合效应的引力场方程与流体方程组；定义了温度（temperature）、化学势（chemical potential）和数密度（number density）等热力学量，揭示了非最小耦合对这些量的影响；证明了 Schutz 与 Brown 的拉格朗日表述在该类模型中不等价。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合会改变流体的热力学量定义，且 Schutz 与 Brown 的变分表述在该类模型中不等价，需在后续应用中选择恰当的拉格朗日表述。

Abstract: Gravitational models with non-minimal couplings involving functions of the matter Lagrangian and curvature have become popular in recent decades. By coupling the matter Lagrangian directly to the gravitational Lagrangian, one hopes to construct theories that can explain dark energy or dark matter without introducing additional sources. When this matter Lagrangian describes a perfect fluid, some technicalities are involved in its variational formulation. We present a careful derivation of the gravitational field equations together with the complete set of fluid equations. The fluid's equations allow us to define thermodynamic quantities such as temperature, chemical potential and number density and thus allow us to understand the effects of the non-minimal couplings on these quantities. We demonstrate the non-equivalence of the Lagrangian formulations of Schutz and Brown for these types of models and provide a detailed interpretation of our results.

</details>


### [105] [Nonlinear stability of continuously self-similar naked singularities for the Einstein-scalar field equations I: main results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16235)
*Weihao Zheng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了球对称爱因斯坦-标量场方程中一类连续自相似裸奇点解（continuously self-similar naked singularity solutions）在局部Hölder拓扑下的非线性稳定性（nonlinear stability），表明泛函框架（functional framework）在弱宇宙监督猜想（Weak Cosmic Censorship conjecture）的表述中起决定性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Christodoulou曾构造了连续自相似裸奇点时空，并证明其在足够粗糙的扰动下会塌缩成黑洞，从而在粗糙泛函框架下验证了弱宇宙监督猜想。该论文旨在研究在相同正则性（regularity）的一般扰动下这些裸奇点时空是否具有非线性稳定性，以揭示泛函框架对弱宇宙监督猜想表述的关键影响。

Method: 论文基于同伴论文中建立的线性化稳定性（linearized stability）结果，研究在局部Hölder拓扑中、位于生成裸奇点解的数据的小开邻域内的初始扰动，证明其非线性稳定性。

Result: 首次获得了这些裸奇点时空在与背景相同正则性的一般扰动下的非线性稳定性，与Christodoulou在粗糙泛函框架下得到的不稳定性结果形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该结果强调了泛函框架（functional framework）在弱宇宙监督猜想（Weak Cosmic Censorship conjecture）表述中的决定性作用。

Abstract: This is the first part of a series of papers proving the nonlinear stability of a one-parameter family of continuously self-similar $C^{1,α}$ naked singularity solutions, with $0<α\ll1$, to the spherically symmetric Einstein-scalar field equations. The stability holds for initial perturbations lying in a small open neighborhood of the data generating these naked singularity solutions, measured in a localized Hölder topology.
  These continuously self-similar naked singularity spacetimes were previously constructed by Christodoulou [D. Christodoulou, Examples of naked singularity formation in the gravitational collapse of a scalar field, Ann. of Math. 140 (1994), 607--653], who also proved their instability to black hole formation under sufficiently rough perturbations [D. Christodoulou, The instability of naked singularities in the gravitational collapse of a scalar field, Ann. of Math. 149 (1999), 183--217], thereby verifying weak cosmic censorship within a rough functional framework.
  In complete contrast, in this paper, we obtain the first nonlinear stability of these naked singularity spacetimes under general perturbations of the same regularity as the background. We rely on the linearized stability result established in the companion paper [J. Singh and W. Zheng, Nonlinear stability of continuously self-similar naked singularities for the Einstein--scalar field equations II: linearized stability]. Our result underscores the decisive role of the functional framework in formulating the Weak Cosmic Censorship conjecture.

</details>


### [106] [Quantum Gravity Beyond the Bulk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15251)
*Jorge Gamboa,Natalia Tapia-Arellano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于外部观测者的量子引力红外与渐近形式化方法，通过渐近固有时规范将演化生成元约化为Regge–Teitelboim边界电荷，实现快慢自由度的Born–Oppenheimer分离，并在红外有效哈密顿量中引入几何（Berry）贡献，最终表明约化密度矩阵的熵由全局红外联络区主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一种适用于外部观测者（external observers）的量子引力（quantum gravity）红外与渐近形式化（infrared and asymptotic formulation），以解决量子引力中动力学生成元与边界条件的关系问题。

Method: 在渐近固有时规范（asymptotic proper-time gauge）下，将物理演化生成元简化为Regge–Teitelboim边界电荷（Regge–Teitelboim boundary charge）；在弱场区域引入Born–Oppenheimer分离（Born–Oppenheimer separation）以区分慢速渐近数据与快速体涨落；通过积分掉快涨落诱导出可容许构型空间上的Berry联络（Berry connection），其和乐（holonomy）表征红外修饰引力态。

Result: 得到了一个红外有效哈密顿量（infrared effective Hamiltonian），其中几何（Berry）贡献成为渐近构型空间上演化算符的一部分；对不可分辨自由度求迹后得到的约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）的熵主要由全局红外联络区（global infrared holonomy sectors）而非局部体动力学主导。

Conclusion: 量子引力的可观测量演化可由渐近构型空间上的红外有效哈密顿量描述，且约化密度矩阵的熵主要来源于全局红外拓扑结构，而非局域体涨落过程。

Abstract: We propose an infrared and asymptotic formulation of quantum gravity adapted to external observers. In an asymptotic proper-time gauge, the physical generator of evolution reduces to the Regge--Teitelboim boundary charge, so that quantum dynamics is governed by infrared gravitational configurations at spatial infinity. In the weak-field regime this leads naturally to a Born--Oppenheimer separation between slow asymptotic data and fast bulk fluctuations. Integrating out the latter induces a Berry connection on the space of admissible configurations, whose holonomy characterizes infrared-dressed gravitational states. Observable evolution is then governed by an infrared effective Hamiltonian obtained after integrating out fast bulk fluctuations, with the geometric (Berry) contribution entering as part of the resulting evolution operator on the space of asymptotic configurations. Tracing over unresolvable degrees of freedom induces a reduced density matrix whose entropy is dominated by global infrared holonomy sectors rather than local bulk dynamics.

</details>

### [107] [Disorder-driven symmetry suppression by van der Waals planar defects in a magnetic topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15332)
*Rikkie Joris,Heyi Xia,Ana Beatriz Pedro Fontes,Seul-Ki Bac,Sara Bey,Jiaqi Zhou,Zviadi Zarkua,Ahmed Samir Lotfy,Muhammed Saad,Philippe Ohresser,Margriet van Bael,Clement Merckling,Xinyu Liu,Francisco Molina-Lopez,Jean-Christophe Charlier,Jin Won Seo,Badih A. Assaf,Lino M. C. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道利用离子辐照（ion irradiation）技术，在不引入化学掺杂的情况下，通过引入本征缺陷（intrinsic defects）来调控范德华磁性拓扑绝缘体（van der Waals magnetic topological insulator）MnBi₂Te₄的磁性和拓扑性质。研究发现低通量下阳离子反位无序导致载流子从p型转变为n型，高通量下形成一种新型层无序相。尽管磁性各向异性显著降低，反常霍尔响应被抑制了一个数量级以上，远超磁化强度的变化，表明Berry曲率被直接调制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性拓扑绝缘体（magnetic topological insulators）可通过磁序调控电子拓扑性质，但可靠地调节其性质的途径仍然有限。该研究旨在探索一种无需化学掺杂即可有效调控此类材料磁性和拓扑性质的方法。

Method: 采用惰性离子束（inert ion beams）对MnBi₂Te₄进行辐照，通过碰撞级联（collision cascades）引入本征缺陷。结合磁强计（magnetometry）和X射线光谱（X-ray spectroscopy）表征磁性质，并测量反常霍尔响应以评估拓扑性质的变化。

Result: 低通量时，阳离子反位无序导致Bi在阳离子位点上近乎完全重新分布，同时保持长程晶体学有序，并伴随从p型到n型导电的转变。高通量时，阳离子-阴离子混合形成一种之前未报道的层无序相（layer-disordered phase），包含高密度的范德华特异性平面缺陷。Mn的高自旋态和反铁磁相互作用保持，但磁性各向异性显著减弱。反常霍尔效应被抑制超过一个数量级，远超磁化强度的变化幅度。

Conclusion: 离子辐照被确立为一种通过缺陷工程（defect engineering）调控拓扑性质的有效手段，并揭示了一种在范德华磁性材料中通过无序驱动控制对称性和电子结构的新方法。

Abstract: Magnetic topological insulators offer a platform to control electronic topology through magnetic order, yet reliable routes to tune their properties remain limited. Here, we show that ion irradiation allows to modify the magnetic and the topological properties of the van der Waals magnetic topological insulator MnBi$_2$Te$_4$. Using inert ion beams, intrinsic defects are introduced via collision cascades without chemical doping. We identify two distinct regimes. At low fluence, cation antisite disorder leads to a near-complete redistribution of Bi over cation sites while preserving long-range crystallographic order, accompanied by a transition from $p$-type to $n$-type transport. At high fluence, cation-anion intermixing drives the formation of a previously unreported layer-disordered phase characterized by a high density of van der Waals-specific planar defects, including swapped bilayers. Despite significant structural disorder, the system retains partial periodic order up to high displacement levels. Magnetometry and X-ray spectroscopy show that the Mn high-spin state and antiferromagnetic interactions persist, while magnetic anisotropy is strongly reduced. At the same time, the anomalous Hall response is suppressed by over an order of magnitude, far exceeding the change in magnetization, indicating a direct modification of Berry curvature. These results establish ion irradiation as a means to tune topology through defect engineering and reveal a disorder-driven approach to control symmetry and electronic structure in van der Waals magnetic materials.

</details>

Conclusion: 该框架通过将固态材料的宏观性质与微观相互作用机制联系起来，为理解和设计复杂材料提供了化学透明的（chemically transparent）基础。

Abstract: Non-bonded interactions govern structure, stability, and function across a wide range of solid-state materials, yet their chemical origins are often difficult to resolve from total energies alone. Here we generalize absolutely localized molecular orbital energy decomposition analysis to quantify and interpret non-bonded interactions within and between solids at the density functional theory level. Across molecular crystals, moiré heterobilayers, and layered perovskite heterostructures, this framework separates lattice-formation energies, interlayer binding energies, and band-structure changes into chemically intuitive contributions from frozen interactions, polarization, and charge transfer. The analysis reveals how dispersion controls polymorph stability in pharmaceutical crystals, how local stacking modulates interlayer coupling in MoS2/WSe2, and how alkali-cation substitution switches the quantum-well character of layered perovskite heterostructures. By connecting emergent solid-state properties to microscopic interaction mechanisms, this framework provides a chemically transparent basis for understanding and designing complex materials.

Abstract: Manipulating the lattice structure of ferroelectric quantum materials enables their use in low-power electronic devices, including field-effect transistors. The T$_\mathrm{d}$ crystal phase results from a Peierls distortion of the 1T parent structure and an interlayer shift. While experiments in WTe$_2$ have established ferroelectric switching and transient control of the predicted topological phase via ultrafast excitations, persistent electronic changes on the nanometer scale remain elusive. Here, we demonstrate that current pulses applied via scanning tunneling microscopy can both write and erase persistent nanometer-scale patterns on the surface of WTe$_2$. The out-of-plane displacements further modulate the Peierls-like distortion present in WTe$_2$, while the in-plane displacements are indicative of ferroelectric switching. Abstract: The spin and orbital angular momentum (SAM and OAM) are conceptually analogous, yet their roles in condensed matter systems have not been often treated on equal footing. While SAM has been extensively explored, OAM has long been regarded as quenched in crystalline environments and thus largely overlooked. Recent experimental and theoretical advances, however, have demonstrated that OAM can drive a variety of novel electronic phenomena, highlighting the importance of probing OAM textures in the electronic band structure. Here, we investigate the momentum-space OAM texture of (TaSe4)2I, a one-dimensional chiral crystal. These observations represent the experimental verification of a new type of OAM texture in crystalline materials. Conclusion: 硼掺入引起Sc环境对称化是(Al,Sc,B)N体系中刚度与压电响应解耦的结构根源，这为调控该类材料的力电耦合性能提供了新的设计原则。

Abstract: We present a first-principles analysis of the wurtzite pseudo-ternary (Al,Sc,B)N to elucidate the structural origin of a decoupling between stiffness $C_{33}$ and piezoelectric response $e_{33}$ upon boron incorporation, using DFT-relaxed 100-atom special quasirandom structures across a broad composition range. Pair distribution function analysis reveals interstitial threefold-coordinated boron atoms that have displaced from the tetrahedral cation site. Direct structural analysis establishes their preferential orientation along the $c$-axis and identifies a scandium-activated creation mechanism. The vertical coordination asymmetry of each cation is quantified through a site-specific axial asymmetry ratio (AAR), showing that boron incorporation progressively symmetrizes the Sc environment. Correlation with Born effective charges demonstrates that this symmetrization is the mechanism behind the piezoelectric enhancement.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三种原子间势模型：嵌入原子法（embedded atom method, EAM）、修正嵌入原子法（modified embedded atom method, MEAM）以及基于神经网络的机器学习模型——瞬态数据衍生势（ephemeral data-derived potential, EDDP）。利用嵌套采样（nested sampling）和副本交换嵌套采样（replica-exchange nested sampling）模拟，在60 GPa压力范围内计算热力学和结构性质，绘制熔化行为和固相稳定性图。

Conclusion: 训练数据的多样性和模型灵活性对准确描述高压相行为至关重要。嵌套采样是一种稳健的相稳定性探索框架，与现代机器学习原子间势结合（提供近从头算（ab initio）精度且计算成本可控），为实现真正预测性、穷举性的相探索开辟了道路。基于多样化非平衡构型训练的EDDP尤其适用于此任务，提供了稳健且可迁移的无偏相发现框架。

Abstract: We compare the predicted phase behaviour of lead (Pb) using three different interatomic potential models, including an embedded atom method (EAM), a modified embedded atom method (MEAM), and a neural network-based machine-learned model in the form of an ephemeral data-derived potential (EDDP). Using nested sampling and replica-exchange nested sampling simulations, we computed thermodynamic and structural properties at pressures up to 60 GPa, mapping both melting behaviour and solid-phase stability. Both the EAM and MEAM models predict the face-centred cubic (FCC) phase to remain stable up to approximately 60 GPa. In contrast, the EDDP model captures the experimentally-observed FCC-to-hexagonal close-packed (HCP) transition at around 15 GPa. These results highlight the importance of training data and model flexibility in accurately describing high-pressure phase behaviour, and demonstrate the effectiveness of nested sampling as a robust framework for exploring phase stability in materials. Particularly, the combination of nested sampling with modern machine-learned interatomic potentials - delivering near ab initio accuracy at tractable cost - opens the door to truly predictive and exhaustive exploration. EDDPs trained on diverse, out-of-equilibrium configurations appear particularly well suited to this task, offering a robust and transferable framework for unbiased phase discovery.

Abstract: In core/shell quantum dots (QDs), the interface between semiconductors of different chemical character largely determines their optoelectronic properties. In III-V/II-VI systems, this boundary involves pronounced chemical and electronic discontinuities that can generate trap states even under complete surface passivation. Using density functional theory on atomistic models of InAs/CdSe QDs, we systematically reconstruct atomic arrangements at the surface and interface to evaluate how local coordination and interfacial dipoles influence the electronic structure. Abrupt interfaces induce charge imbalance and band-gap collapse, whereas introducing an alloyed interlayer that mixes core and shell atoms and vacancies restores energetic alignment and yields delocalized band-edge states, consistent with experimental findings. ### [115] [Fuzzy band structure of quantum dots by Bloch Orbital Expansion, unconventional insights into geometry-electronic structure relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16055)
*Zeger Hens,Jordi Llusar,Ivan Infante*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出利用布洛赫轨道展开（Bloch orbital expansion, BOE）将量子点（quantum dot, QD）的实空间轨道变换到动量空间，从而获得模糊的量子点能带结构，以此揭示量子点几何结构与电子结构之间的关系，并首次将BOE应用于原子级核/壳量子点模型，实现能带对齐（band alignment）的识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于第一性原理（ab-initio）的方法（如密度泛函理论，density functional theory, DFT）已扩展至量子点（quantum dot, QD）几何结构，能够探索QD表面终止与电子结构的关系，但充分挖掘DFT数据需要新颖的量子点轨道分类方法，而实空间分析难以直接识别某些关键特征。

Method: 通过布洛赫轨道展开（Bloch orbital expansion, BOE）将实空间量子点轨道变换到动量空间，得到模糊量子点能带结构（fuzzy QD band structure），并与体相能带结构（bulk band structures）进行比较。

Result: 截断且未钝化（unpassivated）表面的III-V族和II-VI族量子点会产生源自体相表面轨道（bulk surface orbitals）的带隙中间轨道（mid-gap orbitals）；具有重构表面（reconstructed facets）的量子点则呈现由体相布洛赫轨道叠加形成的离域轨道（delocalized orbitals）。首次制备了原子级核/壳量子点模型，并通过BOE成功识别了实空间中无法实现的核/壳能带对齐（core/shell band alignment）。

Conclusion: BOE方法是连接纳米晶体研究中计算与实验洞察的重要工具，能够有效揭示量子点几何与电子结构间的关系，并提供实空间分析难以获得的能带对齐信息。

Abstract: The extension of ab-initio methods like density functional theory (DFT) to quantum dot (QD) geometries has enabled researchers to explore relationships between QD surface termination and electronic structure. However, fully utilizing the data from DFT requires novel classification methods for QD orbitals. Here, we identify relationships between QD geometry and electronic structure by transforming real-space QD orbitals into momentum-space using Bloch orbital expansion (BOE), yielding a fuzzy QD band structure. Comparing with bulk band structures, we show that truncated, unpassivated facets in III-V and II-VI QDs produce mid-gap orbitals derived from bulk surface orbitals; an identification challenging in real space. QDs with reconstructed facets, however, feature delocalized orbitals formed by superposition of bulk Bloch orbitals. Moreover, we prepare for the first time atomistic core/shell QD models and by the BOE expansion we can clearly identify the core/shell band alignment not possible in real space. These findings emphasize BOE as a vital tool for connecting computational and experimental insights in nanocrystal research.

</details>


### [116] [Charge Transfer from Perovskite Quantum Dots to Multifunctional Ligands with Tethered Molecular Species](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16073)

Method: 采用多功能配体设计：季铵盐（quaternary ammonium）结合基团实现强表面附着，长尾基团维持胶体稳定性，靠近量子点表面的功能基团实现电荷转移。通过二茂铁（ferrocene）功能化配体进行实验验证，并结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算分析分子结构变化。

Result: 二茂铁功能化配体修饰的pQDs实现了近单位效率（near-unity efficiency）的光激发空穴转移。DFT计算揭示了空穴转移后二茂铁分子结构的重组现象，该重组影响了电荷分离效率。

Conclusion: 该多功能配体策略可扩展至光激发电子和能量转移过程，为构建高效量子点-分子杂化材料（QD-molecular hybrids）用于光催化等应用提供了通用蓝图。

Abstract: Perovskite quantum dots (pQDs) are promising materials for optoelectronic and photocatalytic applications due to their unique optical properties. To enhance charge carrier extraction or injection donor/acceptor molecules can be tethered to the pQD. These molecules must strongly bind to the ionic surfaces of pQDs without compromising colloidal stability. These we achieve by using multifunctional ligands containing a quaternary ammonium binding group for strong pQDs surface attachment, a long tail group for colloidal stability, and a functional group near the pQD surface. Such pQDs with ferrocene-functionalized ligands show fast photoexcited hole transfer with near-unity efficiency. Density functional theory calculations reveal how ferrocene's molecular structure reorganizes following hole transfer, affecting its charge separation efficiency. This approach can also be extended to in photoexcited electron and energy transfer processes with pQDs. Therefore, this strategy offers a blueprint for creating efficient QD-molecular hybrids for applications like photocatalysis.

### [117] [Long-range magnetic ordering and structural phase transition in disordered high-entropy spinel chromites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16106)
*Sushanta Mandal,Koushik Chakraborty,Isha,Arvind Kumar Yogi,S. D. Kaushik,Sourav Marik,Tirthankar Chakraborty*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了两种Cr基高熵尖晶石氧化物（high-entropy spinel oxides）在温度变化下的结构与磁性演化。结果表明，尽管A位存在显著化学无序，两者仍表现出与低熵体系类似的尼尔温度以下反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic ordering）、螺旋自旋排列（spiral spin arrangement）以及从立方（cubic $Fd\overline{3}m$）到正交（orthorhombic $Fddd$）的结构相变（structural phase transition），提示高构型熵（high configurational entropy）可促进全局结构稳定，保留原始尖晶石体系的对称性破缺转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
