Method: 选取两种Cr基高熵尖晶石组分，即 $(Mn_{0.2}Co_{0.2}Ni_{0.2}Cu_{0.2}Zn_{0.2})Cr_2O_4$ 和 $(Mg_{0.2}Co_{0.2}Ni_{0.2}Cu_{0.2}Zn_{0.2})Cr_2O_4$，通过变温结构表征、磁性测量以及中子衍射（neutron diffraction）实验，系统分析了其晶体结构与磁有序随温度的变化规律。

Result: 两种体系在室温下均为具有 $Fd\overline{3}m$ 空间群的立方结构，并分别在尼尔温度 $T_N$ = 49 K 和 35 K 以下进入反铁磁有序态。中子衍射证实了长程磁有序，且磁结构为螺旋自旋排列。此外，两者分别在约 55 K 和 85 K 发生从立方 $Fd\overline{3}m$ 到正交 $Fddd$ 的 structural 相变。这些行为与低熵尖晶石体系中观察到的转变十分相似。

Conclusion: 尽管A位存在显著化学无序，两种高熵尖晶石体系仍保持了与低熵母体类似的长程磁有序和结构相变。该结果表明，高构型熵可能有助于全局结构稳定（global structural stabilization），从而在局部化学无序条件下仍能维持原始尖晶石体系的关键序与对称性破缺特征。

Abstract: High-entropy spinel oxides provide an excellent platform for investigating entropy-stabilized correlated systems with strong configurational disorder. In this work, we systematically study the temperature evolution of the structural and magnetic properties of Cr-based high-entropy spinels with compositions $(Mn_{0.2}Co_{0.2}Ni_{0.2}Cu_{0.2}Zn_{0.2})Cr_2O_4$ and $(Mg_{0.2}Co_{0.2}Ni_{0.2}Cu_{0.2}Zn_{0.2})Cr_2O_4$. Our results reveal that both systems crystallize in cubic structure with space group \textit{$Fd\overline{3}m$} at room temperature. Each system undergoes antiferromagnetic ordering below the Néel temperatures $ T_N$ = 49 K and 35 K, respectively. Neutron diffraction measurements confirm the emergence of long-range magnetic order with spiral spin arrangement. Both systems exhibit a structural phase transition from cubic \textit{$Fd\overline{3}m$} to orthorhombic \textit{Fddd} symmetry at approximately 55 K and 85 K, respectively. Notably, despite the significant chemical disorder at the A site, both systems undergo transitions analogous to those observed in low entropy spinel systems. This behavior suggests that high configurational entropy may promote global structural stabilization despite local chemical disorder, thereby preserving long-range orderings and the characteristic symmetry-breaking transitions of the pristine spinel systems.

### [118] [Thermal conductivity of seifertite and pyrite-type SiO$_2$: A comparative study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16123)
*Doyoon Park,Yihang Peng,Jie Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用基于SCAN和PBEsol泛函的机器学习势（MLP）驱动的分子动力学（MD）模拟，采用Green-Kubo方法首次计算了seifertite和pyrite型SiO₂的晶格热导率。研究发现Green-Kubo方法预测的热导率比声子准粒子方法高出最高119%，且温度依赖接近T⁻¹；从seifertite到pyrite型相变导致热导率降低19%，暗示在超级地球地幔中可能形成隔热层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于两个机器学习势（machine learning potentials, MLPs）（分别由SCAN和PBEsol交换关联泛函构建）驱动的分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，采用Green-Kubo方法计算晶格热导率。同时使用声子准粒子方法（phonon quasiparticle approach）进行对比验证。

Conclusion: Green-Kubo方法能完整捕捉高温下声子准粒子方法遗漏的扩散型声子（diffusion-like phonons）。seifertite到pyrite型相变导致的热导率显著下降表明，超级地球（super-Earth）地幔中可能形成热绝缘层。

Abstract: Thermal conductivity is a fundamental material property that plays a crucial role in understanding the dynamics and evolution of planetary interiors. Despite its importance, the thermal conductivity of seifertite and pyrite-type SiO$_2$ remains unknown. Here, we calculate the lattice thermal conductivities of seifertite and pyrite-type SiO$_2$ using the Green-Kubo method based on molecular dynamics (MD) simulations driven by two machine learning potentials (MLPs) constructed from the SCAN and PBEsol exchange-correlation functionals, with $\textit{ab initio}$-level accuracy. To demonstrate our methodology, we also compute thermal conductivities using the phonon quasiparticle approach for comparison. Overall, the Green-Kubo method predicts up to 119 % higher thermal conductivity with a temperature dependence close to $T^{-1}$, as it fully captures diffusion-like phonons at high temperatures that are missed by the phonon quasiparticle approach. The 19 % reduction in thermal conductivity across the phase transition from seifertite to the pyrite-type phase suggests the potential formation of a thermally insulating layer in the mantle of super-Earths.

Abstract: Transparent conducting oxides (TCOs) are essential for the optoelectronics industry, but there is a critical gap in cost-effective methods to rapidly deposit low sheet resistance, high transmittance films without damaging delicate materials, including emerging soft semiconductors like metal-halide perovskites. In this work, atmospheric pressure chemical vapor deposition (AP-CVD) is used to synthesise H:In2O3 films with 7.20+/-0.01 Ohm/sq sheet resistance (0.50+/-0.06 mOhm.cm resistivity) and transmittance up to 89% in the near-infrared (NIR), surpassing commercial sputter-deposited indium tin oxide. The growth rate is 40x higher than atomic layer deposition (ALD), and the AP-CVD films are fully processed under atmospheric conditions at only 140 C. Comparison of secondary ion mass spectrometry and time-of-flight elastic recoil detection analysis with changes in carrier concentration indicate that H dopants are introduced from the water oxidant. There is an increase in mobility form 40+/-10 cm2/Vs to 160+/-30 cm2/Vs when changing from O2 to H2O as the oxidant, which is attributed to H dopants passivating oxygen vacancies that act as carrier scattering centers. This work establishes AP-CVD as a promising method for manufacturing high figure-of-merit TCOs in a rapid, scalable and cost-effective manner, using mild growth conditions compatible with thermally-sensitive materials.

### [120] [Bridging Atomistic Simulation and Experimental Processing Timescales with Goal-Directed Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16214)
*Wonseok Jeong,Francesca Tavazza,Brian DeCost*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于E(3)-等变深度强化学习（E(3)-equivariant deep reinforcement learning）的原子模拟框架，无需手工定义的反应坐标即可实现目标导向的路径发现。该框架通过势垒感知奖励（barrier-aware rewards）保持动力学合理性，并在非理想化环境中直接模拟材料形成过程。以硅干法氧化（silicon dry oxidation）为基准，框架成功发现O₂分子在无序Si/a-SiO₂环境中的扩散和解离路径，有效降低了有效激活势垒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 即使拥有精确的势能面（potential energy surface）和明确的目标材料，现有原子动力学框架仍无法模拟材料在实际合成与加工条件下的形成过程。现有加速方法需要事先知道反应坐标（reaction coordinates）、集体变量（collective variables）或路径猜想等先验机制知识，这在真实实验中往往不可得。

Method: 提出一个E(3)-等变深度强化学习框架，将O₂分子视为智能体（agent），在Si/a-SiO₂环境中执行连续刚体平移与旋转。采用幕级目标（episode-level objective），对验证通过且有效激活势垒低的O₂解离事件给予奖励，通过势垒感知奖励保持动力学合理性。

Result: 训练后的策略能够发现动力学有利的O₂扩散与解离路径，在无序Si/a-SiO₂环境中逐步提高成功率，同时降低有效激活势垒。

Conclusion: 该框架为原子模拟提供了一种互补的运行模式，可直接处理真实非理想化环境。该方法可推广至其他加工与合成问题。

Abstract: Atomic-scale modeling has advanced rapidly through integration of machine learning, yet a key bottleneck remains. Even with an accurate potential energy surface and a clear target material, we still lack a practical atomistic dynamics framework that can simulate how materials form under realistic synthesis and processing conditions. Many processing transformations are governed by rare events in non-idealized evolving environments, while direct molecular dynamics is limited by femtosecond timesteps and short accessible trajectories. Existing acceleration methods often require prior mechanistic knowledge, including reaction coordinates, collective variables, event tables, or pathway guesses, which is rarely available in real experiments. Here we present an E(3)-equivariant deep reinforcement learning framework that enables goal-directed pathway discovery without hand-crafted reaction coordinates. The framework introduces a complementary operating mode for atomistic simulation in which realistic, non-idealized environments can be addressed directly while retaining kinetic plausibility through barrier-aware rewards. As a challenging benchmark, we target silicon dry oxidation, where rare-event pathways in amorphous SiO2 are effectively inaccessible to conventional atomistic methods. We treat an O2 molecule as an agent that performs continuous rigid-body translations and rotations in a Si/a-SiO2 environment. The agent is trained with an episode-level objective that rewards verified O2 dissociation while preferring low effective activation barriers. We demonstrate that the learned policy discovers kinetically favorable O2 diffusion and dissociation pathways in a disordered Si/a-SiO2 environment, progressively improving success rate while reducing effective activation barriers over training. We also discuss how the approach can be generalized to other processing and synthesis problems.

### [121] [Universal Magnetic Structure Prediction from Atomic Coordinates with Near-Experimental Accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16230)
*Abhijatmedhi Chotrattanapituk,Ryotaro Okabe,Eunbi Rha,Mariya Al-Hinai,Eugene Jiang,Daniel Pajerowski,Yongqiang Cheng,Joshua J. Turner,Mingda Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了磁结构网络（MSN, magnetic structure network），一种E(3)等变图神经网络（E(3) equivariant graph neural network），直接从原子晶体结构预测共线和非共线磁结构。同时引入单元调制结构表示（PMSR, primitive modulated structure representation），在不依赖对称性假设的前提下，以统一方式编码公度（commensurate）和非公度磁结构。

Result: 模型在所有调制分量（modulation components）上均取得了优异的预测性能，能够以高保真度（high fidelity）重建实验测定的磁结构。

Conclusion: 该方法为快速磁结构预测提供了一个可扩展的框架，开辟了一条数据驱动的磁性材料发现（data-driven discovery of magnetic materials）新路径。

Abstract: Magnetic order is a fundamental property of materials, governing collective behavior and enabling a broad range of functionalities. Yet magnetic structure remains difficult to determine: experiments are costly and specialized, while first-principles methods often struggle with the noncollinear and incommensurate orders found in real materials. Here we introduce magnetic structure network (MSN), an E(3) equivariant graph neural network that predicts both collinear and non-collinear magnetic structures directly from atomic crystal structures, trained directly on experimentally determined structures from MAGNDATA. By proposing the primitive modulated structure representation (PMSR), we are able to encode commensurate and incommensurate structures in a unified way without symmetry assumptions. The model achieves strong performance across all modulation components and reconstructs experimental magnetic structures with high fidelity. Our approach provides a scalable framework for rapid magnetic structure prediction and opens a route to data-driven discovery of magnetic materials.

*Mohamed El Gazzah,Daniel Kaplan,Zachary Morgan,Abhijeet Nayak Resham Regmi,Sk Jamaluddin,Huibo Cao,Igor I. Mazin,Nirmal J. Ghimire*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过中子衍射实验推翻了此前密度泛函理论(DFT)关于EuAgAs是体态交变磁狄拉克半金属的预言，发现其基态为面内↑↑↓↓反铁磁(AFM)结构；DFT计算显示铁磁(FM)与交变磁(AM)构型与基态能量近简并，且引入双二次耦合可稳定观测到的反铁磁相；约14 GPa静水压下可驱动至交变磁相，使EuAgAs成为实现拓扑交变磁的可调控平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体(Altermagnets)作为连接铁磁体(Ferromagnets)与反铁磁体(Antiferromagnets)的新兴磁性类别，兼具零净磁化与动量依赖自旋劈裂特性，但兼具交变磁性与非平庸带拓扑的实验可获取材料极为稀缺，亟需寻找可控的平台材料。

Method: 采用中子衍射实验测定EuAgAs的磁性基态结构，结合基于密度泛函理论(Density Functional Theory, DFT)的第一性原理计算系统比较铁磁(FM)、交变磁(AM)及多种反铁磁(AFM)构型的能量，并引入海森堡模型(Heisenberg model)与非海森堡双二次耦合(Biquadratic coupling)分析磁序稳定性。

Result: 中子衍射表明EuAgAs基态为波矢q=(0,0,1/2)的面内↑↑↓↓反铁磁结构；DFT显示FM与AM构型能量仅分别高出基态0.11和0.40 meV/f.u.；简单海森堡模型预言自旋螺旋基态，而加入双二次耦合后观测到的公度反铁磁相得以稳定；约14 GPa静水压下可驱动至交变磁相。

Conclusion: EuAgAs的磁性基态呈现多种磁序的近简并性，使其磁态高度可调，在约14 GPa静水压下可实现向交变磁相的转变，为研究拓扑交变磁(Topological altermagnetism)提供了可控的材料平台。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) have recently emerged as a distinct magnetic class bridging central features of ferromagnets (FMs) and antiferromagnets (AFMs), offering new opportunities for spin-based electronics. While they possess zero net magnetization like collinear AFMs, they simultaneously exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting long thought exclusive to FMs. Despite intense theoretical interest, experimentally accessible materials hosting both altermagnetism and nontrivial band topology remain scarce. EuAgAs, crystallizing in space group $P6_3/mmc$, was previously identified via density functional theory (DFT) as a bulk altermagnetic Dirac semimetal. Contrary to these predictions, our neutron diffraction experiments reveal that the bulk ground state adopts a $\mathbf{q} = (0,0,\tfrac{1}{2})$ AFM structure with an in-plane $\uparrow\uparrow\downarrow\downarrow$ spin sequence. Systematic DFT calculations, however, uncover a remarkable near-degeneracy among competing magnetic orders: the FM and AM configurations lie only $0.11$ and $0.40~\text{meV/f.u.}$ above the AFM ground state, respectively. We further show that while a simple Heisenberg model favors a spin-spiral ground state, the inclusion of non-Heisenberg biquadratic coupling stabilizes the observed commensurate AFM phase. This near-degeneracy renders the magnetic state highly tunable, with DFT predicting a transition to the altermagnetic phase under hydrostatic pressure at approximately $14 \text{ GPa}$, establishing EuAgAs as a controllable platform for accessing topological altermagnetism.

</details>


<div id='nlin.CD'></div>

# nlin.CD [[Back]](#toc)

### [123] [Symmetry breaking and high-dimensional chaos in sparse random networks of exact firing rate models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15872)
*Pau Clusella*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过稀疏随机网络耦合的全兴奋性或全抑制性下一代神经质量模型（NG-NMMs）的动力学行为。利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）界定失稳参数区域，发现无向网络中仅抑制性系统产生异质驻留模式（winner-takes-all机制），有向网络中两类系统均出现高频奇异节律态，对应高维混沌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确发放率模型（exact firing rate models），即下一代神经质量模型（NG-NMMs），为神经群体动力学提供了严格描述。尽管单群体仅呈现不动点活动，多群体模型可能展现多种行为。本文旨在研究通过稀疏随机网络耦合的NG-NMMs的动力学特性，特别是异质性时空模式的产生条件。

Method: 采用行归一化网络拓扑的稀疏随机网络耦合全兴奋性或全抑制性NG-NMMs。通过系统均匀态（代表异步神经活动）的线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis），推导出色散关系（dispersion relation），将时空动力学涌现与连接矩阵谱联系起来。利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）的边界条件界定失稳发生的参数区域。

Result: 在无向网络中，仅抑制性系统产生异质驻留模式（heterogeneous stationary patterns），对应赢家通吃（winner-takes-all）机制。在有向网络中，兴奋性和抑制性系统均出现高频奇异节律态（exotic rhythmic states）。数值模拟表明，这些活跃振荡态对应具有广延性质的高维混沌（high-dimensional chaos with extensive properties）。

Conclusion: 网络拓扑结构（无向/有向）和突触类型（兴奋/抑制）共同决定了NG-NMMs的涌现动力学行为。有向网络可诱导两类系统产生高频混沌节律，而无向网络中仅抑制性耦合支持非平凡空间模式。

Abstract: Exact firing rate models, also known as next-generation neural mass models (NG-NMMs), provide a rigorous description of the dynamics of neural populations. While in its simplest form a single population only displays fixed-point activity, multi-population models may display a range of different behaviors. In this work, we study the dynamics of all-excitatory or all-inhibitory NG-NMMs coupled through sparse random networks with row-normalized network topology. Linear stability analysis of the homogeneous states of the system, representing asynchronous neural activity, provides a dispersion relation linking the emergence of spatiotemporal dynamics to the spectra of the connectivity matrix. Using bounds from random matrix theory, we identify the parameter regions where instabilities occur. In undirected networks, only inhibitory systems produce heterogeneous stationary patterns, corresponding to a winner-takes-all mechanism. In directed networks, exotic rhythmic states with high frequencies emerge in both, excitatory and inhibitory systems. Numerical simulations reveal that these hectic oscillatory states correspond to high-dimensional chaos with extensive properties.

</details>
